# 2026-06-23 · quant-ph 论文速递


## 不含字符串或自相似分数逻辑运算符的三维随机局部稳定码

**Original Title:** Random Local Stabilizer Codes in Three Dimensions without String or Self-Similar Fractal Logical Operators

**Authors:** Han Yan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19873v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.19873v2

**Submitted:** 2026-06-18


### 摘要

量子错误纠正码（QEC）是量子计算的重要组成部分，与物质的量子相有着深刻的联系。被动自纠正QEC的一个关键障碍是字符串逻辑运算符的存在，它可以通过恒能屏障过程产生逻辑错误。Haah ' s Codes（fracton Codes）表明，三维稳定器代码可以禁止此类字符串逻辑运算符，但它们的稳定不变结构支持具有对数能垒的自相似分数逻辑运算符。我们引入了qutri随机立方体码，这是一个本地qutri Calderbank-Shor-Steane稳定器家族，具有与Haah ' s Code 1类似的立方体检查结构，但由空间变化的稳定器构建。我们证明了这些模型保留了无字符串性质，并在数字上观察到它们具有与平移不变分子码不同的性质：对于奇数$L$来说，最小的基状态简并指数为$k=2$，对于偶数$L$来说，$k=4$;不可收缩的平面逻辑运算符跨越整个逻辑空间;和电荷推送诊断表明自相似的分维运算符不存在。这些结果表明，受约束的随机性可以从根本上改变稳定器代码的性质并提高其自纠正性能。他们进一步指出了超越经典拓扑和分子阶的更广泛的量子错误纠正码和量子相家族。


### Abstract

Quantum error-correcting codes (QECs) are essential components of quantum computation and have deep connections to quantum phases of matter. A key obstruction to passive self-correcting QECs is the presence of string logical operators, which can generate logical errors through constant-energy-barrier processes. Haah's Codes (fracton codes) showed that three-dimensional stabilizer codes can forbid such string logical operators, but their translation-invariant structure supports self-similar fractal logical operators with a logarithmic energy barrier. We introduce the qutrit random cubic codes, a family of local qutrit Calderbank-Shor-Steane stabilizer Hamiltonians with similar cube-check structure as Haah's Code 1 but built from spatially varying stabilizers. We prove that these models retain the no-string property and numerically observe that they have properties distinct from translation-invariant fracton codes: the smallest ground-state degeneracy exponent is $k=2$ for odd $L$ and $k=4$ for even $L$; noncontractible plane-logical operators span the entire logical space; and charge-push diagnostics show that the self-similar fractal operators are absent. These results demonstrate that constrained randomness can fundamentally change the nature of stabilizer codes and improve their self-correction properties. They further point to broader families of quantum error-correcting codes and quantum phases beyond canonical topological and fracton orders.


---


## 有限温度下无场分子取向的Schur--Horn束缚

**Original Title:** Schur--Horn bound on field-free molecular orientation at finite temperature

**Authors:** Tanveer Ahmad

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21164v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21164v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

The maximum field-free orientation attainable from a \emph{thermal} molecular ensemble within a finite rotational subspace has not been characterised analytically. Here we derive a Schur--Horn-type upper bound on the field-free orientation $\avg{\cosθ}$ achievable by \emph{any} $M$-conserving unitary control acting on a Boltzmann ensemble truncated to rotational levels $J\le\Jmax$. The bound is the sum, over magnetic-quantum-number sectors, of the sorted Boltzmann weights paired with the sorted spectrum of $\cosθ$; it is purely kinematic, set by temperature, the rotational constant, and $\Jmax$ alone, and interpolates exactly between the zero-temperature subspace eigenvalue and a finite-temperature ceiling fixed by the rotational partition function. Benchmarked on LiH against the analytical $N$-subpulse resonant protocol of Hong \textit{et al.} [Phys.\ Rev.\ Research \textbf{7}, L012049 (2025)], it reveals three regimes: the protocol saturates the bound to within about $1.6\%$ for $T\le\SI{5}{\kelvin}$, loses roughly $10\%$ of its zero-temperature orientation at $T=B/\kB\approx\SI{10.8}{\kelvin}$, and leaves a $10$--$40\%$ gap above $\SI{10}{\kelvin}$. Optimising the subpulse areas and carrier phases within the fixed layout closes only $\approx7\%$ of that gap, the optimal phase offsets vanishing, which localises the dominant loss in the rigidity of the analytic layout rather than in the choice of areas or phases. The bound is a control-independent target for coherent-control design, applies unchanged to any linear polar molecule in a $^1Σ^+$ state, and is mapped across the $(\Jmax,T)$ plane.


### Abstract

The maximum field-free orientation attainable from a \emph{thermal} molecular ensemble within a finite rotational subspace has not been characterised analytically. Here we derive a Schur--Horn-type upper bound on the field-free orientation $\avg{\cosθ}$ achievable by \emph{any} $M$-conserving unitary control acting on a Boltzmann ensemble truncated to rotational levels $J\le\Jmax$. The bound is the sum, over magnetic-quantum-number sectors, of the sorted Boltzmann weights paired with the sorted spectrum of $\cosθ$; it is purely kinematic, set by temperature, the rotational constant, and $\Jmax$ alone, and interpolates exactly between the zero-temperature subspace eigenvalue and a finite-temperature ceiling fixed by the rotational partition function. Benchmarked on LiH against the analytical $N$-subpulse resonant protocol of Hong \textit{et al.} [Phys.\ Rev.\ Research \textbf{7}, L012049 (2025)], it reveals three regimes: the protocol saturates the bound to within about $1.6\%$ for $T\le\SI{5}{\kelvin}$, loses roughly $10\%$ of its zero-temperature orientation at $T=B/\kB\approx\SI{10.8}{\kelvin}$, and leaves a $10$--$40\%$ gap above $\SI{10}{\kelvin}$. Optimising the subpulse areas and carrier phases within the fixed layout closes only $\approx7\%$ of that gap, the optimal phase offsets vanishing, which localises the dominant loss in the rigidity of the analytic layout rather than in the choice of areas or phases. The bound is a control-independent target for coherent-control design, applies unchanged to any linear polar molecule in a $^1Σ^+$ state, and is mapped across the $(\Jmax,T)$ plane.


---


## 量子系统的布局荷的界限

**Original Title:** Bounds on the Topological Charge of Photonic Systems

**Authors:** F. R. Prudencio, I. Souza, M. G. Silveirinha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21175v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21175v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

Topology已成为理解物理现象的核心概念，导致凝聚物质和光电子学的重要进展。最近的工作建立了电子系统中Chern绝缘体的能隙的普遍上界，揭示了布局、量子几何和光吸收之间的基本联系。在这里，我们将这个框架推广到光学系统，在不需要明确的布局分析的情况下推导出间隙陈数的严格上界。我们的方法能够估计频散和非频散区域中带间隙的拓扑荷。


### Abstract

Topology has become a central concept in understanding physical phenomena, leading to important advances in condensed matter and photonics. Recent work has established a universal upper bound on the energy gap of Chern insulators in electronic systems, revealing a fundamental connection between topology, quantum geometry, and optical absorption. Here, we generalize this framework to photonic systems, deriving rigorous upper bounds on gap Chern numbers without requiring explicit topological analysis. Our approach enables the estimation of the topological charge of band gaps in both dispersive and nondispersive regimes.


---


## 用于资源高效的容错量子计算的有界深度时空格子手术

**Original Title:** Bounded-depth spacetime lattice surgery for resource-efficient fault-tolerant quantum computation

**Authors:** Kou Hamada, Hiroki Hamaguchi, Yosuke Ueno, Yasunari Suzuki, Teruo Tanimoto, Nobuyuki Yoshioka

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21192v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21192v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

基于格子手术的容错量子计算需要以低时空负担的位置和路径编译。特别是，路由面临着通过更大的空间分配来抑制路径冲突和利用时间方向来实现辅助高效的时空路由之间的基本矛盾。现有的方法无法完全解决这种权衡问题，同时保持与工厂内部布局和终止保证的兼容性。在这里，我们介绍了双片路由，这是一种恒深时空路由方法，它使用两个连续的时间片，并保证其扭结宇称纠正在平面和堆叠架构下都终止。我们数值基准编译器上的哈密顿模拟工作负载表明，双片路由编译成本降低了高达2.4倍，在一个单一的切片基线。与投影路由（一种允许每条路径无限数量的时间片的现有方法）相比，双片路由实现了更小的电路体积，只有一个边际执行时间惩罚。结合与培养兼容的映射优化，整体改进达到了7.5倍以上的天真的单片编译基线。这些结果确定双层布线作为一个实际有用的操作点，在网格手术编译，并显示了显着的好处，在联合优化映射和路由。


### Abstract

Fault-tolerant quantum computing based on lattice surgery requires place-and-route compilation with low spacetime overhead. Routing, in particular, faces a basic tension between suppressing path conflicts through greater spatial allocation and exploiting the time direction to realize ancilla-efficient spacetime routing. Existing approaches do not fully resolve this trade-off while retaining compatibility with inner factory layouts and termination guarantees. Here we introduce double-slice routing, a constant-depth spacetime-routing method that uses two consecutive time slices with a guarantee that its kink-parity correction terminates under both planar and stacked architectures. We numerically benchmark the resulting compiler on Hamiltonian-simulation workloads to show that double-slice routing reduces compilation cost by up to a factor of 2.4 over a single-slice baseline. Compared to projective routing, an existing method that allows an unbounded number of time slices per path, double-slice routing achieves smaller circuit volume with only a marginal execution-time penalty. Combined with a cultivation-compatible mapping optimization, the overall improvement reaches up to 7.5-fold over a naive single-slice compilation baseline. These results identify double-slice routing as a practically useful operating point in lattice-surgery compilation and show the substantial benefit in joint optimization of mapping and routing.


---


## 量子体系中的同步

**Original Title:** Synchronization in the quantum regime

**Authors:** Finn Schmolke, Eric Lutz

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21226v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21226v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

同步--经典非线性系统中协调动力学的广泛自发出现--也能发生在量子体系中吗？这个问题最近引发了对量子系统中集体行为和时间自组织的深入研究。典型的量子特征，例如时间演化的线性性和量子噪音的存在，似乎阻碍了微观水平上同步性的出现。与此同时，量子一致性和量子相关性可能提供超越经典对应物的新型机制来增强同步性。在这里，我们调查最近的理论和实验进展，在量子同步，从同步振荡和真正的非经典形式的同步，以多体同步量子网络的表征。


### Abstract

Can synchronization -- the widespread spontaneous emergence of coordinated dynamics in classical nonlinear systems -- also occur in the quantum regime? This question has recently sparked intense research into collective behavior and temporal self-organization in quantum systems. Typical quantum features such as the linearity of time evolution and the presence of quantum noise seem to hinder the appearance of synchrony at the microscopic level. At the same time, quantum coherence and quantum correlations may provide novel mechanisms for enhancing synchronization beyond its classical counterpart. We here survey recent theoretical and experimental advances in quantum synchronization, ranging from the characterization of synchronous oscillations and genuinely nonclassical forms of synchrony to many-body synchronization on quantum networks.


---


## 量子蛋白质结构预测中的成本Hamilton可靠性评估

**Original Title:** Assessing Cost Hamiltonian Reliability in Quantum Protein Structure Prediction

**Authors:** Mathieu Roget, Cedric Damour, Frederic Cadet, Jingbo Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21241v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21241v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

在变分量子算法、QAOA和量子模拟中，成本Hamilton量定义了量子硬件探索的优化格局;然而，在许多应用驱动公式中，这个Hamilton量是真正任务级目标的简化代理。以基于格点的量子蛋白质结构预测为案例研究，我们研究了这种环境中常用的接触能成本Hamilton是否与结构准确性充分一致，正如RMSD针对实验确定的结构所测量的那样。通过这个具体问题，我们表明了独立于所使用的量子方法研究成本Hamilton的可靠性的重要性。这项工作表明，对于小肽和平均而言，所考虑的成本Hamilton的能量格局与实际误差的相关性不够好，无法提供有意义的预测。此外，这种相关性是通过更大的情况下的蒙特卡罗抽样来估计的。它表明，对于更大的问题实例和考虑更多的交互壳时，所述相关性会增加。这项研究说明了独立于所使用的量子算法来研究成本Hamilton相关性的意义。


### Abstract

In variational quantum algorithms, QAOA, and quantum annealing, the cost Hamiltonian defines the optimization landscape explored by the quantum hardware; however, in many application-driven formulations, this Hamiltonian is a simplified proxy for the true task-level objective. Using lattice-based quantum protein structure prediction as a case study, we investigate whether the contact-energy cost Hamiltonian commonly used in this setting is sufficiently aligned with structural accuracy, as measured by RMSD against experimentally determined structures. Through this specific problem, we show the importance of studying the reliability of the cost Hamiltonian independently from the quantum approach used. This work shows that, for small peptides and on average, the energy landscape of the considered cost Hamiltonian is not correlated well enough to the actual error to provide meaningful predictions. Moreover, this correlation was estimated through Monte-Carlo sampling for larger instances. It shows an increase of said correlation for larger problem instances and when more interaction shells are considered. This investigation illustrates the meaningfulness of investigating cost Hamiltonian relevance independently from the quantum algorithm used.


---


## 受挫折的1/2旋转海森堡梯中临界和拓扑量子相的纠缠-熵分析

**Original Title:** Entanglement-entropy analysis of critical and topological quantum phases in a frustrated spin-1/2 Heisenberg ladder

**Authors:** Azadeh Ghannadan, Hana Vargová, Jozef Genzor, Roman Krčmár, Andrej Gendiar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21242v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21242v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们研究了横向磁场中具有各向异性级间交换耦合$a $的受扰旋转-1/2海森堡梯的接地状态图。该键各向异性参数在类伊辛极限$a =0$、各向同性点$a =1$和XY主导区域$a\gg 1$之间连续插值。使用矩阵-积-状态框架内的密度矩阵重整化群计算，我们分析了二元纠缠、磁性和旋转相关性，以描述涌现的量子相。我们确定了六种不同的底价相，包括龙单重态、类霍尔丹态、Tomonaga-Luttinger液体、倾斜伊辛有序、XY极化和有序铁磁状态。虽然磁性和局部相关性提供了对相分类的第一个见解，但纠缠测量的有限尺寸缩放提供了对有间隙和无间隙状态的更敏感和统一的诊断。在无间隙状态下，我们提取了中心电荷$c \simeq 1$，证实了Tomonaga-Luttinger液体行为，而在倾斜伊辛相和铁磁相之间的转变，我们观察到$c \simeq 1/2$，与伊辛普适性一致。最后，我们发现类霍尔丹行为和扩展的临界Tomonaga-Luttinger液体状态都强烈限制在各向同性点$a = 1$附近。


### Abstract

We investigate the ground-state phase diagram of a frustrated spin-1/2 Heisenberg ladder in the transverse magnetic field with an anisotropic inter-rung exchange coupling $α$. This bond-anisotropic parameter continuously interpolates among the Ising-like limit $α=0$, the isotropic point $α=1$, and the XY-dominated regime $α\gg 1$. Using density-matrix renormalization group calculations within a matrix-product-state framework, we analyze bipartite entanglement, magnetization, and spin correlations to characterize the emergent quantum phases. We identify six distinct ground-state phases, including rung-singlet, Haldane-like, Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid, canted Ising-ordered, XY-polarized, and ordered ferromagnetic states. While magnetization and local correlations provide a first insight into phase classifications, the finite-size scaling of the entanglement measures offers a more sensitive and unified diagnostics of both gapped and gapless regimes. In the gapless regime, we extract the central charge $c \simeq 1$, confirming Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid behavior, while at the transition between the canted Ising and ferromagnetic phases, we observe $c \simeq 1/2$, consistent with the Ising universality. Finally, we find that both the Haldane-like behavior and the extended critical Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid regime are strongly confined to the vicinity of the isotropic point $α= 1$.


---


## 具有Rashba旋转轨道耦合的2D $d$波交流磁铁中的Floquet感生各向异性磁电阻和反常霍尔效应

**Original Title:** Floquet-induced anisotropic magnetoresistance and anomalous Hall effect in 2D $d$-wave altermagnets with Rashba spin-orbit coupling

**Authors:** Mohsen Yarmohammadi, Pieter M. Gunnink, Jairo Sinova, James K. Freericks

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21281v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21281v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

Alternagnets（AM）结合了动量相关的自旋分裂和零净磁化，使其成为自旋电子学的希望。周期性驱动使动态对称工程超越静态、特定材料的控制。我们表明，Floquet工程在2D $d$-波AM与平面外Néel顺序和Rashba自旋轨道耦合解锁平衡禁输运响应。单色驱动产生纯粹的面外磁化，产生纵向各向异性磁阻（AMR）和异常霍尔效应，而双色驱动产生面内和面外磁化，并通过次级光束的二次谐波激活横向AMR。类似的静态磁场需要数百特斯拉，在Floquet驾驶中避免。这些效应在线性、圆形和混合光偏振下持续存在，并且可以通过光参数进行调节。我们的研究结果建立了多色Floquet工程控制磁化和保护运输的AM。


### Abstract

Altermagnets (AMs) combine momentum-dependent spin splitting with zero net magnetization, making them promising for spintronics. Periodic driving enables dynamic symmetry engineering beyond static, material-specific control. We show that Floquet engineering in 2D $d$-wave AMs with out-of-plane Néel order and Rashba spin-orbit coupling unlocks equilibrium-forbidden transport responses. Monochromatic driving produces purely out-of-plane magnetization, yielding longitudinal anisotropic magnetoresistance (AMR) and an anomalous Hall effect, whereas bichromatic driving generates both in-plane and out-of-plane magnetizations and additionally activates transverse AMR via the second harmonic of the secondary beam. Comparable static magnetic fields would require hundreds of tesla, avoided in Floquet driving. These effects persist across linear, circular, and mixed light polarizations and are tunable via light parameters. Our results establish multi-color Floquet engineering for controlling magnetization and symmetry-protected transport in AMs.


---


## 通过自适应性减少测量误差

**Original Title:** Reducing measurement error with adaptivity

**Authors:** James Byrne, Noah Linden, Paul Skrzypczyk

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21283v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21283v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们表明，自适应性（也称为前向）是减少结合了有噪测量设备的多次使用的测量电路误差的强大资源。在之前的工作中，已经表明可以通过多次使用测量设备来减轻测量误差。到目前为止，最有效的协议是并行测量方案，其中所有测量都是同时进行的。我们将这个想法扩展到自适应测量方案，其中之前测量的结果可能会影响我们在电路中进一步处理的选择。我们表明，自适应测量电路通常可以比任何具有相同测量次数的非自适应测量电路进一步降低总体测量误差。特别是，我们表明，对于一大类有噪的双结果量子位测量，当使用少至三个测量时，就可以存在这种自适应优势。我们还表明，随着设备使用次数的增加，自适应优势在有噪的双结果量子位测量类别中是无限的。作为这项工作的一部分，我们设计并使用在非自适应和自适应情况下寻找最佳测量电路的方法。此外，我们还证明了有关此类电路极限的一般结果，无论是在测量量子位时，还是在测量量子位时。


### Abstract

We show that adaptivity, also called feed-forward, is a powerful resource in reducing the error of measurement circuits that combine multiple uses of a noisy measuring device. In previous work, it has been shown that error in measurements can be mitigated by using the measuring device multiple times. So far, the most effective protocols have been parallel measurement schemes, where all measurements are simultaneous. We extend this idea to adaptive measurement schemes, where the results of previous measurements can influence our choice of processing further down the circuit. We show that adaptive measurement circuits can in general reduce overall measurement errors further than any non-adaptive measurement circuit could with the same number of measurements. In particular, we show that for a large class of noisy two-outcome qubit measurements, such an adaptive advantage can exist when as few as three measurements are used. We also show that the adaptive advantage is unbounded across the class of noisy two-outcome qubit measurements, as the number of uses of the device increases. As part of this work, we devise and use methods for finding optimal measurement circuits in both the non-adaptive and adaptive cases. In addition, we prove general results about the limits of such circuits, both in measuring a qubit, and more generally, a qudit.


---


## 使用磷化铟和氮硅光电集成电路的时间段BB 84 QKD系统

**Original Title:** Time-Bin BB84 QKD System Using Indium Phosphide and Silicon Nitride Photonic Integrated Circuits

**Authors:** Denis Fatkhiev, Alexander Grebenchukov, João dos Reis Frazão, Gleb Nazarikov, Chigo Okonkwo, Idelfonso Tafur Monroy

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21308v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21308v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们演示了一个双芯片InP-SiN光量子密钥分配系统，具有片内脉冲产生和可重新配置解码，实现具有有限密钥安全性的时间点BB 84，以抵御一致攻击。该系统将QBER维持在4%以下，并在150-250公里的光纤上以kMbps的速率提供密钥。


### Abstract

We demonstrate a dual-chip InP-SiN photonic QKD system with on-chip pulse generation and reconfigurable decoding, implementing time-bin BB84 with finite-key security against coherent attacks. The system sustains a QBER below 4% and delivers secret keys at kbps rates over 150-250 km of fiber.


---


## 具有混合量子经典库的量子状态的时间处理

**Original Title:** Temporal processing of quantum states with hybrid quantum-classical reservoirs

**Authors:** Mateu Coll-Comas, Gian Luca Giorgi, Roberta Zambrini

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21327v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21327v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

量子水库计算（QRC）的一个独特特征是能够将量子输入状态直接嵌入到水库动力学中。然而，对于单个输入状态，最终的输出基本上是线性的，从而阻止QRC自然计算非线性函数，例如纯度或熵。我们通过量子-经典混合架构克服了这一限制，该架构将量子位量子库与经典回声状态网络（ESN）相结合，允许非线性函数逼近和有效的时间处理。我们系统地研究了两种信息状态下的性能：全断层扫描和部分信息（单轴测量），后者证明，由于量子库提供的增强信息检索，混合系统在线性和非线性任务中都优于其独立组件。在这些结果的基础上，我们应用了一种在线监控协议，该协议明确考虑了测量反作用和有限测量集合，从而能够在实验条件下对性能进行现实评估。这些结果建立了混合量子-经典库计算（HRC）架构，作为在近期量子位硬件上增强量子机器学习的实用且可扩展的途径。


### Abstract

A distinctive feature of Quantum Reservoir Computing (QRC) is the ability to directly embed quantum input states into the reservoir dynamics. However, the resulting output is fundamentally linear for a single input state, preventing QRC from naturally computing nonlinear functionals such as purity or entropy. We overcome this limitation with a quantum-classical hybrid architecture combining a qubit quantum reservoir with a classical echo state network (ESN), allowing both nonlinear functional approximation and effective temporal processing. We systematically study performance under two information regimes: full-tomography and partial information (single-axis measurements), with the latter demonstrating that the hybrid system outperforms its standalone components in both linear and nonlinear tasks due to the enhanced information retrieval provided by the quantum reservoir. Building on these results, we apply an online monitoring protocol that explicitly accounts for measurement back-action and finite measurement ensembles, enabling a realistic assessment of performance under experimental conditions. These results establish hybrid quantum-classical reservoir computing (HRC) architectures as a practical and scalable route for enhanced quantum machine learning on near-term qubit hardware.


---


## 与局部状态有效验证纠缠测量

**Original Title:** Efficient Verification of Entangled Measurements with Local States

**Authors:** Kun Wang, Masahito Hayashi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21355v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21355v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们开发了一个框架，量子测量验证（QMV）只使用本地状态的准备。对于局部传递和不可约的投影测量，我们证明了对称性将局部约束的QMV减少到单个基态的量子态验证，从而将协议设计减少到齐次验证算子的优化。我们将该框架应用于广义Bell测量，两个量子比特的单参数测量，优雅的联合测量，稳定状态诱导测量，并导出显式本地协议连同封闭形式的验证算子，成功概率和样本复杂性。我们进一步表明，同质QMV协议可以直接从观察到的通过频率估计测量保真度。


### Abstract

We develop a framework for quantum measurement verification (QMV) using only local state preparations. For locally transitive and irreducible projective measurements, we prove that symmetry reduces locality constrained QMV to quantum state verification of a single basis state, thereby reducing protocol design to the optimization of homogeneous verification operators. We apply the framework to generalized Bell measurements, single-parameter measurements on two qubits, elegant joint measurements, and stabilizer state induced measurements, and derive explicit local protocols together with closed form verification operators, success probabilities, and sample complexities. We further show that homogeneous QMV protocols can estimate measurement fidelity directly from observed passing frequencies.


---


## 大型俘获离子晶体中的量子分束器冷却和测温

**Original Title:** Quantum Beam-Splitter Cooling and Thermometry in Large Trapped-Ion Crystals

**Authors:** Kirthik Rajakumar, Ansh Das, Abhinay Pandey, Athreya Shankar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21357v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21357v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们提出并描述了一种用于快速近接地状态冷却质量中心（c.m.）的协议大型俘获离子晶体的模式。当模式$\bar{n}_i$的初始平均热占用与离子数量$N$相比较小时，红色边带驱动器在模式和$N$离子的集体旋转之间实施分束器型SWAP操作，后者有效地充当量子谐振子。随后，旋转的重置消除了熵，导致厘米的近接地状态冷却。模式我们将该协议称为量子分束器冷却（QBSC）。我们分析了几个实际缺陷对QBSC下可实现的最终温度的影响，包括有限离子数、非共振载子和蓝带贡献，以及旁观者模式产生的边带驱动的影响。此外，我们还概述了消除载体驱动的实用策略。此外，我们表明，在SWAP操作结束时测量离子的布居统计数据可以实现接近最佳的量子分束器测温（QBST），经典的费舍尔信息接近热状态的量子费舍尔信息。我们讨论了QBSC与连续边带冷却的联系，并将QBST与最近提出的基于快速隔热恒温的测温方案进行了比较。我们的工作构成了利用多体效应在大型俘获离子晶体中开辟激光冷却和测温新途径的一个例子。


### Abstract

We propose and characterize a protocol for rapid near-ground state cooling of the center-of-mass (c.m.) mode of a large trapped ion crystal. When the initial mean thermal occupation of the mode $\bar{n}_i$ is small compared to the number of ions $N$, a red sideband drive implements a beam-splitter type SWAP operation between the mode and the collective spin of the $N$ ions, with the latter effectively serving as a quantum harmonic oscillator. Subsequently, a reset of the spins removes the entropy, leading to near-ground state cooling of the c.m. mode. We term this protocol as quantum beam-splitter cooling (QBSC). We analyze the impact of several practical imperfections on the final temperature achievable under QBSC, including finite ion number, off-resonant carrier and blue-sideband contributions, and the impact of the sideband drives arising from spectator modes. In addition, we outline practical strategies to eliminate the carrier drive. Furthermore, we show that measuring the population statistics of the ions at the end of the SWAP operation can enable near-optimal quantum beam-splitter thermometry (QBST), with the classical Fisher information approaching the quantum Fisher information of a thermal state. We discuss the connection of QBSC with continuous sideband cooling and compare QBST with a recently proposed rapid adiabatic passage-based thermometry scheme. Our work constitutes an example of harnessing many-body effects to open new routes to laser cooling and thermometry in large trapped ion crystals.


---


## 贝尔不等式专为最佳全球随机性认证定制

**Original Title:** Bell inequalities tailored to optimal global randomness certification

**Authors:** Ignacio Perito, Raffaele D'Avino, Michał Jung, Piotr Mironowicz, Antonio Acín, Remigiusz Augusiak

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21362v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21362v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们提出了两个新颖的二元贝尔不等式族，旨在为任意数量的输出$d$实现最佳全局随机性证明。我们首先使用对称性论点来证明它们的最大量子违背证明$2\log d$随机比特。对于第一个家庭，我们使用$d\乘d$最大纠缠态构建量子实现，该量子实现提供了我们推测对于任何$d$来说都是最佳的量子破坏。然后通过数值证明，对于$d= 3，4 $，获得的量子破坏证明了最佳的全局随机性，达到了数字精度。对于第二个家庭，我们为任何$d$提供了最佳量子破坏及其量子实现，再次使用$d\乘d$最大纠缠态和对其中一方的至少两个无偏基的投影测量。我们对$d=3$进行了自我测试，这意味着两个完全随机的trits的最佳认证。


### Abstract

We present two novel families of bipartite Bell inequalities designed to achieve optimal global randomness certification for an arbitrary number of outputs $d$. We first use symmetry arguments to argue that their maximal quantum violations certify $2\log d$ random bits. For the first family, we construct a quantum realization using $d\times d$ maximally entangled states which provides a quantum violation that we conjecture to be optimal for any $d$. It is then numerically shown that the obtained quantum violation certifies optimal global randomness, up to numerical precision, for $d=3,4$. For the second family, we provide the optimal quantum violation and its quantum realization for any $d$, again using $d\times d$ maximally entangled states and projective measurements over at least two unbiased bases on one of the parties. We self-test this realization for $d=3$, which implies the optimal certification of two fully random trits.


---


## 来自各个维度投影测量的最大全球设备独立随机性

**Original Title:** Maximal global device-independent randomness from projective measurements in every dimension

**Authors:** Máté Farkas, Piotr Mironowicz, Remigiusz Augusiak

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21369v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21369v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

与设备无关的随机数生成（DIQRNG）是使用量子物理过程生成私人随机性的最安全形式。它的优势在于产生任何受量子理论定律限制的窃听者都无法预测的数字。此外，安全性仅通过观察到的测量统计数据来证明，无需验证或信任随机数生成中使用的设备。然而，实施DIQRNG的成本很高，因为它需要高质量的纠缠系统。因此，充分利用可用资源非常重要。在这项工作中，我们表明，使用投影测量（最容易通过实验实现），可以从局部维度$d$的二元系统中验证$2\log（d）$比特的设备无关随机性，从而达到DIQRNG的理论上可能的最大速率。我们提供了基于相互无偏基础的达到$2\log（d）$比特的显式协议。此外，我们计算了不完美实现情况下速率的数字界限，表明我们的协议对实验噪音具有鲁棒性。


### Abstract

Device-independent random number generation (DIQRNG) is the most secure form of generating private randomness using quantum physical processes. Its strength lies in producing numbers that are impossible to predict by any eavesdropper restricted by the laws of quantum theory. Moreover, security is proven solely from observed measurement statistics, without the need to characterise or trust the devices used in random number generation. Implementing DIQRNG is, however, costly, as it requires high-quality entangled systems. It is therefore important to make the best use of available resources. In this work, we show that using projective measurements -- which are most readily implementable experimentally -- one can certify $2\log(d)$ bits of device-independent randomness from a bipartite system of local dimension $d$ for every $d \ge 2$, thus reaching the theoretically maximum possible rate of DIQRNG. We provide explicit protocols reaching $2\log(d)$ bits based on mutually unbiased bases. Furthermore, we compute numerical bounds on the rate for the case of imperfect implementations, showing that our protocols are robust to experimental noise.


---


## 贝尔认证量子随机性的三种结果的噪音稳健性

**Original Title:** Noise robustness of three outcome Bell certified quantum randomness

**Authors:** Raffaele D'Avino, Ignacio Perito, Piotr Mironowicz, Antonio Acín, Remigiusz Augusiak

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21371v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21371v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们根据双方场景中违反贝尔不等式，调查了与设备无关的全球随机性认证，每方有三个结果。我们的目标是确定多结果测量是否允许人们超越现实场景中二进制输出可实现的随机性。我们首先分析几个已知的贝尔表达，并评估它们对随机性认证的噪音的鲁棒性。然后，我们引入一种在结构化家族中生成新贝尔表达的系统方法，并进行大规模数值研究。我们发现，大量的不等式证明了大量的最小信息。特别是，我们识别了简单的不等式，这些不等式可以实现接近最大的全局随机性，同时涉及减少的测量设置数量，从而改善了认证随机性和输入数量之间的平衡。此外，绝大多数非平凡证书都表现出对现实噪音的鲁棒性，保持了远离理想制度的正认证随机性。这些结果表明，多结果场景中与设备无关的强随机性扩展并不局限于精心设计的不等式，而是普遍出现在适当构造的贝尔表达族中。


### Abstract

We investigate device-independent certification of global randomness based on Bell inequality violations in bipartite scenarios with three outcomes per party. Our goal is to determine whether multi-outcome measurements allow one to surpass the amount of randomness achievable with binary outputs in realistic scenarios. We begin by analyzing several known Bell expressions and evaluating their robustness against noise for randomness certification. We then introduce a systematic method for generating new Bell expressions within structured families and perform a large-scale numerical study. We find that a substantial number of inequalities certify significant amounts of min-entropy. In particular, we identify simple inequalities that achieve near-maximal global randomness while involving a reduced number of measurement settings, thus improving the balance between certified randomness and number of inputs. Moreover, the vast majority of nontrivial certificates exhibit robustness against realistic noise, maintaining positive certified randomness away from the ideal regime. These results demonstrate that strong device-independent randomness expansion in multi-outcome scenarios is not restricted to carefully engineered inequalities, but arises generically within suitably constructed families of Bell expressions.


---


## 离子晶体边带冷却的集体增强

**Original Title:** Collective enhancement in sideband cooling of ion crystals

**Authors:** Ivan Vybornyi, Artem Zhdanov, Matthias Bock, Leo Walz, Nele Griesbach, Klemens Hammerer, Christian F. Roos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21374v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21374v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

离子库伦晶体的低熵运动状态是大量应用的必要先决条件，通常通过激光冷却来制备。随着更大的晶体在量子机制中运行，增加离子数量是否有利于冷却仍然不清楚，并且最近也引起了争论。在这里，我们从理论和实验上研究了多离子边带冷却以及集体效应在不同的旋转运动耦合区中的作用。对于弱耦合，多体效应并不重要。然而，在强耦合机制中，旋转和运动子系统经历了相干状态交换，从而能够通过适当定时的激光脉冲进行冷却。使用最多91个离子的平面库伦晶体，我们证明了一个这样的脉冲后的剩余平均音素占据随着离子数量的变化而变化为1美元/N2美元。通过迭代脉冲，我们测量平均音素占据率$<2\cdot10 '' cdot 10 ''''。对于处于相干区的大型晶体，我们进一步表明，旋转运动动力学在很大程度上与初始音素统计无关。通过旋转测量，可以利用状态交换机制来探测模式中的音素分布。


### Abstract

Low-entropy motional states of ion Coulomb crystals are an essential prerequisite for a plethora of applications and are typically prepared by laser cooling. As larger crystals are operated in the quantum regime, it remains unclear, and has recently become debated, whether increasing the ion number can be beneficial for cooling. Here, we investigate theoretically and experimentally many-ion sideband cooling and the role of collective effects in different spin-motion coupling regimes. For weak coupling, the many-body effects are insignificant. In the strong-coupling regime, however, the spin and motional subsystems undergo a coherent state swap, enabling cooling by a suitably timed laser pulse. Using planar Coulomb crystals with up to 91 ions, we demonstrate that the residual mean phonon occupation after one such pulse scales as $1/N^2$ with the number of ions. By iterating the pulses, we measure mean phonon occupations $<2\cdot10^{-4}$. For large crystals in the coherent regime, we further show that the spin-motion dynamics becomes largely independent of the initial phonon statistics. Through spin measurements, the state-swap mechanism can be utilized to probe the phonon distribution in the mode.


---


## 基于交叉克尔相互作用和机械参数放大的磁力学系统纠缠工程

**Original Title:** Entanglement engineering in magnomechanical system via cross-Kerr interaction and mechanical parametric amplification

**Authors:** E. Kongkui Berinyuy, P. Djorwé, A. N. Al-Ahmadi, H. Ardah, A. -H. Abdel-Aty

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21388v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21388v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

腔磁机械系统中的量子纠缠在现代量子技术中有着广泛的应用。在这项工作中，我们提出了一个理论方案，通过磁机械系统中的交叉克尔非线性和机械参数放大（MPA）来产生和增强量子纠缠。我们的系统由磁共振模式组成，该模式同时驱动Y铁石榴球中的声学音素和质量中心运动（CMA）音素。声学模式和质量中心机械（CMA）模式通过音素跳变率$J_m$弱耦合。此外，磁振子模和音素模通过交叉克尔相互作用相互作用，而音素模还通过机械参数放大（MPA）驱动。如果没有机械耦合（$J_m = 0$）和MPA，子系统之间纠缠的产生需要相对较强的有效交叉克尔耦合。然而，当考虑到音素跳变和MPA时，即使交叉克尔耦合强度的值很小，也可以产生量子纠缠，这揭示了这些相互作用在我们的提案中量子相关工程中的关键作用。此外，对于相同参数的区域，产生的纠缠态的相关纯度仍然很高，这表明产生的量子纠缠是在没有显着增加系统中所涉及状态的混合的情况下建立的。我们的工作表明，如何在基于非线性相互作用的磁力学结构中设计出稳健和稳定的量子相关性。这些结果对于现代量子应用非常有用，包括量子信息处理、量子通信和量子计算任务。


### Abstract

Quantum entanglement in cavity magnomechanical system has a wide range of applications in modern quantum technologies. In this work, we propose a theoretical scheme to generate and enhance quantum entanglement through cross-Kerr nonlinearity and mechanical parametric amplification (MPA) in a magnomechanical system. Our system is made of a magnonic mode that is simultaneously driving the acoustic phononic and the center-of-mass motion (CMM) phonon in a yttrium iron garnet sphere. The acoustic mode and the center-of-mass mechanical (CMM) mode are weakly coupled via the phonon hopping rate $J_m$. Moreover, the magnonic and phononic modes interact through cross-Kerr interaction, while the phononic mode is additionally driven via a Mechanical Parametric Amplification (MPA). Without the mechanical coupling ($J_m = 0$) and the MPA, the generation of entanglement among the subsystems requires a relatively strong effective cross-Kerr coupling. However, when phonon hopping and MPA are accounted, quantum entanglement can be generated even for weak values of the cross-Kerr coupling strength, revealing the key role of these interactions in the engineering of quantum correlations in our proposal. Furthermore, the related purity of the generated entangled states remains high for the same parameter's regime, revealing that the generated quantum entanglement is established without significantly increasing the mixing of the involved states in the system. Our work suggests how robust and stable quantum correlations can be engineered in magnomechanical structures based on nonlinear interactions. These results are useful for modern quantum applications including quantum information processing, quantum communication, and quantum computational tasks.


---


## 自旋量子比特的通道模式穿梭操作

**Original Title:** Spin qubit operations by conveyor-mode shuttling

**Authors:** M. De Smet, Y. Matsumoto, D. Fernández-Fernández, L. Tryputen, S. L. de Snoo, D. J. Michalak, H. G. J. Eenink, G. Platero, S. Bosco, G. Scappucci, L. M. K. Vandersypen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21452v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21452v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

动态量子位路由正在成为半导体量子处理器的一种有前途的架构路径。电荷载体可以使用称为传送带的传播波势在芯片上快速移动，以高保真度保持旋转状态。纵向模式穿梭最初是为了旋转传输而开发的，它还可能提供执行由运动本身直接控制的量子位操作的机会。在这里，我们使用两种概念上不同的方法，通过半导体模式电子穿梭来演示相干单量子位和双量子位控制。首先，传送带电偶极旋转共振（传送带EDSR）通过以平均拉莫尔频率在横向磁场梯度中共振穿梭旋转来实现高保真度旋转。其次，传送带非对称门利用量化轴倾斜来实现可调的砰砰控制。将非热传送带传输与由运动控制的交换激活相结合，直接产生各种有效的两量子位相互作用，可通过穿梭速度和距离进行选择。这些实验结果激发了可重新配置和传输驱动的旋转量子位的架构范式。


### Abstract

Dynamic qubit routing is emerging as a promising architectural path for semiconductor quantum processors. Charge carriers can be rapidly moved around on a chip using traveling-wave potentials known as conveyors, preserving the spin state with high fidelity. Originally developed for spin transport, conveyor-mode shuttling may also offer opportunities for performing qubit operations directly controlled by the motion itself. Here, we demonstrate coherent single- and two-qubit control by conveyor-mode electron shuttling, using two conceptually different approaches. First, conveyor electric-dipole spin resonance (conveyor EDSR) achieves high-fidelity rotations by resonantly shuttling spins through transverse magnetic-field gradients at their mean Larmor frequency. Second, conveyor diabatic gates exploit quantization-axis tilts for tunable bang-bang control. Combining diabatic conveyor transport with exchange activation controlled by the motion directly yields a variety of effective two-qubit interactions selectable via the shuttling speed and distance. These experimental results motivate an architectural paradigm of reconfigurable and transport-driven spin qubits.


---


## 激冷玻色子约瑟夫森结中的量子功统计和相干效应

**Original Title:** Quantum work statistics and coherence effects in quenched bosonic Josephson junctions

**Authors:** Mattia Orlandini, Stefano Gherardini, Lorenzo Buffoni, Beatrice Donelli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21472v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21472v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们研究了玻色子约瑟夫森结中突然熄灭产生的非平衡功统计。特别是，通过采用Holstein-Primakoff逼近，在弱相互作用区域中对功统计进行了分析描述，其中动力学映射到与时相关的量子谐振子上。对于在预灭Hamilton的基态中初始化的结，我们证明了功统计由负二项分布决定，正如在跨越临界点驱动的全连接模型中所发生的那样。此外，我们还考虑了能量基中包含量子内聚性的初始叠加态。为了描述相应的功分布，我们使用柯克伍德-狄拉克准概率（KDK）。即使在最简单的情况下，当结初始化为基态和第二激发态的叠加时，功的KDK分布也会表现出负值或复值，反映出非经典特征。此外，可以优化初始状态的相干含量，以增强从激灭提取的可提取功，超出经典界限。最后，我们提出了一种实验干涉协议，以直接测量实验可访问的环境中功分布的特征函数。


### Abstract

We investigate the non-equilibrium work statistics originating from a sudden quench in a bosonic Josephson junction. In particular, by employing the Holstein-Primakoff approximation, the work statistics are analytically characterized in the weak-interaction regime, where the dynamics map onto a time-dependent quantum harmonic oscillator. For a junction initialized in the ground state of the pre-quench Hamiltonian, we demonstrate that the work statistics are governed by a negative binomial distribution, as occurs in fully-connected models driven across a critical point. Furthermore, we also consider initial superposition states containing quantum coherences in the energy basis. To characterize the corresponding work distributions, we employ Kirkwood-Dirac quasiprobabilities (KDQ). Even in the simplest case, when the junction is initialized in a superposition of the ground and second excited states, the KDQ distribution of work exhibits negative or complex values, reflecting non-classical features. Moreover, the coherence content of the initial state can be optimized to enhance the extractable work extracted from the quench, beyond classical bounds. Finally, we propose an experimental interferometric protocol to directly measure the characteristic function of the work distribution in experimentally accessible settings.


---


## 通过信息集本地解码实现LOSR量子网络中的最佳GZZ状态分布

**Original Title:** Optimal GHZ-State Distribution in LOSR Quantum Networks via Local Decoding from Information Sets

**Authors:** Leonardo Oleynik, Shehbaz Tariq, Symeon Chatzinotas

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21500v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21500v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

分配多方纠缠是可扩展量子网络的先决条件。限制于本地操作和共享随机性（LOSR）的网络避免了与基于LOCC的网络所需的实时经典通信相关的量子存储器和延迟成本。然而，当只有双方来源可用时，LOSR网络无法准备有用的GZZ状态。在早期的工作中，我们推测多方来源克服了这一限制，并通过一个数字例子支持了这一主张。在这项工作中，我们证明了任意大小的规则和均匀网络的猜想。通过用线性码的坐标识别网络的超边界，我们表明，每当每个节点的边形成信息集时，固定的本地正元集合（即代码的本地解码器）就会将源状态转换为具有保真度（d '{m-M}）的（N）方GZZ状态，而不需要任何经典通信。这里，（m）表示涉及到每个节点的边的数量，（M）表示网络中边的总数。对于完全（N-1））-一致超图（K_N^{（N-1）}），这种保真度减少到（1/d）。我们进一步证明，这个值在所有局部单一策略中是最优的，并且超过了仅使用双方源可实现的最佳保真度。例如，在四节点的情况下，最佳保真度为（1/2），而二部界为（1/8）。这些结果表明，多方源加上共享随机性，可以取代实时经典通信进行纠缠分布。


### Abstract

Distributing multipartite entanglement is a prerequisite for scalable quantum networks. Networks restricted to local operations and shared randomness (LOSR) avoid the quantum-memory and latency costs associated with the real-time classical communication required by LOCC-based networks. However, when only bipartite sources are available, LOSR networks cannot prepare useful GHZ states. In earlier work, we conjectured that multipartite sources overcome this limitation and supported this claim with a single numerical example. In this work, we prove the conjecture for regular and uniform networks of arbitrary size. By identifying the hyperedges of the network with the coordinates of a linear code, we show that whenever the edges incident to each node form an information set, a fixed collection of local unitaries, namely the local decoders of the code, transforms the source state into an (N)-party GHZ state with fidelity (d^{m-M}), without requiring any classical communication. Here, (m) denotes the number of edges incident to each node and (M) the total number of edges in the network. For the complete ((N-1))-uniform hypergraph (K_N^{(N-1)}), this fidelity reduces to (1/d). We further prove that this value is optimal among all local-unitary strategies and exceeds the best fidelity achievable using only bipartite sources. For example, in the four-node case, the optimal fidelity is (1/2), compared with the bipartite bound of (1/8). These results demonstrate that multipartite sources, together with shared randomness, can replace real-time classical communication for entanglement distribution.


---


## 相稳定集成延迟线非对称马赫曾德干涉仪由高效率3分贝耦合器实现，用于芯片级QKD

**Original Title:** Phase Stable Integrated Delay Line Asymmetric Mach Zehnder Interferometers Enabled by High Efficiency 3 dB Couplers for Chip Scale QKD

**Authors:** Mahsa. Ghezelbash, Abdollah Eslami Majd

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21542v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21542v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

精确的时间延迟生成是用于高速量子密钥分发（QKD）接收机的非对称马赫-曾德干涉仪（aMZZ）的关键要求。在这项工作中，提出了一种基于二氧化硅上的硅氮（Si 3 N4/SiO2）光学平台的紧凑集成aMZZ架构。设计并优化了一个3-分贝定向耦合器，能够在1550纳米电信波长下实现精确的50：50功率分配。耦合长度最初根据偶数和奇数超模之间的有效指数差估计，随后使用三维本征模展开（EME）模拟进行细化。   优化的结构采用横截面积为1 um x 0.4 um的单模Si 3 N4光路，提供接近2的群指数，并实现精确的延迟工程。频谱分析表明，C频段上存在稳定的3分贝功率分配，插入损耗低于0.5分贝，功率失衡可忽略不计，表明传输效率高且结构对称性。进一步演示了集成的Si 3 N4 aMZZ延迟线，提供500 ps的光延迟，对应于2 GHz自由光谱范围（FSR）。   模拟显示，190-200 THz频率范围内的群延迟几乎恒定，变化低于10 ps，并且具有平滑、近线性的相响应。这些特征使干扰可见性高于0.99，对应于千兆赫速率时元QKD系统的估计量子误比特率（QBER）低于0.5%。宽带线性相行为还表明与时分多路传输（CDM）QKD架构的兼容性。结果证实，拟议的Si 3 N4集成aMZZ提供了一种低损耗、分散受控且光谱稳定的延迟解决方案，适合可扩展芯片级量子光接收器。


### Abstract

Precise temporal delay generation is a key requirement for asymmetric Mach-Zehnder interferometers (aMZIs) used in high-speed quantum key distribution (QKD) receivers. In this work, a compact integrated aMZI architecture based on a silicon nitride on silicon dioxide (Si3N4/SiO2) photonic platform is presented. A 3-dB directional coupler enabling accurate 50:50 power splitting at the 1550 nm telecommunication wavelength is designed and optimized. The coupling length is initially estimated from the effective index difference between the even and odd supermodes and subsequently refined using three-dimensional eigenmode expansion (EME) simulations.
  The optimized structure employs single-mode Si3N4 waveguides with a cross section of 1 um x 0.4 um, providing a group index close to 2 and enabling accurate delay engineering. Spectral analysis demonstrates stable 3-dB power splitting across the C-band with insertion loss below 0.5 dB and negligible power imbalance, indicating high transmission efficiency and structural symmetry. An integrated Si3N4 aMZI delay line providing a 500 ps optical delay, corresponding to a 2 GHz free spectral range (FSR), is further demonstrated.
  Simulations show nearly constant group delay across the 190-200 THz frequency range with sub-10 ps variation and a smooth, near-linear phase response. These characteristics enable interference visibility above 0.99, corresponding to an estimated quantum bit error rate (QBER) below 0.5 percent for gigahertz-rate time-bin QKD systems. The wideband linear phase behavior also indicates compatibility with wavelength division multiplexed (WDM) QKD architectures. The results confirm that the proposed Si3N4 integrated aMZI provides a low-loss, dispersion-controlled, and spectrally stable delay solution suitable for scalable chip-scale quantum photonic receivers.

## 半单立方格子上具有费米子的SU（2）规范理论

**Original Title:** SU(2) gauge theory with fermions on a semi-simple cubic lattice

**Authors:** Randy Lewis, Shidsa Pourbakhsh, Arnab Pradhan, Lance Siquioco

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21563v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21563v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

一个实用的格点规范理论的哈密顿方法将提供进入现象学的几个重要领域，已经超出了传统的格点方法。量子计算机似乎是这种方法的天然平台。考虑到近期的量子计算机，我们的工作考虑了一个三维空间晶格，它可以容纳费米子和非阿贝尔规范场，同时需要比简单立方晶格更少的量子位。具体地说，半简单立方（ssc）晶格是通过从标准立方晶格中移除一半的规范链接来获得的，以这种方式每个顶点都变成三价的，这简化了高斯定律的处理。ssc网格在布局上与三角网格等效，但由于每个点的规范链接跨越所有三个方向，因此ssc网格可以容纳局部费米子求导。这里介绍了具有SU（2）规范场的交错费米子的情况。


### Abstract

A practical Hamiltonian approach to lattice gauge theories would provide access to several important areas of phenomenology that have been beyond the reach of conventional lattice methods. Quantum computers seem to be a natural platform for this approach. With near-term quantum computers in mind, our work considers a three-dimensional spatial lattice that can host fermions and non-Abelian gauge fields while needing fewer qubits than a simple cubic lattice. Specifically, the semi-simple cubic (ssc) lattice is obtained by removing half of the gauge links from a standard cubic lattice in such a way that every vertex becomes trivalent, which streamlines the handling of Gauss's law. The ssc lattice is topologically equivalent to the triamond lattice but, because the gauge links at each vertex span all three directions, the ssc lattice can accommodate a local fermion derivative. The case of staggered fermions with SU(2) gauge fields is presented here.

## 移动的费米极化子

**Original Title:** The moving Fermi polaron

**Authors:** Johanna Hennebichler, Ruben Erlenstedt, Erich Dobler, Cosetta Baroni, Rudolf Grimm, Matteo Caldara, Georg Bruun, Pietro Massignan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21567v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21567v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

费米极化子由与周围费米海相互作用的杂质形成，体现了典型准粒子概念，作为我们描述广泛能量尺度上的量子多体系统的基石。原子量子气体实验为费米极化子的普遍性质提供了深刻的见解。虽然之前的大多数研究都集中在零杂质动量的情况下，但有限动量性质在很大程度上仍然未知。在这里，我们通过将新型拉曼加速方案与高精度射频光谱相结合来研究移动的费米极化子，探索宽动量范围内的准粒子分散关系。我们将能量漂移和光谱线宽度的测量结果与微观理论进行了比较，并对所有动量达成了定量一致。对于低动量，我们发现移动极化子的能量与具有恒定有效质量的修饰粒子的费米液体图像完全一致。在高动量下，极化子接近弱相互作用裸粒子的行为，具有小的能量漂移和弱的增宽。对于中间动量，增宽通常更大，最引人注目的是，吸引和排斥极化子的行为不同。虽然排斥极化子在两个状态之间表现出平滑的联系以及能量移动的单调变化，但有吸引力的情况显示出一种奇特的非单调行为。随着动量的增加，有吸引力的极化子进入一个状态，其中其能量偏离恒定有效质量表达并且增宽突然增加。通过将这一观察结果与理论进行比较，我们表明这种突然行为与吸引极化子进入分子-洞连续体相一致，其中它不再是底价。我们将其解释为运动引起的极化子-分子转变。


### Abstract

The Fermi polaron, formed by an impurity interacting with a surrounding Fermi sea, exemplifies the canonical quasiparticle concept as a cornerstone in our description of quantum many-body systems across a wide range of energy scales. Experiments on atomic quantum gases have provided profound insights into the universal nature of the Fermi polaron. While most previous studies have focused on the case of zero impurity momentum, finite-momentum properties have remained largely uncharted. Here, we investigate the moving Fermi polaron by combining a novel Raman acceleration scheme with high-precision radio-frequency spectroscopy, exploring the quasiparticle dispersion relation over a wide range of momenta. We compare our measurements of energy shifts and spectral linewidths with a microscopic theory and reach quantitative agreement for all momenta. For low momenta, we find the energy of the moving polaron to be fully consistent with the Fermi liquid picture of a dressed particle with a constant effective mass. At high momenta, the polaron approaches the behavior of a weakly interacting bare particle, featuring small energy shifts and weak broadening. For intermediate momenta, broadening is generally larger and, most strikingly, the behavior differs for attractive and repulsive polarons. While the repulsive polaron exhibits a smooth connection between both regimes along with a monotonic change of the energy shift, the attractive case shows a peculiar non-monotonic behavior. With increasing momentum, the attractive polaron enters a regime where its energy deviates from the constant effective mass expression and broadening suddenly increases. By comparing this observation with theory, we show that this abrupt behavior coincides with the attractive polaron entering a molecule-hole continuum, where it is no longer the ground state. We interpret this as a motion-induced polaron-molecule transition.


---


## 用于变分量子分类的相关感知量子特征图

**Original Title:** A Correlation Aware Quantum Feature Map for Variational Quantum Classification

**Authors:** Murat Kurt

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21570v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21570v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

量子机器学习已成为学习复杂数据模式的一个有前途的研究领域。然而，大多数现有的量子特征地图采用固定编码策略，这些策略没有明确考虑数据集中特征之间的关系。在这项研究中，我们提出了一种相关感知量子特征地图（CAQFM），它将特征依赖性集成到量子编码过程中。所提出的方法利用Pearson、Spearman、Kendall Tau、互信息和距离相关性测量来识别特征之间的关系。超过预定义阈值的依赖通过受控量子门被纳入量子电路，从而能够构建更丰富的量子表示，更好地反映数据的底层结构。   使用变分量子分类器（VQC）对三个基准数据集进行评估，即乳腺癌诊断、信用违约预测和学生安置分类。模拟结果表明，与传统编码策略相比，基于相关性的量子编码可以提高分类性能。特别是，基于Spearman和Kendall Tau的CAQFM变体实现了最高的预测性能，并且始终优于标准量子特征地图。研究结果表明，将依赖信息从经典的数据到量子特征映射有利于产生更多的歧视性量子表示，并提高变分量子分类器的有效性。


### Abstract

Quantum machine learning has emerged as a promising research area for learning complex data patterns. However, most existing quantum feature maps employ fixed encoding strategies that do not explicitly consider the relationships among features within a dataset. In this study, we propose a Correlation Aware Quantum Feature Map (CAQFM) which integrates feature dependencies into the quantum encoding process. The proposed approach utilizes Pearson, Spearman, Kendall Tau, Mutual Information, and Distance Correlation measures to identify relationships among features. Dependencies exceeding a predefined threshold are incorporated into the quantum circuit through controlled quantum gates, enabling the construction of richer quantum representations that better reflect the underlying structure of the data.
  The proposed method is evaluated using a Variational Quantum Classifier (VQC) on three benchmark datasets, namely breast cancer diagnosis, credit default prediction, and student placement classification. Simulation results demonstrate that correlation based quantum encoding can improve classification performance compared to conventional encoding strategies. In particular, the Spearman and Kendall Tau based CAQFM variants achieved the highest predictive performance and consistently outperformed standard quantum feature maps. The findings indicate that incorporating dependency information from classical data into quantum feature maps facilitates the generation of more discriminative quantum representations and enhances the effectiveness of variational quantum classifiers.

## 任意维Tsirelson界的系统推导

**Original Title:** Systematic derivation of Tsirelson bounds in arbitrary dimensions

**Authors:** Lorenzo Coccia, Matteo Padovan, Giuseppe Vallone

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21626v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21626v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

贝尔非定域性和量子相关性界限（所谓的齐瑞尔森界限）的研究是量子信息科学和探索量子理论极限的基础。虽然量子位系统的量子界限已经得到了广泛的描述，但确定用多维量子状态和测量可获得的相关性的紧量子界限仍然是一个重大挑战。在这项工作中，我们提出了用平方和分解写成的二元Tsirelson和局部界的系统推导。使用这种方法，我们发现了新的界限，并恢复了量子位和qu$d$its的最大纠缠态的既定结果。


### Abstract

The study of Bell nonlocality and the bounds of quantum correlations, the so-called Tsirelson bounds, is fundamental to quantum information science and the exploration of the limits of quantum theory. While quantum bounds for qubit systems have been extensively characterized, determining tight quantum bounds for correlations attainable with high-dimensional quantum states and measurements remains a significant challenge. In this work, we propose a systematic derivation of bipartite Tsirelson and local bounds written in terms of sum-of-squares decompositions. Using this method, we discover novel bounds and recover established results for maximally entangled states of qubits and qu$d$its.

## 量子博弈的无信号值--操作符代数的视角

**Original Title:** No-signaling values of quantum games--an operator algebra perspective

**Authors:** Roy Araiza, Marius Junge, Carlos Palazuelos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21664v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21664v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

这项工作的目的是研究两个证明者量子博弈（即，具有量子输入和输出的游戏）从运算子代数和运算子空间的角度来看。我们通过用操作符空间类别中的张量规范来表达这些游戏价值的几个概念。本文的主要结果涉及这些游戏所谓的无信号值的描述，为此我们不仅提供了一个精确的操作符空间公式，而且还在这项研究与操作符代数中的一些问题之间建立了密切的联系。特别是，我们展示了如何将\cite{Ara}中给出的格罗滕迪克定理的最近反例理解为量子信息论结果的直接结果。我们还获得了两个证明者量子博弈的无信号值和量子值之间差距的新上限，改进了之前已知的最佳估计。


### Abstract

The aim of this work is to study two-prover quantum games (i.e., games with quantum inputs and outputs) from an operator-algebraic and operator-space point of view. We characterize several notions of the value of such games by formulating them in terms of tensor norms in the category of operator spaces. The main results of the paper concern the description of the so-called no-signalling value of these games, for which we not only provide a precise operator-space formulation, but also establish close connections between this study and some problems in operator algebras. In particular, we show how the recent counterexample to Grothendieck's theorem for operator spaces given in \cite{Ara} can be understood as a direct consequence of results in quantum information theory. We also obtain new upper bounds on the gap between the no-signalling value and the quantum value of two-prover quantum games, improving the best previously known estimates.

## 连续超辐射激光的不稳定性

**Original Title:** Instabilities of the continuous superradiant laser

**Authors:** Bruno Laburthe-Tolra, Martin Robert-de-Saint-Vincent, Benjamin Pasquiou

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21675v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21675v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们研究了超辐射激光的强度稳定性。我们的研究重点是处于电子激发状态的连续原子束穿过高精细度法布里-佩罗腔模式的架构，该架构已被提出为主动光学时钟的新架构。我们表明，这种超辐射激光可能会变得不稳定并发展出混乱行为。我们推导出这种不稳定性的分析准则，并发现只有当腔中的量子寿命明显短于原子寿命时，这种不稳定性才可能发生。该标准允许完善必要的参数，以运行超辐射激光器作为光域中的频率参考。特别是，我们指出了不稳定性对强度波动和激光线宽度的影响。另一方面，我们还指出，当超辐射激光处于不稳定状态时，可以成为研究混乱的有趣游乐场。在平均场水平上，存在与流体湍流相关的贝纳德不稳定性的直接映射;然而，与量子输出耦合和原子重新填充相关的量子涨落极大地改变了预期的行为。最后，我们指出在大原子数下存在规则的自脉冲机制。


### Abstract

We investigate the intensity stability of the superradiant laser. Our study focuses on the architecture where a continuous beam of atoms in an electronically excited state crosses the mode of a high-finesse Fabry-Perot cavity, which has been proposed as a new architecture of an active optical clock. We show that such superradiant laser can become unstable and develop chaotic behavior. We derive an analytical criterion for this instability and find that it may only occur when the lifetime of photons in the cavity is significantly shorter than the lifetime of atoms. This criterion allows for refining the necessary parameters to run a superradiant laser as a frequency reference in the optical domain. In particular, we point-out the consequences of the instability on intensity fluctuations and laser linewidth. On the other hand, we also point out that the superradiant laser, when in the unstable regime, can become an interesting playground for studying chaos. At the mean-field level, there is a direct mapping to the Bénard instability associated with fluid turbulence; however quantum fluctuations associated with photon out-coupling and atom re-filling substantially modify the expected behaviors. Finally, we point-out the existence of a regular self-pulsing regime at large atom numbers.

## 积分虚散射本征相揭示的异常点

**Original Title:** Exceptional Points revealed by the integrated imaginary scattering eigenphase

**Authors:** J. Colín-Gálvez, V. Domínguez-Rocha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21684v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21684v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们提出并分析证明，散射矩阵的本征相提供开放PT对称系统中异常点的直接、相敏特征。使用具有平衡收益和损失的一维PT对称量子二聚体，与连续体引线耦合，我们跟踪了整个PT精确到PT破断转变中散射本征相的演变。当接近异常点时，本征相的虚部发展出符号相反的局部结构，反映了散射本征模中收益/损失不对称的出现。我们引入积分虚散射本征相G（gamma），它将这些信息浓缩为单个实验可访问的纯量。G（gamma）在PT精确阶段小到可以忽略不计，并在异常点附近经历急剧转变--明显的拐点，然后饱和进入平台期。G（gamma）的拐点在gamma_{EP}之前，并与传输共振的最大幅度重合，这表明峰值收益/损失不对称性和本征态聚并由开放系统中的独立条件决定--这是它们有限耦合到连续体的直接指纹。由于分析完全在S矩阵水平上制定--而不参考任何特定的物理实现--因此结果普遍适用于波动系统，包括可进行相分辨测量的光学、声学和微波平台。


### Abstract

We propose and analytically demonstrate that the eigenphases of the scattering matrix provide direct, phase-sensitive signatures of exceptional points in open PT-symmetric systems. Using a one-dimensional PT-symmetric quantum dimer with balanced gain and loss, coupled to continuum leads, we track the evolution of the scattering eigenphases across the PT-exact to PT-broken transition. The imaginary parts of the eigenphases develop localized structures of opposite sign as the exceptional point is approached, reflecting the emergence of gain/loss asymmetry in the scattering eigenmodes. We introduce the integrated imaginary scattering eigenphase G(gamma), which condenses this information into a single experimentally accessible scalar. G(gamma) is negligibly small in the PT-exact phase and undergoes a sharp transition -- a pronounced inflection followed by saturation into a plateau -- near the exceptional point. The inflection point of G(gamma) precedes gamma_{EP} and coincides with the maximum amplitude of the transmission resonances, revealing that peak gain/loss asymmetry and eigenstate coalescence are governed by independent conditions in open systems -- a direct fingerprint of their finite coupling to the continuum. Because the analysis is formulated entirely at the level of the S-matrix -- without reference to any specific physical realization -- the results are universally applicable across wave systems, including photonic, acoustic, and microwave platforms where phase-resolved measurements are available.


---


## 用于概率错误消除和Clifford数据回归的随机操作窗口

**Original Title:** Finite-shot operating windows for probabilistic error cancellation and Clifford data regression

**Authors:** Vicenzo Scavino

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21686v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21686v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

有噪设备上的量子误差缓解不仅受到残余偏差的限制，还受到缓解程序本身引入的散粒噪音和校准误差的限制。我们推导出概率误差消除（AEC）、Clifford数据回归（CDR）的有限镜头均方误差边界，并且没有对有噪的保利可观测估计进行缓解。Exact FEC以准概率方差额外费用为代价消除了精确噪音反相下的目标偏差，而群体线性CDR可以具有较小的目标射击方差，但在训练和目标噪音响应不匹配时保留校准下限。这种竞争产生了一个有限的CDR主导操作窗口，其上端点扩展为$B_{\mathrm{FEC}=\mathrm{CDR}}（p）\propto 1/（δ_1 ' 2 p）$，其中$δ_1$是一阶CDR校准不匹配。我们进一步证明了目标响应投影定理，表明响应盲仿射CDR仅在目标噪音响应仿射在理想目标值中时才消除一阶偏差;否则非零投影误差给出了不可约的局部校准下限。相同的均方误差公式扩展到二阶校准、换值泡利·汉密尔顿方程、有限CDR训练镜头和残余FEC模型偏差。封闭形式的两量子位计算和QAOA模拟支持预测的无缓解、CDR主导和REC主导机制。


### Abstract

Quantum error mitigation on noisy devices is limited not only by residual bias but also by the shot noise and calibration errors introduced by the mitigation procedure itself. We derive finite-shot mean-square-error boundaries for probabilistic error cancellation (PEC), Clifford data regression (CDR), and no mitigation for noisy Pauli-observable estimates. Exact PEC removes the target bias under an exact noise inverse at the price of a quasi-probability variance overhead, whereas population linear CDR can have smaller target-shot variance but retains a calibration floor when the training and target noise responses do not match. This competition yields a finite CDR-dominant operating window whose upper endpoint scales as $B_{\mathrm{PEC}=\mathrm{CDR}}(p)\propto 1/(δ_1^2p)$, where $δ_1$ is the first-order CDR calibration mismatch. We further prove a target-response projection theorem showing that response-blind affine CDR removes the first-order bias only when the target noise response is affine in the ideal target value; otherwise a nonzero projection error gives an irreducible local calibration floor. The same mean-square-error formulation extends to second-order calibration, commuting Pauli Hamiltonians, finite CDR training shots, and residual PEC model bias. A closed-form two-qubit calculation and QAOA simulations support the predicted no-mitigation, CDR-dominant, and PEC-dominant regimes.

## 四波混合中通过Dirac梳展开的任意图像传播的连续变量模型

**Original Title:** Continuous-variable model for arbitrary image propagation via Dirac-comb expansion in Four-Wave Mixing

**Authors:** Fabián Ramírez-Pacheco, Andrea Basilio-Zárate, Hans Marin Florez, Pablo Solano, Carla Hermann-Avigliano

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21692v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21692v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

我们开发了一个受激四波混合（4 WM）的宏观连续变量模型，产生亮探测束和共规束的平均强度、方差和协方差的封闭形式表达，适用于泵和种子的任意横向轮廓。非线性相互作用强度的所有阶数。该模型使用泵场的Dirac梳状展开，使量子统计数据可从一组公式逐像素计算。在平面波极限下，我们恢复了对相不敏感的放大器结果。超过这个限制，形式主义明确地证明了早期实验中观察到的信息的空间路径：种子角谱被转移到双束强度，而平方抽运场的角谱被转移到探针和共轴之间的空间互相关。我们在协方差中描述了高保真图像传输的参数窗口，协方差由种子与泵腰围比和相互作用强度控制。我们的模型在一个分析框架中提供了对明亮强度或空间互相关中的非局部信息进行编码的实验的理论解释。


### Abstract

We develop a macroscopic continuous-variable model of stimulated four-wave mixing (4WM) yielding closed-form expressions for the mean intensity, variance, and covariance of bright probe and conjugate beams, valid for arbitrary transverse profiles of the pump and seed to all orders in the nonlinear interaction strength. The model uses a Dirac-comb expansion of the pump field, making the photon statistics computable pixel-by-pixel from one set of expressions. In the plane-wave limit, we recover the phase-insensitive amplifier results. Beyond this limit, the formalism explicitly demonstrates the spatial routing of information observed in earlier experiments: the seed angular spectrum is transferred to the twin-beam intensities, whereas the angular spectrum of the squared pump field is transferred to the spatial cross-correlation between the probe and conjugate. We characterize the parameter window of high-fidelity image transfer in the covariance, which is controlled by the seed-to-pump waist ratio and the interaction strength. Our model provides, in one analytical framework, a theoretical account of experiments encoding information in the bright intensities or non-locally in the spatial cross-correlations.

## NISQ时代网络攻击检测的变分量子分类器（VQC）评估

**Original Title:** Evaluation of Variational Quantum Classifiers (VQC) for Cyberattack Detection in the NISQ Era

**Authors:** Angelos Thomos, Theodore Andronikos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21715v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21715v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

本文研究了变分量子分类器（VQC）在有噪音的中间规模量子（NISQ）系统时代检测网络异常的有效性和结构限制。使用NSL-KDD数据集的官方20%研究子集，开发了一个具有24个参数可训练类比的4量子位分类器，利用幅度编码嵌入16个主成分。在该子集的固定分区上，该模型实现了88%的一致二进制分类准确率。对两种根本不同的优化器COBYLA和SPSA进行的比较评估发现，观察到的性能平台并不归因于收敛到局部最小值，我们将这一结果解释为与编码相关的表达性限制一致，而不是优化产物。与经典神经网络（具有四个节点的Tiny MLP，实现97%的准确率）的架构对等性比较强调了与数据过度压缩到受限量子状态相关的表达能力差距。该模型在跨越22个原始NSL-KDD攻击类别的类平衡集上进行训练，并在样本中进行评估，作为代表能力的探测：在此配置下，VQC仅达到9%的准确率，并在一小部分类上表现出退化模式崩溃。我们将这种行为解释为与量子概率空间中过度压缩引起的线性可分性的丧失一致，同时明确指出我们的实验没有将编码与模拟深度、优化器预算和测量解码方案隔离开来（请参阅局限性）。受这些观察和Cover定理的启发，我们概述了一种替代范式：具有角度编码的16量子位VQC，扩展了Hilbert空间表示，而不是依赖于激进的经典维度约简。


### Abstract

This paper investigates the effectiveness and structural limits of Variational Quantum Classifiers (VQC) for detecting network anomalies in the era of Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) systems. Using the official 20\% research subset of the NSL-KDD dataset, a 4-qubit classifier featuring a 24-parameter trainable ansatz was developed, utilizing amplitude encoding to embed 16 principal components. On a held-out partition of this subset, the model achieved a consistent binary-classification accuracy of 88\%. A comparative evaluation with two fundamentally different optimizers, COBYLA and SPSA, found that the observed performance plateau is not attributable to convergence to local minima, a result we interpret as consistent with an encoding-related expressibility limit rather than an optimization artifact. An architectural parity comparison with a classical neural network (a Tiny MLP with four nodes, achieving 97\% accuracy) highlighted the expressiveness gap associated with data overcompression into restricted quantum states. The model was trained on a class-balanced set spanning the 22 raw NSL-KDD attack categories and evaluated in-sample as a probe of representational capacity: under this configuration the VQC reached only 9\% accuracy and exhibited a degenerate mode collapse onto a small subset of classes. We interpret this behavior as consistent with the loss of linear separability induced by excessive compression in the quantum probability space, while explicitly noting that our experiments do not isolate the encoding from the ansatz depth, optimizer budget, and measurement-decoding scheme (see Limitations). Motivated by these observations and by Cover's theorem, we outline an alternative paradigm: a 16-qubit VQC with angle encoding that expands the Hilbert-space representation rather than relying on aggressive classical dimensionality reduction.


---


## 量子神经网络的中心极限定理和萨诺夫原理

**Original Title:** On a Central Limit Theorem and Sanov's principle for quantum neural networks

**Authors:** Anderson Melchor Hernandez

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21721v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21721v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们研究了由通过梯度流训练的量子神经网络生成的专家混合（MoE）的波动。我们的主要结果建立了中心极限定理（CLT）和Sanov关于MoE的原则，因为专家数量不同。我们证明，其参数的经验测量的波动接近其相应的极限概率测量，可以解决线性输运方程。作为副产品，我们表明MoE收敛于极限函数，该函数求解由与量子神经网络相关的神经切核支配的进化方程。


### Abstract

In this work, we study the fluctuations of a Mixture of Experts (MoE) generated by a quantum neural network trained via gradient flow on supervised learning problems. Our main results establish the Central Limit Theorem (CLT), and Sanov's principle for an MoE as the number of experts diverges. We demonstrate that the fluctuations of the empirical measure of its parameters close to its corresponding limit probability measure solve a linear transport equation. As a byproduct, we show that the MoE converges to a limit function which solves an evolution equation governed by the neural tangent kernel associated with the quantum neural network.

## 量子硬件上组织病理学癌症检测的可配置算法

**Original Title:** Configurable Algorithms for Histopathologic Cancer Detection on Quantum Hardware

**Authors:** Nandika Goyal, Glen Uehara, Andreas Spanias

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21752v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21752v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

由于组织变异性、染色差异和疾病类别之间微妙的视觉差异，组织病理学癌症检测具有挑战性。我们为这项任务提出了两种量子算法：一种可配置的双梯度CSWAP电路（DG-CSWAP），通过每像素本地Ry编码在单次执行中计算多方向边缘响应，以及一种硬件高效的破坏性交换电路（DG-DST），以低得多的电路复杂性本地匹配量子处理单元（QPU）门集。我们证明了DG-CSWAP和DG-DST之间的代数等效性，从而实现了双回路QPU验证策略。三阶段NISQ缓解流水线（包括读出误差纠正、偏差减法和斜坡回归）将单像素硬件SSE降低约8倍。该方法通过Amazon Braket在五个量子处理器上进行验证，在所有本地模拟器对上实现了平台间Pearson r ~ 0.93-0.94。与之前的基于量子傅里叶变换（QFT）的幅度编码基线需要12量子位全局状态准备和三模型系综（PatchCamelyon上的85.55%）相比，提出的方法使用基于镜头的测量，在真实的量子硬件上执行，并通过单个ResNet-50实现79.80%的准确率。Lite配置以2.59%的准确性成本提供17倍的预处理加速。据我们所知，这是第一个用于组织病理图像分类的具有降噪功能的量子硬件实施研究。


### Abstract

Histopathologic cancer detection is challenging due to tissue variability, staining differences, and subtle visual distinctions between disease classes. We propose two quantum algorithms for this task: a configurable dual-gradient CSWAP circuit (DG-CSWAP) that computes multi-directional edge responses in a single execution via per-pixel local Ry encoding, and a hardware-efficient destructive swap circuit (DG-DST) natively matched to quantum processing unit (QPU) gate sets at substantially lower circuit complexity. We prove algebraic equivalence between DG-CSWAP and DG-DST, enabling a two-circuit QPU validation strategy. A three-stage NISQ mitigation pipeline, including readout error correction, bias subtraction, and slope regression, reduces single-pixel hardware MSE by ~8x. Validated on five quantum processors via Amazon Braket, the method achieves inter-platform Pearson r ~ 0.93-0.94 across all local-simulator pairs. Compared to a prior Quantum Fourier Transform (QFT) based amplitude-encoding baseline requiring 12-qubit global state preparation and a three-model ensemble (85.55% on PatchCamelyon), the proposed method uses shot-based measurements, executes on real quantum hardware, and achieves 79.80% accuracy with a single ResNet-50. A Lite configuration delivers a 17x preprocessing speedup at a 2.59% accuracy cost. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first quantum hardware implementation study with noise mitigation for histopathologic image classification.

## 反馈控制的磁振子-原子纠缠和量子统计

**Original Title:** Feedback-Controlled Magnon-Atom Entanglement and Photon Statistics

**Authors:** Yiping Lu, Yulong Hu, Zhuzheng Han, Shirong Lin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21758v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21758v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

量子系统在实现精确控制方面面临着固有的挑战，而对于复杂的混合平台来说，求解薛定格方程通常很棘手。在这里，我们首次将磁振子引入反馈控制量子系统。为了以数字方式有效地解决动态问题，我们采用长短期记忆网络（一种机器学习方法）将概率幅度传播到稳态。通过应用相关反馈，我们有效地稳定了腔内状态。我们的结果表明，光-光相关函数和共生性（磁振子-原子纠缠的一种衡量标准）随着腔镜距离的变化而呈现出周期性振荡，并且当失调变化时，反馈显着增强反聚束和聚束。这些发现不仅展示了人工智能在量子动力学模拟中的力量，而且为混合磁子系统中的按需量子状态工程开辟了一条有前途的道路，并在量子网络和量子信息处理中具有潜在的应用。


### Abstract

Quantum systems face inherent challenges in achieving precise control, and solving the Schrödinger equation is often intractable for complex hybrid platforms. Here, for the first time, we introduce a magnon into a feedback-controlled quantum system. To solve the dynamics numerically and efficiently, we employ a Long Short-Term Memory network, a machine learning approach, to propagate the probability amplitudes to the steady state. By applying coherent feedback, we effectively stabilize the intracavity state. Our results reveal that the photon-photon correlation function and the concurrence, a measure of magnon-atom entanglement, exhibit periodic oscillations with the cavity-mirror distance, and that feedback significantly enhances both antibunching and bunching when the detuning is varied. These findings not only demonstrate the power of artificial intelligence in quantum dynamics simulation, but also open a promising route for on-demand quantum state engineering in hybrid magnonic systems, with potential applications in quantum networks and quantum information processing.

## 使用通用最优跟踪的动态脱钩

**Original Title:** Dynamical Decoupling using Universal Optimal Tracking

**Authors:** Amit Devra, Emanuel Malvetti, Niklas J. Glaser, Abhishek Agarwal, Ivan Rungger, Santana Lujan, Max Werninghaus, Stefan Filipp, Leo Van Damme, Steffen J. Glaser

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21762v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21762v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

动态去耦合（DD）是一种广泛使用且资源高效的错误抑制技术，但传统的DD依赖于周期性地重复短脉冲块以在空闲期间重新聚焦量子位状态。该块中的不完美会导致残余错误累积，最终在长时间空闲时间内降低状态恢复。在这里，我们引入了一种通用的最佳跟踪方法，该方法将原始跟踪概念扩展到用于设计DD序列的完全状态独立的设置。通过在优化期间监控量子位在预定义路点的演变，该方法动态补偿残余误差，同时保持定期重新聚焦。在超导量子位平台上进行的实验演示证实了静态控制不完善下误差积累的抑制，这与数值预测一致。补充模拟进一步表明，基于最佳跟踪的序列在时间相关的噪音下保持了强大的性能。这些结果将最佳跟踪确立为一种实用且硬件不可知的方法，用于设计适合有噪量子设备的短、鲁棒的DD序列。


### Abstract

Dynamical decoupling (DD) is a widely used and resource-efficient technique for error suppression, but conventional DD relies on periodically repeating a short pulse block to refocus the qubit state during idle periods. Imperfections in this block cause residual errors to accumulate, ultimately degrading state recovery over long idle times. Here, we introduce a universal optimal tracking approach that extends the original tracking concept to a fully state-independent setting for designing DD sequences. By monitoring the qubit's evolution at predefined waypoints during optimization, the method dynamically compensates residual errors while preserving regular refocusing. Experimental demonstrations on a superconducting-qubit platform confirm the suppression of error accumulation under static control imperfections, in agreement with numerical predictions. Complementary simulations further show that optimal-tracking-based sequences maintain strong performance under time-dependent noise. These results establish optimal tracking as a practical and hardware-agnostic approach to designing short, robust DD sequences suitable for noisy quantum devices.

## 量子相同粒子的常见原因

**Original Title:** Common causes for quantum identical particles

**Authors:** A. Hovhannisyan, S. Weigert, A. E. Allahverdyan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21768v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21768v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

违反贝尔不等式意味着两个（不相同）量子粒子上的非交换测量产生的联合概率没有单一的共同原因。但通过交换测量为此类不相同粒子生成的联合概率确实具有非平凡的共因变量。我们专注于交换测量并考虑两个相同的量子粒子，其密度矩阵和可观测量（埃尔米特操作员）必然是排列对称的。很自然地要求描述联合概率的共同原因也是排列对称的，即，它对称地作用于两个粒子。研究从相同测量数据定义联合概率的各种方法，我们得出的结论是，对称的共同原因不一定存在（即，粒子可以隐藏地区分），或者对称筛选变量存在，但它们是微不足道的，即，没有单一的共同原因可以解释所有单一测量相关性。


### Abstract

Violations of Bell's inequalities imply that joint probabilities generated by non-commutative measurements on two (non-identical) quantum particles do not have a single common cause. But joint probabilities generated for such non-identical particles via commutative measurements do have non-trivial common cause variables. We focus on commutative measurements and consider two identical quantum particles, whose density matrices and observables (hermitian operators) are necessarily permutation-symmetric. It is natural to demand that the common cause describing joint probabilities is also permutation symmetric, i.e., it acts symmetrically on both particles. Looking at various ways of defining joint probabilities from the same measurement data, we conclude that either symmetric common causes need not exist (i.e., that the particles can be hiddenly distinguishable), or that symmetric screening variables exist, but they are trivial, i.e., no single common cause can explain all single-measurement correlations.


---


## 具有周期和Dirichlet边界条件的一次量子化相对论量子模拟

**Original Title:** First-Quantized Relativistic Quantum Simulation with Periodic and Dirichlet Boundary Conditions

**Authors:** Jeongho Bang, Timothy P. Spiller, Kyunghyun Baek, Kyoungho Cho, Jaewoo Joo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21794v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21794v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们提出了一种在格子模型中最常用的两种边界条件下对一维有限域进行第一量子化相对论量子模拟的方法：周期性边界条件（TBC）和Dirichlet边界条件（DBC）。从正能量相对论动力学操作员开始，我们构造了弱相对论格子Hamilton体，其主要修正需要边界一致的离散动量矩$\langle \hat{P}' s\rangle$和$\langle \hat{P}' s\rangle$。这些矩是在TBC Hamilton量中根据正循环平移的矩重建的，而DBC Hamilton量则使用开链有限差。在量子位寄存器实现中，它可以被评估为相应的循环翻译估计器加上删除非物理环绕链接的边界本地项。由此产生的能量估计工作流程使用动力学项的平移测量，DBC的少量端点和近端点重叠概率，以及对角电位的位置基础采样。我们在各种基准势下验证了相对论量子模拟的框架，例如PBC的无势和余弦势以及DBC的无限方阱和谐波势，并进行了有限次抽样测试。这些基准显示出良好的估计重建和直接矩阵评估之间的协议，同时分离的有限网格离散化，弱相对论截断，和测量误差。


### Abstract

In this work, we present a methodology for first-quantized relativistic quantum simulation on one-dimensional finite domains under the two boundary conditions most commonly used in lattice models: periodic boundary conditions (PBC) and Dirichlet boundary conditions (DBC). Starting from the positive-energy relativistic kinetic operator, we construct weakly relativistic lattice Hamiltonians whose leading correction requires the boundary-consistent discretized momentum moments $\langle \hat{P}^{2}\rangle$ and $\langle \hat{P}^{4}\rangle$. These moments are reconstructed in the PBC Hamiltonian from moments of a unitary cyclic translation while the DBC Hamiltonian uses the open-chain finite-difference. In a qubit-register implementation, it can be evaluated as the corresponding cyclic translation estimator plus boundary-local terms that remove the unphysical wrap-around link. The resulting energy-estimation workflow uses translation measurements for the kinetic terms, a small number of endpoints and near-endpoints overlap probabilities for DBC, and position-basis sampling for diagonal potentials. We valdate the framework of the relativistic quantum simulation in various benchmark potentials such as no potential and a cosine potential for PBC as well as an infinite square well and a harmonic potential for DBC, with finite-shot sampling tests. These benchmarks show good agreement between the estimator reconstruction and direct matrix evaluation while separating the finite-grid discretization, weak-relativistic truncation, and measurement errors.
