## 一般违约强度模型的半分析定价

**Original Title:** Semi-Analytical Pricing for General Default Intensity Models

**Authors:** Ryan Parker, Mark Stedman, Luca Capriotti

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21800v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21800v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-19


### 摘要

使用路径积分形式主义，我们开发了一个准确的和易于计算的半解析近似的一般类的{默认强度}模型。我们说明了该方法的准确性，提出的Black-Karasinski模型的结果，所提出的近似提供了非常准确的结果，即使在制度的高波动性和多年的时间范围。所提出的近似的准确性和计算效率，使其成为一个可行的替代完全数值计划的各种应用在计量经济学和衍生品定价，包括计算信用产品的XVA。作为一个实例，我们考虑了在随机违约强度和外汇贬值模型下的一个量子信用违约互换（CDS）的定价问题。


### Abstract

Using the path-integral formalism, we develop an accurate and easy-to-compute semi-analytical approximation for a general class of {default intensity} models. We illustrate the accuracy of the method by presenting results for the Black-Karasinski model for which the proposed approximation provides remarkably accurate results, even in regimes of high volatility and multi-year time horizons. The accuracy and the computational efficiency of the proposed approximation makes it a viable alternative to fully numerical schemes for a variety of applications in econometrics and derivatives pricing, including the computation of XVA for credit products. As a practical example, we consider the pricing of a quanto Credit Default Swap (CDS) under stochastic intensity of default and an FX devaluation model.


---


## 多体量子激冷预热冷却

**Original Title:** Prethermal cooling with many-body quantum quenches

**Authors:** Jacob F. Steiner, Mohammad Hafezi, Stefan Kehrein, Gil Refael

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21813v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21813v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

多体量子猝灭通常与加热有关。在这项工作中，我们表明，如果猝灭能量沉积在长寿命的高能激发中，对系统进行正功的量子猝灭仍然可以导致低能量自由度的有效冷却。我们针对强耦合（U >> t）费米哈伯德模型中跳跃项t在半填充时的猝灭进行了明确讨论，其中猝灭会导致寿命非常长的非平衡双粒子密度。相关的预热状态持续的时间以（U/t）' 2为指数级大。在这个时间窗口期间，我们找到了有效预热温度，该温度降低了最终跳频幅度与初始跳频幅度之比相对于初始温度的平方。这表现为一种有效的波动-消散关系，该关系适用于双数保存操作员。在实际实施中，哈伯德系统充当制冷剂来冷却目标系统，前提是耦合器保留双倍数。我们的协议可以被认为是隔热退磁的量子激灭多体概括。


### Abstract

Many-body quantum quenches are typically associated with heating. In this work, we show that quantum quenches that perform positive work on the system can still lead to effective cooling of low-energy degrees of freedom if the quench energy is deposited in long-lived high-energy excitations. We discuss this explicitly for a quench of the hopping term t in the strong-coupling (U >> t) fermionic Hubbard model at half filling, where the quench induces a very long-lived non-equilibrium doublon density. The associated prethermal state persists for a time exponentially large in (U/t)^2. During this time window, we find an effective prethermal temperature that is reduced by the square of the ratio of final to initial hopping amplitude with respect to the initial temperature. This manifests as an effective fluctuation-dissipation relation that holds for doublon-number conserving operators. In a practical implementation the Hubbard system acts as a refrigerant to cool a target system provided the coupling conserves doublon number. Our protocol can be thought of as a quantum quench many-body generalization of adiabatic demagnetization.


---


## 纯量诱导引力波中的量子记忆

**Original Title:** Quantum Memory in Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves

**Authors:** Waqas Ahmed

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21835v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21835v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

纯量引起的引力波通常被视为由相随机弯曲扰动产生的经典随机背景。我们表明这种描述可能会错过剩余量子信息。从去量子化的双峰高斯纯量态出发，推导出纯量反常相关性与诱导张量模的协方差矩阵之间的显式传递关系。对于局部纯量功率谱来说，普通张量功率来自纯量功率压缩，而反模张量相干性来自纯量奇异相干压缩。即使在纯量纠缠消失之后，这种相干性也可以产生非零张量不和谐和连接张量-功率协方差。我们将相关协方差和相敏应变相关性确定为次级引力波背景中原始量子相关性的探测器，并讨论它们与未来空基干涉仪和脉冲星计时阵列可能的相关性。


### Abstract

Scalar-induced gravitational waves are usually treated as a classical stochastic background sourced by phase-random curvature perturbations. We show that this description can miss residual quantum information. Starting from a decohered two-mode Gaussian scalar state, we derive explicit transfer relations between the scalar anomalous coherence and the covariance matrix of induced tensor modes. For a localized scalar power spectrum, the ordinary tensor power is sourced by scalar power contractions, whereas the opposite-mode tensor coherence is sourced by scalar anomalous-coherence contractions. This coherence can generate nonzero tensor discord and a connected tensor-power covariance even after scalar entanglement has vanished. We identify the connected covariance and phase-sensitive strain correlations as probes of primordial quantum coherence in secondary gravitational-wave backgrounds, and discuss their possible relevance for future space-based interferometers and pulsar timing arrays.


---


## 量子极限环中的动态倾斜

**Original Title:** Dynamical Tipping in a Quantum Limit Cycle

**Authors:** Ya-Xin Xiang, Zhengyang Bai, Yu-Qiang Ma

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21849v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21849v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

非平衡系统通过能量消散和熵产生维持时空秩序。在这里，我们通过设计一个量子极限环来证明这一原理，该极限环是由一阶吸收状态相转变与耦合阶和控制参数的反馈机制之间的相互作用产生的。量子极限环体现了由乘性量子噪音和周期性穿越临界点驱动的动态相关性，这充当状态转变的鲁棒预警信号。这种周期性的交叉导致每次倾翻事件附近的动态敏感性增强和长期相关性的短暂上升，并随后从其中消失。这些关键转变伴随着能量消散率的急剧增加，导致动态信息量随着时间的推移逐步积累。我们的结果为在强相互作用的驱动-消散开放量子系统中实现动态涨落和远程相关性提供了一种方法。


### Abstract

Nonequilibrium systems maintain spatiotemporal order through energy dissipation and entropy production. Here, we demonstrate this principle by engineering a quantum limit cycle that emerges from the interplay between a first-order absorbing-state phase transition and feedback mechanism coupling order and control parameters. The quantum limit cycle manifests dynamical correlations driven by multiplicative quantum noise and periodic traverses through tipping points, which act as a robust early-warning signal for state transitions. This periodic crossing results in the enhanced dynamical susceptibility and transient rise of long-range correlations near each tipping event and their subsequent disappearance away from it. These critical transitions are accompanied by a sharp increase in the energy dissipation rate, leading to a stepwise accumulation of dynamical entropy production over time. Our results provide a way for realizing dynamical fluctuations and long-range correlations in strongly interacting driven-dissipative open quantum systems.


---


## 基于范德华材料的极化纠缠光对的单片和完全光纤兼容可调谐光源的演示

**Original Title:** Demonstration of a Monolithic and Fully Telecom-Fiber-Compatible Tunable Source of Polarization Entangled Photon Pairs Based on a van der Waals Material

**Authors:** Benjamin Laudert, Fatemeh Abtahi, Duk Choi, Dragomir Neshev, Falk Eilenberger

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21874v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21874v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们提出了一种用于近红外电信频段的可调、基于单一模式光纤的极化纠缠量子对源，可在标准基础设施中部署。通过自发参数下转换（SPDC）在位于两个光纤连接器之间的过渡金属二硫属化合物二硫代钼（3 R-MoS $_2$）的反型破缺斜方面体多型的亚微米级薄膜中产生。通过利用3R-MoS$_2$的二阶非线性极化率张量的固有对称性，这种混合方法通过输入泵极化来控制产生的双量子极化状态。最值得注意的是，可以产生四个最大纠缠贝尔状态中的两个，以及完全共极化对。这代表着比现有光纤集成光源在可调谐性和简单性方面的重大改进，后者需要额外的光学元件、精确的对准或精心设计的设计参数。此外，在低抽运功率下观察到3R-MoS$_2$背景光致发光信号的非线性下降，使我们能够达到$（8.3/pm1.8）\x10 #


### Abstract

We present a tunable, single-mode-optical-fiber-based source of polarization entangled photon pairs for the near-infrared telecommunication band that is deployable in standard infrastructure. The photon pairs are generated via spontaneous parametric down-conversion (SPDC) in a submicron-scale thin film of the inversion-broken rhombohedral polytype of the transition metal dichalcogenide molybdenum disulfide (3R-MoS$_2$), located between two fiber connectors. By exploiting the intrinsic symmetries of the second-order nonlinear susceptibility tensor of 3R-MoS$_2$, this hybrid approach offers control over the generated two-photon polarization state through the incident pump polarization. Most notably, two of the four maximally entangled Bell states, as well as fully co-polarized pairs can be produced. This represents a substantial improvement in terms of tunability and simplicity over established fiber-integrated sources, which require additional optical elements, precise alignment, or careful engineering of design parameters. Additionally, a nonlinear drop in the background photoluminescence signal of 3R-MoS$_2$ is observed at low pump powers, allowing us to reach a coincidences-to-accidentals ratio (CAR) of $(8.3\pm1.8)\times10^{3}$, the highest value recorded for SPDC in van der Waals materials to date.

## 在具有T形结的二维分段离子陷阱量子处理器中穿梭

**Original Title:** Shuttling in Bidimensional Segmented Ion-Trap Quantum Processors with T-Junctions

**Authors:** J. Durandau, C. A. Brunet, F. Schmidt-Kaler, U. Poschinger, F. Mailhot, Y. Bérubé-Lauzière

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21899v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21899v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

基于航天飞机的俘获离子量子处理器通常采用一维（1D）线性架构来在实施量子门的一个或多个激光相互作用区以及几个量子位寄存器存储段之间传输离子量子位。二维（2D）量子CCD架构还采用T或X结以提高缩放率和效率。在这里，我们探索了此类架构中量子算法典型构建块的编译中的穿梭层。为了权衡线性穿梭机和枢纽穿梭机的工作量，我们为每次操作引入了单独的成本函数。这允许比较量子电路构建块的总成本，例如QFT，进位，加法器，移位和比较器电路。我们研究了它们随量子比特数增加的标度特性。在相同的运输成本的结和线性穿梭，我们表明，2D架构优于1D线性陷阱的比例提高离子的数量增加。最后，我们讨论使用的细胞，这样整个处理器是从一个二维阵列的这种互连的细胞。该工作旨在优化量子处理器架构，实施适合特定任务的协同设计，并以航天飞机高效的方式进行扩展。


### Abstract

Shuttle-based trapped ion quantum processors typically employ a one-dimensional (1D) linear architecture to transport ion-qubits between one ore more laser interaction zones where the quantum gates are implemented, along with several qubit register storage segments. The two-dimensional (2D) quantum CCD architecture employs also T- or X-junctions for an improved scaling and efficiency. Here, we explore the shuttling layer in the compilation of quantum algorithm typical building blocks in such architecture. To weight the effort of linear shuttle and junction shuttle, we introduce individual cost functions for each operation. This allows comparing the total cost for quantum circuit building blocks such as the QFT, Carry, Adder, Shift, and Comparator circuits. We study their scaling properties with increased qubit numbers. At equivalent transport cost for junction and linear shuttling, we show that 2D architectures outperform the 1D linear trap with the ratio improving as the number of ions increases. Finally, we discuss the use of cells, such that the entire processor is constructed from a 2D array of such interconnected cells. The work aims to optimize quantum processor architectures, implementing a co-design that fits to the specific task and scaling up in a shuttle-efficient way.

## 纯量诱导引力波中的纠缠、不和谐和剩余相关性

**Original Title:** Entanglement, Discord, and Residual Coherence in Scalar-Induced Gravitational Waves

**Authors:** Waqas Ahmed

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21901v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21901v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

纯量引起的引力波通常被建模为源自原始弯曲扰动的经典随机背景。我们研究纯量扇形的剩余量子信息属性是否能够经受退相干并在诱导张量背景中留下印记。使用协方差矩阵形式主义，我们将原始弯曲扰动描述为去量子化的双峰压缩高斯态，并识别出在纯量纠缠消失后可能保留的异常纯量相干性。然后，我们推导出反向动量诱导张量模式的主要量到张量传输关系。普通张量功率来自纯量功率压缩，而反模张量相干性来自异常纯量相干压缩。这种张量相关性控制诱导的高斯不和谐并生成连接的和相敏的可观测量，包括连接的功率协方差$k（k）\propto| γ_k| ' 2/a_k ' 2 $。因此，稳健的特征并不是引力波谱的普遍漂移，而是具有非平凡协方差和相结构的相关张量背景。我们讨论现象学模板，并为未来的引力波观测提供说明性的费舍尔估计。我们的结果表明，纯量诱导的引力波可能会为纠缠之外的原始量子相关性提供新的探索。


### Abstract

Scalar-induced gravitational waves are usually modeled as a classical stochastic background sourced by primordial curvature perturbations. We investigate whether residual quantum-information properties of the scalar sector can survive decoherence and leave imprints in the induced tensor background. Using the covariance-matrix formalism, we describe primordial curvature perturbations as decohered two-mode squeezed Gaussian states and identify the anomalous scalar coherence that may remain after scalar entanglement has vanished. We then derive the leading scalar-to-tensor transfer relations for opposite-momentum induced tensor modes. The ordinary tensor power is sourced by scalar power contractions, whereas the opposite-mode tensor coherence is sourced by anomalous scalar-coherence contractions. This tensor coherence controls the induced Gaussian discord and generates connected and phase-sensitive observables, including a connected power covariance $κ(k)\propto |γ_k|^2/α_k^2$. Thus the robust signature is not a universal shift of the gravitational-wave spectrum, but a correlated tensor background with nontrivial covariance and phase structure. We discuss phenomenological templates and provide an illustrative Fisher estimate for future gravitational-wave observations. Our results suggest that scalar-induced gravitational waves may offer a new probe of primordial quantum correlations beyond entanglement.


---


## 通过最小纠缠下降量化和探索多方纠缠

**Original Title:** Quantifying and Probing Multipartite Entanglement via Minimum Entanglement Drop

**Authors:** Dong-Dong Dong, Xue-Ke Song, Liu Ye, Dong Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21950v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21950v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

量化真正的多方纠缠仍然是一个重大挑战。我们提出了一种由最小纠缠降定义的多方纠缠单调--追踪单个粒子时全球一对群纠缠的减少。我们使用纠缠和负性制定了一个计算高效的变体，以确保W类状态的非零值，并严格证明它在局部操作和经典通信下是有效的单调。在三方机制中，最小的纠缠下降在物理上相当于最小的成对并发性。我们建立了一个操作框架，其中纠缠滴充当结构探测器：通过评估对量子位丢失的敏感性，它识别出不可分割的集群，提取唯一区分同一本地Clifford等效类内的图布局的连接性指纹。将这种映射与经典阴影集成可以实现对纠缠网络演变的高效实验估计和动态跟踪。我们推导出环境噪音下n量子位W状态的精确分析解，揭示了鲁棒的标度行为。最后，我们承认其局限性，并指出对于高度稳健的状态（例如5量子位错误纠正代码），诊断灵敏度严格消失。


### Abstract

Quantifying genuine multipartite entanglement remains a significant challenge. We propose a multipartite entanglement monotone defined by the minimum entanglement drop -- the reduction in global one-to-group entanglement upon tracing out a single particle. We formulate a computationally efficient variant using tangle and negativity to ensure non-vanishing values for W-class states, and rigorously prove it is a valid monotone under local operations and classical communication. In the tripartite regime, the minimum tangle drop is physically equivalent to the minimum pairwise concurrence. We establish an operational framework where the entanglement drop acts as a structural probe: by assessing sensitivity to qubit loss, it identifies inseparable clusters, extracting connectivity fingerprints that uniquely differentiate graph topologies within the same local Clifford equivalence class. Integrating this mapping with classical shadows enables efficient experimental estimation and dynamic tracking of entanglement network evolution. We derive exact analytical solutions for n-qubit W states under environmental noise, revealing robust scaling behaviors. Finally, we acknowledge limitations, noting that diagnostic sensitivity strictly vanishes for highly robust states such as the 5-qubit error-correcting code.


---


## 利用量子时间晶体加速自由电子

**Original Title:** Acceleration of Free Electrons by Photonic Time-Crystals

**Authors:** Lior Bar-Hillel, Alexey Gorlach, Ido Kaminer, Mordechai Segev

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21953v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21953v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们研究了时变媒体中自由电子和量子之间的量子相互作用，发现周期性调制指数级放大了动量间隙内的电子-量子耦合，从而实现任意大的动量转移。通过在双模压缩真空状态下制备光，电子动量的增长速度快于其光谱扩展，从而建立了时间调制的光媒体作为加速自由电子并塑造其量子状态的平台。


### Abstract

We study the quantum interaction between free electrons and photons in a time-varying media, and find that periodic modulation exponentially amplifies electron-photon coupling within momentum gaps, enabling arbitrarily large momentum transfer. By preparing the light in a two-mode squeezed vacuum state, the electron momentum grows faster than its spectral spreading, establishing time-modulated photonic media as a platform for accelerating free-electrons and shaping their quantum state.

## 通过对称平均虚拟蒸馏抑制量子误差

**Original Title:** Quantum Error Suppression via Symmetry-Averaged Virtual Distillation

**Authors:** Canyu He, Chunhua Zeng, Ruyu Yang, Yongdan Yang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21962v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21962v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

可靠的量子模拟受到算法近似和硬件噪声的限制，这两种噪声通常共存于近期和早期容错量子器件的输出中。现有的错误抑制策略通常分别针对这些错误源。在这里，我们介绍了对称平均虚拟蒸馏（SAVD），一个错误抑制协议，适用于对称平均虚拟蒸馏之前，并在密度矩阵的水平上对待这两个缺陷。该协议构造了一个平均输出合奏的平均标记的实现，离开的平均不变的目标贡献不变，而平均残留成分的平均相关分支。然后将虚蒸馏（VD）应用于这个平均系综，而不是原始输出状态，以放大其主要特征分量。我们分析了由此产生的光谱抑制机制，并确定了对称平均作为VD状态预处理层的作用。各向同性海森堡链的数值演示表明，在存在一致算法错误和硬件噪音的情况下，准确性得到了提高。我们的结果提供了一种通用的基于虚拟的架构来增强量子模拟。


### Abstract

Reliable quantum simulation is limited by both algorithmic approximations and hardware noise, which usually coexist in the output of near-term and early fault-tolerant quantum devices. Existing error-suppression strategies often target these error sources separately. Here, we introduce symmetry-averaged virtual distillation (SAVD), an error-suppression protocol that applies symmetry averaging before virtual distillation and treats both imperfections at the density-matrix level. The protocol constructs a symmetry-averaged output ensemble from symmetry-labeled implementations, leaving the symmetry-invariant target contribution unchanged while averaging residual components over symmetry-related branches. Virtual distillation (VD) is then applied to this averaged ensemble, rather than to the raw output state, to amplify its dominant eigencomponent. We analyze the resulting spectral suppression mechanism and identify the role of symmetry averaging as a state-preconditioning layer for VD. Numerical demonstrations on an isotropic Heisenberg chain show improved accuracy in the presence of both coherent algorithmic errors and hardware noise. Our results provide a general symmetry-based architecture for enhancing quantum simulations.


---


## 用于量子推理的微调大型语言模型

**Original Title:** Fine-Tuning Large Language Models for Quantum Reasoning

**Authors:** Katherine Ip, Casey R. Myers, Udaya Parampalli, James Quach, Peiyong Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21974v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21974v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

大型语言模型（LLM）展现出超出自然语言建模和文本生成的能力。其推理能力的最新进展激发了人们对将LLM应用于需要深层领域专业知识和复杂推理的复杂科学任务的兴趣。量子计算作为一个具有严重知识障碍和硬件限制的高度专业化领域，可以从这些进步中受益匪浅。然而，首先必须回答的一个关键悬而未决的问题是：我们如何开发微调管道，在LLM中灌输真正的量子推理，而不是特定任务的模式匹配？我们通过量子电路模拟作为训练目标来研究这个问题，其中模型必须预测量子门操作序列产生的测量概率分布。我们提出并比较了两种微调管道：（1）基于显式逐门状态载体模拟轨迹的监督微调（SFT），以及（2）两阶段SFT+群组相对政策优化（GRPO）方法，该方法顺序应用SFT，然后应用GRPO，并具有可验证的奖励。我们的研究结果表明，SFT实现了近乎完美的内分布和门数外推准确性，显着优于基本模型和GPT-OSS-120 B基线。SFT+GRPO牺牲了一定的分布精度，以更好地推广到SFT单独无法处理的更大量子位系统。这两个管道的表现都显着优于基线，这表明对显式推理轨迹进行有针对性的微调是推进LLM量子推理的有效策略。


### Abstract

Large language models (LLMs) exhibit abilities beyond natural language modelling and text generation. Recent advances in their reasoning capabilities have spurred interest in applying LLMs to complex scientific tasks requiring deep domain expertise and sophisticated reasoning. Quantum computing, as a highly specialised field with significant knowledge barriers and hardware constraints, could greatly benefit from such advancements. However, a key open question that first must be answered is: How can we develop fine-tuning pipelines that instil genuine quantum reasoning in LLMs, rather than task-specific pattern matching? We study this question through quantum circuit simulation as a training objective, where the model must predict the measurement probability distribution resulting from a sequence of quantum gate operations. We propose and compare two fine-tuning pipelines: (1) Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) on explicit gate-by-gate state-vector simulation traces, and (2) a two-stage SFT+Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) approach that sequentially applies SFT followed by GRPO with verifiable rewards. Our findings show that SFT achieves near-perfect in-distribution and gate-count extrapolation accuracy, significantly outperforming both the base model and the GPT-OSS-120B baseline. SFT+GRPO trades some in-distribution precision for better generalisation to larger qubit systems that SFT alone cannot handle. Both pipelines significantly outperform the baselines, demonstrating that targeted fine-tuning on explicit reasoning traces is an effective strategy for advancing quantum reasoning in LLMs.


---


## 通过能带布局工程对SrRuO 3中的拓扑输运的磁离子控制

**Original Title:** Magneto-ionic control of topological transport in SrRuO3 via band topology engineering

**Authors:** Xuanchi Zhou, Xiaohui Yao, Xiaomei Qiao, Guowei Zhou, Wenjing Huo, Shuang Li, Huihui Ji, Xiaohong Xu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.21999v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.21999v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

铁磁性体中的旋转轨道耦合（SOC）和非平凡能带布局之间的相互作用产生了丰富的地形输运现象，例如反常霍尔效应（AHE）和拓扑霍尔效应（THE）。现代旋转电子学的一个核心目标是以可逆的方式实现对拓扑输运现象的主动控制，而明确地理清THE和AHE对净霍尔效应的各自贡献仍然是一个艰巨的挑战。在这里，我们建立了磁离子控制，作为在具有相当大SOC和流动铁磁性的4d轨道SrRuO 3系统中动态工程布局输运的强大范式。利用可控质子化或氧空位掺入，通过能带填充控制实现费米能相对于避免的能带交叉的上移，从而产生可调的AHE电极反转温度。特别值得注意的是，通过广泛的离子掺杂出现了像驼峰一样的霍尔异常，无论AHE电极如何，这种现象都可以可逆地切换，为THE信号由破坏的反相对称性而不是双通道AHE驱动提供了证据。我们的研究结果为Berry弯曲工程提供了一个可行的调谐旋钮，能够按需控制强SOC铁磁性体中的拓扑输运，用于低功率、可重新配置的全氧化物旋电子器件。


### Abstract

The interplay between spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and nontrivial band topology in ferromagnets gives rise to a rich landscape of topological transport phenomena such as anomalous Hall effect (AHE) and topological Hall effect (THE). One central goal in modern spintronics lies in the realization of the active control over topological transport phenomena in a reversible fashion, while unambiguously disentangling respective contributions of THE and AHE to the net Hall effect remains a formidable challenge. Here we establish magneto ionic control as a powerful paradigm for dynamically engineering topological transports in a 4d-orbital SrRuO3 system with sizable SOC and itinerant ferromagnetism. Harnessing controllable protonation or oxygen vacancy incorporation, the Fermi-level upshift relative to avoided band crossings are realized through band filling control, giving rise to tunable reversal temperature of AHE polarity. Of particular note is the emergence of hump like Hall anomalies through extensive ionic doping that can be reversibly switched, irrespective of AHE polarity, providing evidence for a THE signal driven by broken inversion symmetry rather than a two channel AHE. Our findings provide a viable tuning knob for Berry curvature engineering, enabling on demand control of topological transports in strong SOC ferromagnets for low power, reconfigurable all oxide spintronic devices.

## 探测器级Gerium作为Indium受体旋转量子比特的低无序宿主：五量子比特材料到架构设计研究

**Original Title:** Detector-Grade Germanium as a Low-Disorder Host for Indium-Acceptor Spin Qubits: A Five-Qubit Materials-to-Architecture Design Study

**Authors:** D. -M. Mei, K. -M. Dong, S. A. Panamaldeniya, N. Budhathoki, S. Chhetri, A. Prem, S. Bhattarai

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22067v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22067v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

砷（Gee）中的受体束缚黑洞旋转为半导体量子信息处理提供了一条有希望但探索不足的途径。我们提出了一项基于在超高纯度Gee中有意引入的In（In）受体的探测器级Gee受体-旋转平台的理论指导设计研究。提出的材料策略将接近$10 ' x 10 ' m ' m的目标In密度结合在一起，相当于约170纳米的受体间距。具有合适横模体积的1 μ m长的活性通道平均可以包含约5个受体，从而实现统计选择的制造后寄存器，而不是确定性放置的链。我们分析了物理基础、设备架构、应变和无序限制、耦合层次结构、建模工作流程、制造路径和扩展前景。我们的结果表明，检测器级的Gee可以将不受控制的体静电和应变无序抑制到与受体-洞量子位兼容的水平，而旋转轨道活跃的价带集合体支持全电控制和偶极或音素介导的耦合。直接交换被视为紧对或门增强相互作用，而不是一般的平均间距耦合。音素晶体工程被确定为第二阶段增强，用于在基线控制、读出和最近邻耦合得到验证后抑制不需要的声学模式并实现选定的腔介导相互作用。剩余的挑战包括统计受体放置、界面无序、电荷噪音、读出集成和实验验证。这项工作将检测器级Gee In受体量子位确定为基于供体的杂质量子位和完全门定义的Gee洞旋转硬件之间的可靠中间架构。


### Abstract

Acceptor-bound hole spins in germanium (Ge) offer a promising but underexplored route to semiconductor quantum information processing. We present a theory-guided design study of a detector-grade Ge acceptor-spin platform based on intentionally incorporated indium (In) acceptors in ultra-high-purity Ge. The proposed materials strategy combines a residual impurity background near $10^{10} \mathrm{cm^{-3}}$ with a target In density of approximately $2\times10^{14} \mathrm{cm^{-3}}$, corresponding to an acceptor spacing of about 170 nanometer. A 1 $μ$m-long active channel with a suitable transverse mode volume can contain about five acceptors on average, enabling a statistically selected post-fabrication register rather than a deterministically placed chain. We analyze the physical basis, device architecture, strain and disorder limits, coupling hierarchy, modeling workflow, fabrication pathway, and scaling prospects. Our results indicate that detector-grade Ge can suppress uncontrolled bulk electrostatic and strain disorder to levels compatible with acceptor-hole qubits, while the spin--orbit-active valence-band manifold supports all-electrical control and dipolar or phonon-mediated coupling. Direct exchange is treated as a close-pair or gate-enhanced interaction rather than the generic mean-spacing coupling. Phononic crystal engineering is identified as a second-stage enhancement for suppressing unwanted acoustic modes and enabling selected cavity-mediated interactions after baseline control, readout, and nearest-neighbor coupling are validated. Remaining challenges include statistical acceptor placement, interface disorder, charge noise, readout integration, and experimental validation. This work identifies detector-grade Ge In-acceptor qubits as a credible intermediate architecture between donor-based impurity qubits and fully gate-defined Ge hole-spin hardware.

## 使用cQED编码的迭代量子相估计

**Original Title:** Iterative quantum phase estimation with cQED encoding

**Authors:** Changchun Zhong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22071v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22071v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

量子相估计是以海森堡有限精度确定正运算符或Hamilton体本征值的基石算法。传统的实现依赖于深度受控么正运算以及逆量子傅里叶变换，从而导致相当大的电路深度和硬件负担。在这里，我们提出了一种概念上简单且实验上可行的替代方案，该替代方案利用了电路量子电动力学的工具箱。该协议通过一系列二进制阈值测试来提取相，从而消除了对量子傅里叶逆变换的需要。玻色子模式充当高效的量子存储器，其中相的二进制数字被编码到相空间旋转的方向。然后通过高保真零差测量顺序读出这些数字。我们表明，该协议在估计精度方面实现了海森堡缩放，同时提供指数级抑制的失败概率。通过用玻色子自由度取代辅助电路，该方案显着降低了硬件复杂性，并提供了在电路量子电动力学平台上实施高精度量子相估计的实用途径。


### Abstract

Quantum phase estimation is a cornerstone algorithm for determining eigenvalues of unitary operators or Hamiltonians with Heisenberg-limited precision. Conventional implementations rely on deep controlled-unitary operations together with an inverse quantum Fourier transform, resulting in substantial circuit depth and hardware overhead. Here, we propose a conceptually simple and experimentally feasible alternative that exploits the toolbox of circuit quantum electrodynamics. The protocol extracts the phase through a sequence of binary threshold tests, eliminating the need for an inverse quantum Fourier transform. A bosonic mode serves as an efficient quantum memory in which the binary digits of the phase are encoded into the direction of phase-space rotations. These digits are then read out sequentially via high-fidelity homodyne measurements. We show that the protocol achieves Heisenberg scaling in estimation precision while simultaneously providing exponentially suppressed failure probability. By replacing the ancillary circuit with a bosonic degree of freedom, the scheme significantly reduces hardware complexity and offers a practical route toward implementing high-precision quantum phase estimation on circuit quantum electrodynamics platforms.


---


## 优化参数放大器的抽运条件以快速多路读出导体量子位

**Original Title:** Optimizing Pump Conditions of Parametric Amplifiers for Fast Multiplexed Readout of Superconducting Qubits

**Authors:** Jeongwon Kim, Wei Dai, Omrie Ovdat, Akiva Feintuch, Nir Alfasi, Yonuk Chong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22080v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22080v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

低噪音参数放大器被广泛用作量子位读出链中的第一级放大器。参数放大器的性能敏感地取决于泵条件的选择。我们提出了一种用于确定泵条件的策略，该策略专为快速多路传输读出量身定制。选择放大器泵以最大限度地提高极限量子位（需要最长的读出时间才能达到目标SNR的量子位）的读出频率处的信噪比（SNR）改善可以最大限度地减少总的多路传输读出时间。我们在带有行波参数放大器的五量子位多路传输读出链上通过实验展示了我们的泵校准策略。使用我们的策略，与优化所有量子位的平均SNR改进相比，我们将多路传输读出时间减少了320 ns，而不会降低任何量子位的目标SNR。


### Abstract

Low-noise parametric amplifiers are widely used as the first-stage amplifier in qubit readout chains. The performance of parametric amplifiers depends sensitively on the choice of the pump condition. We propose a strategy for determining the pump condition that is tailored for fast multiplexed readout. Choosing the amplifier pump to maximize the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) improvement at the readout frequency of the limiting qubit--the qubit that requires the longest readout time to reach a target SNR--minimizes the total multiplexed readout time. We demonstrate our pump calibration strategy experimentally on a five-qubit multiplexed readout chain with a traveling-wave parametric amplifier. Using our strategy, we reduce the multiplexed readout time by 320 ns compared to optimizing the average SNR improvement on all qubits, without degrading the target SNR for any qubit.

## 一致激子-音素-质子动力学中的瞬时信息划分

**Original Title:** Transient Information Partition in Coherent Exciton-Phonon-Photon Dynamics

**Authors:** Kunio Ishida

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22099v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22099v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们利用子系统分辨量子互信息（QMI）研究了相干激子-音素-量子系统中的瞬时信息划分。通过采用具有激子、音素和光自由度的模型，我们分析了$J$-$v $平面中的动力学，其中$J$描述激子脱域，$v $表示激子-音素耦合强度。通过比较时间平均QMI图与吸收的量子数，我们表明光活性本身并不能决定光致瞬时状态的特征。以激子为中心的信息分区识别了类极化子和类极化子瞬时响应之间的广泛交叉，具体取决于激子信息是主要与量子系统共享。相比之下，以音素为中心的分区在零激子和一激子接地区之间的边界附近揭示了一个更尖锐的邻近边界的再分布岭。该山脊在接地状态扇形图和光吸收图中都没有，这表明它既不是静态扇形边界，也不是光吸收的增强。变分强度函数分析将脊连接到类似II区的有限能极化子激发，其主要光谱权重位于单音素能量附近，因此脊代表了隐藏的瞬时相关结构，其中有限数量的音素相关信息在主要分配给激子-音素修饰之前优先与子系统共享。这些结果表明，基于QMI的信息划分提供了一个基于相关性的框架来描述相干光诱导的瞬时状态，其中光学和材料自由度共同参与量子力学。


### Abstract

We study transient information partition in a coherent exciton-phonon-photon system using subsystem-resolved quantum mutual information (QMI). By employing a model with excitonic, phononic, and photonic degrees of freedom, we analyze the dynamics in the $J$-$ν$ plane, where $J$ characterizes excitonic delocalization and $ν$ denotes the exciton-phonon coupling strength. By comparing time-averaged QMI maps with the absorbed photon number, we show that optical activity alone does not determine the character of the light-induced transient state. The exciton-centered information partition identifies a broad crossover between polariton-like and polaron-like transient responses, depending on whether excitonic information is mainly shared with the photon or phonon subsystem. In contrast, the phonon-centered partition reveals a sharper boundary-adjacent redistribution ridge near the boundary between the zero- and one-exciton ground-state sectors. This ridge is absent from both the ground-state sector map and the photon-absorption map, indicating that it is neither a static sector boundary nor an enhancement of optical absorption. A variational strength-function analysis connects the ridge to a region-II-like finite-energy polaronic excitation whose dominant spectral weight lies near the one-phonon energy, and thus the ridge represents a hidden transient correlation structure in which a limited amount of phonon-related information is preferentially shared with the photon subsystem before being predominantly allocated to exciton-phonon dressing. These results show that QMI-based information partition provides a correlation-based framework for characterizing coherent light-induced transient states in which optical and material degrees of freedom jointly participate quantum mechanically.


---


## 具有自伴随变形动量的超对称量子系统的光谱和热力学性质

**Original Title:** Spectral and thermodynamic properties of supersymmetric quantum systems with self-adjoint deformed momentum

**Authors:** J. A. Oke, F. A. Dossa

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22107v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22107v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们通过广义扩展动量操作符（GEMO）形式主义构造严格自伴随变形动量操作符，为具有几何变形的量子系统建立了严格的框架。与以前依赖边界条件Hermitability的方法不同，我们的方法确保了统一非Hermitian超对称因式分解方案内线性（$μ（x）= a x$）和二次（$μ（x）= a x #）变形的内在自伴随性。这产生了精确的分析光谱，同时揭示了隐藏的$\mathfrak{su}（1，1）$对称结构。至关重要的是，我们通过欧拉-麦克劳林逼近分析评估配分函数，提供了此类系统的第一个完整热力学描述。几何变形从根本上重塑了状态密度$p（E）$，产生了不同的热特征：由于最大能量附近的状态积累导致线性变形的分歧热容量峰值，以及二次变形的饱和$C/k_{\mathrm{B}}\至0.6$（低于Dulong-Petit极限）。这些结果确立了几何变形作为弯曲纳米结构中工程量子热力学响应的可调参数。


### Abstract

We establish a rigorous framework for quantum systems with geometric deformations by constructing a strictly self-adjoint deformed momentum operator through the generalized extended momentum operator (GEMO) formalism. Unlike previous approaches relying on boundary-condition hermiticity, our method ensures intrinsic self-adjointness for both linear ($μ(x)=αx$) and quadratic ($μ(x)=αx^{2}$) deformations within a unified non-Hermitian supersymmetric factorization scheme. This yields exact analytical spectra while revealing hidden $\mathfrak{su}(1,1)$ symmetry structures. Crucially, we provide the first complete thermodynamic characterization of such systems by analytically evaluating the partition function via the Euler--Maclaurin approximation. Geometric deformation fundamentally reshapes the density of states $ρ(E)$, producing distinct thermal signatures: a divergent heat capacity peak for linear deformation due to state accumulation near a maximal energy, and a saturation $C/k_{\mathrm{B}}\to 0.6$ (below the Dulong--Petit limit) for quadratic deformation. These results establish geometric deformation as a tunable parameter for engineering quantum thermodynamic responses in curved nanostructures.

## 关系量子因果过程中马尔科夫粗粒化布尔事实的出现

**Original Title:** Emergence of Boolean Facts from Markovian Coarse-Graining in Relational Quantum Causal Processes

**Authors:** Yipeng Xu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22127v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22127v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们制定了一种运算子代数机制，通过该机制，精确的布尔记录可以从局部完全正的量子运算中产生，而无需作为微观结构强加。运动学输入是一个代数过程函数，将概率分配给有限操作上下文中的局部正常完全正操作。从目标代数对源干预的先验反应，相对于背景策略类，我们定义了影响代数;根据定义，确切的事件就是其中心的投影。动态问题是非平凡中心是否可以通过粗粒化而不是通过分裂记录实验室插入。我们使用状态保持正常单位完全正粗粒度通道来解决这个问题。如果这样的通道的Cesaro平均收敛到Choi-Effros红外范围，并且该范围在GNS插值中是渐进阿贝尔的，那么所代表的红外代数是交换冯诺伊曼代数。因此，它的投影格是一个完全布尔代数。我们还给出了一个受局部性和扰乱驱动的有限部门块原始准则，这意味着这种渐进绝对性，并对部门外的内性和部门内的波动进行指数抑制。结果是一个保守的数学陈述：经典事实不是用III型局部代数的任意投影来识别的，而是用渐进阿贝尔完全正红外极限选择的中心投影来识别的。


### Abstract

We formulate an operator-algebraic mechanism by which exact Boolean records can arise from local completely positive quantum operations without being imposed as microscopic structure. The kinematic input is an algebraic process functional assigning probabilities to local normal completely positive operations in a finite operational context. From the predual response of a target algebra to source interventions, relative to a background strategy class, we define an influence algebra; exact events are then, by definition, the projections in its center. The dynamical question is whether nontrivial centers can be generated by coarse-graining rather than inserted through split-record laboratories. We address this question using state-preserving normal unital completely positive coarse-graining channels. If the Cesaro means of such a channel converge to a Choi-Effros infrared range and the range is asymptotically abelian in the GNS seminorm, then the represented infrared algebra is a commutative von Neumann algebra. Its projection lattice is therefore a complete Boolean algebra. We also give a finite-sector block-primitive criterion, motivated by locality and scrambling, which implies this asymptotic abelianness with exponential suppression of off-sector coherences and intra-sector fluctuations. The result is a conservative mathematical statement: classical facts are not identified with arbitrary projections of a Type-III local algebra, but with central projections selected by an asymptotically abelian completely positive infrared limit.


---


## StableShots：量子电路执行的在线镜头停止

**Original Title:** StableShots: Online Shot Stopping for Quantum Circuit Execution

**Authors:** Giuseppe Bisicchia, Alessandro Bocci, Ernesto Pimentel, Antonio Brogi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22170v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22170v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

量子电路执行通过重复测量来估计输出分布，但开发人员通常在执行之前选择固定的发射预算。这种静态选择很脆弱：低预算可能会导致分布样本不足，而高预算会浪费测量结果。在本文中，我们提出了StableShots，这是静态量子电路的黑匣子在线停止规则。该方法小批量执行固定电路，监控累积经验分布之间的总变化距离，并在重复证明局部稳定性后停止。我们对180条QSimBench轨迹进行了StableShots评估，该轨迹跨越6个电路系列、4到14个量子位的6种尺寸和5个有噪音的IBM模拟后台。通过仅验证校准和100次重复的尾端保持分裂，所选配置在所有持续测试评估中达到TVD <= 0.05，中位数为7，650次，而固定射击基线要么失败得更频繁，要么花费了更多的射击。


### Abstract

Quantum circuit execution estimates output distributions by repeated measurements, yet developers commonly choose a fixed shot budget before execution. This static choice is brittle: low budgets can under-sample the distribution, while high budgets waste measurements. In this paper, we present StableShots, a black-box online stopping rule for static quantum circuits. The method executes a fixed circuit in small batches, monitors the total-variation distance between cumulative empirical distributions, and stops after repeated evidence of local stability. We evaluate StableShots on 180 QSimBench traces spanning six circuit families, six sizes from 4 to 14 qubits, and five noisy IBM simulated backends. With validation-only calibration and 100 repeated backend-holdout splits, the selected configuration reaches TVD <= 0.05 on all held-out test evaluations with median 7,650 shots, whereas fixed-shot baselines either fail more often or spend substantially more shots.


---


## 离散时间的基本不可逆转性

**Original Title:** Fundamental Irreversibility from Discrete Time

**Authors:** M. W. AlMasri

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22187v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22187v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

1964年，余. A.戈尔方德提出了将量子力学扩展到离散时间，预测了内在的非正性和熵增加。虽然具有历史意义，但这种形式主义早于开放量子系统的现代理论。在这项工作中，我们严格地将Gol ' fand的离散进化方程改写为完全正踪迹保留（CPTP）量子通道，并推导出其连续时间粗粒度极限。我们证明动力学收敛到以基本时间尺度$T $为特征的特定Lindblad主方程，这在能量基和基本操作符基$W$中都引起了去相关。我们使用斯波恩的熵产生形式主义分析了热力学含义，证明离散时间步引起了由量子内聚衰变驱动的严格正的熵产生率，从而为独立于环境耦合的时间之箭提供了微观基础。此外，我们通过保真度衰变和纯度损失来量化量子一致性的损失，为容错量子计算建立了精确的约束。我们进一步研究了这种内在退散对离散时间晶体（DTCs）的影响，表明Gol ' fand动力学对时间转换对称性破缺相施加了基本的寿命限制。最后，我们利用来自光学格子钟、物质波干涉测量和中微子振荡的精确数据来对$tau $设定严格的上限。我们的结果将基本时间离散化限制为$T\lesssim 10^{-26}$ s，显着收紧了之前的限制，并为量子引力现象学提供了一个可测试的框架。


### Abstract

In 1964, Yu. A. Gol'fand proposed an extension of quantum mechanics to discrete time, predicting intrinsic non-unitarity and entropy increase. While historically significant, this formalism predates the modern theory of open quantum systems. In this work, we rigorously recast Gol'fand's discrete evolution equation as a Completely Positive Trace-Preserving (CPTP) quantum channel and derive its continuous-time coarse-grained limit. We demonstrate that the dynamics converge to a specific Lindblad master equation characterized by a fundamental time scale $τ$, which induces decoherence in both the energy basis and a fundamental operator basis $W$. We analyze the thermodynamic implications using Spohn's entropy production formalism, proving that the discrete time step induces a strictly positive entropy production rate driven by the decay of quantum coherences, thereby providing a microscopic foundation for the arrow of time independent of environmental coupling. Furthermore, we quantify the loss of quantum coherence via fidelity decay and purity loss, establishing exact constraints for fault-tolerant quantum computing. We further investigate the impact of this intrinsic decoherence on Discrete Time Crystals (DTCs), showing that Gol'fand dynamics impose a fundamental lifetime limit on time-translation symmetry breaking phases. Finally, we utilize precision data from optical lattice clocks, matter-wave interferometry, and neutrino oscillations to place stringent upper bounds on $τ$. Our results constrain the fundamental time discretization to $τ\lesssim 10^{-26}$ s, significantly tightening previous limits and offering a testable framework for quantum gravity phenomenology.


---


## 机器学习最佳量子错误纠正假设

**Original Title:** Machine Learning Optimal Quantum Error Correction Thresholds

**Authors:** Dominik Seip, Luis Colmenarez, Markus Schmitt, Markus Müller

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22194v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22194v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

由于量子计算机仍然容易受到噪音的影响，QEC对于在计算期间保存逻辑信息至关重要。然而，QEC代码的性能会超出某些噪音阈值，揭示了其保护量子信息能力的根本限制。这些限制可以使用信息论测量来描述，例如连贯信息，它量化了通过有噪量子通道可靠传输逻辑信息的最大速率。在这项工作中，我们建立了CI和训练神经网络解码器时使用的二进制交叉熵损失之间的直接联系。具体来说，我们表明CI构成了跨有噪通道跟踪逻辑运算符的解码器可实现的损失的急剧下限。为此，我们开发了一个基于最大似然解码的基于变换器的神经网络模型。我们训练这个网络来估计CI并评估其在三种噪音模型下在表面代码上的性能：代码容量、现象学和电路级噪音。我们的结果表明，该网络可以准确地预测CI并产生与已知理论限制密切匹配的阈值估计。当用作解码器时，网络在逻辑错误率方面显着优于最小权重完美匹配解码器。我们还引入了一种新颖的软后选择方案，该方案独立处理两种逻辑运算符中的不确定性，并依赖于对网络输出的基于置信度的过滤。我们证明了这种基于MLD陪集的后选择策略是最佳的，并证明了其在逻辑错误率和中止概率方面的可扩展性。这些发现将基于变压器的架构确立为QEC的强大工具，并提供了支持基于MLD的后选择的最佳性和可扩展性的第一个数字证据。


### Abstract

As quantum computers remain susceptible to noise, QEC is essential for preserving logical information during computations. However, the performance of QEC codes breaks down beyond certain noise thresholds, revealing fundamental limits on their ability to protect quantum information. These limits can be characterized using information-theoretic measures such as the coherent information, which quantifies the maximum rate at which logical information can be reliably transmitted through a noisy quantum channel. In this work, we establish a direct connection between the CI and the binary cross-entropy loss used when training neural network decoders. Specifically, we show that the CI constitutes a sharp lower bound on the achievable loss for decoders that track logical operators across noisy channels. To this end, we develop a transformer-based neural network model based on maximum likelihood decoding. We train this network to estimate the CI and evaluate its performance on the surface code under three noise models: code capacity, phenomenological, and circuit-level noise. Our results demonstrate that the network accurately predicts CI and yields threshold estimates that closely match known theoretical limits. When used as a decoder, the network significantly outperforms the minimum weight perfect matching decoder in terms of logical error rate. We also introduce a novel soft post-selection scheme that independently treats uncertainty in both logical operators and relies on confidence-based filtering of the network's output. We prove that such post-selection strategies, based on the MLD cosets, are optimal, and demonstrate their scalability in terms of both logical error rate and abort probability. These findings establish transformer-based architectures as powerful tools for QEC and provide the first numerical evidence supporting the optimality and scalability of MLD-based post-selection.


---


## 通过漂移感知射击方法探索弱驱动量子速度极限

**Original Title:** Probing the Weak-Driving Quantum Speed Limit via Drift-Aware Shooting Methods

**Authors:** Denis Janković, Saba Taherpour, Paul-Louis Etienney, Paul-Antoine Hervieux, Christoph Wolf

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22212v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22212v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

量子最优控制的中心目标是实现高保真度和低能量控制脉冲。当量子最优控制方法独立地优化在小时间步上离散化的脉冲的每个点时，这可以产生高保真度控制，但也会导致宽带和耗电的波型。我们扩展了MAGICARP --一种受庞特里亚金能量最大原理启发的射击方法，从一小组参数生成整个脉冲，通过构造使其光滑且节能--从无漂移系统扩展到具有恒定漂移Hamilton的封闭系统。外部磁场中的两个交换耦合的旋转。优化分阶段进行：漂移Hamilton的修饰状态结构目标，在脉冲波框架中执行初始射击优化，随后进行精确的实验室框架细化。MAGICARP以匹配门不保真度与Krotov和GRAPE为基准，始终实现最低的能量和保守的脉冲面积，将其频谱权重集中在门相关的转变上，并且对交换耦合中的波动最稳健; GRAPE独立收敛到基本相同的脉冲，而Krotov的方法则支付了数量级的能量溢价。此外，对RST优化运行的大规模统计调查解决了两个交换耦合电子旋转的弱驱动量子速度限制：两量子位量子傅里叶变换的低幅度实现在由漂移的相互作用率设置的临界门控时间$T '*$以下不再存在，并且最小控制能量在接近这一限制时会偏离。分歧遵循简单的双参数面积极点定律，$E_2^{\mathrm{law}}（T）=A/T+B/（T-T^*）$，其第一项是时间最优面积成本，其第二项是速度极限处的极点。


### Abstract

A central goal of quantum optimal control is to achieve high-fidelity and low-energy control pulses. When quantum optimal control methods optimize every point of a pulse discretized over small time steps independently this can yield high fidelity control but also results in broadband and energy-hungry waveforms. We extend MAGICARP -- a shooting method inspired by Pontryagin's maximum principle on energy that generates an entire pulse from a small set of parameters, making it smooth and energy-efficient by construction -- from driftless systems to closed systems with the constant drift Hamiltonian of two exchange-coupled spins in an external magnetic field. The optimization proceeds in stages: the dressed states of the drift Hamiltonian structure the target, an initial shooting optimization is performed in the rotating-wave frame, and an exact laboratory-frame refinement follows. Benchmarked against Krotov and GRAPE at matched gate infidelity, MAGICARP consistently achieves the lowest energy and a conserved pulse area, concentrates its spectral weight on the gate-relevant transitions, and is the most robust to fluctuations in the exchange coupling; GRAPE independently converges to essentially the same pulse, while Krotov's method pays an order-of-magnitude energy premium. Moreover, a large statistical survey of unselected optimization runs resolves a weak-driving quantum speed limit for two exchange-coupled electron spins: low-amplitude realizations of the two-qubit quantum Fourier transform cease to exist below a critical gate time $T^*$ set by the drift's interaction rate, and the minimum control energy diverges on approach to this limit. The divergence obeys a simple two-parameter area-pole law, $E_2^{\mathrm{law}}(T)=A/T+B/(T-T^*)$, whose first term is the time-optimal area cost and whose second term is a pole at the speed limit.


---


## 螺旋轨道角动量光电子学中的几何控制异常点

**Original Title:** Geometry-Controlled Exceptional Points in Helicoidal Orbital-Angular-Momentum Photonics

**Authors:** Edilberto O. Silva

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22240v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22240v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

异常点（EP）是特征值和特征载体结合的非厄米特谱奇异性。我们提出了轨道角动量（OSC）光电子学中的EP的几何控制路径。在有效的无扭转螺旋背景中，扭转在相反的OSC模式之间提供有符号的、真实的手征分裂，而开放性、收益、损失、泄漏或通道耦合则提供非厄米性。当几何失调补偿残余模式分裂并且线宽对比度满足非厄米平衡条件时，达到EP;因此，扭转率是控制参数，而不是非厄米性的来源。我们获得了受限量子问题和近轴区域中螺旋扭曲引导的OSC斜坡，并将OSC双峰嵌入到多模式-空间模型中，以表明EP在旁观者模式中生存。特征值合并、相刚性崩溃、具有残余失调的线性EP跟踪以及几何环绕下的分支交换提供了可证伪的签名。OSC解析的输入-输出响应将这些映射到光谱级的可观测物上，包括光谱图和三维Riemann表面可视化。对两个不同的光平台（一个是互逆的，一个是非对称耦合的Wiersig型平台）进行设备级近轴模拟，重现了预测的异常点及其线性几何跟踪。


### Abstract

Exceptional points (EPs) are non-Hermitian spectral singularities where eigenvalues and eigenvectors coalesce. We propose a geometry-controlled route to EPs in orbital-angular-momentum (OAM) photonics. In an effective torsion-free helicoidal background, the twist supplies a signed, real chiral splitting between opposite-OAM modes, while openness, gain, loss, leakage, or channel coupling, supplies the non-Hermiticity. The EP is reached when the geometric detuning compensates for a residual mode splitting and the linewidth contrast meets the non-Hermitian balance condition; the twist rate is thus the control parameter, not the source of non-Hermiticity. We obtain the OAM slope both for a confined quantum problem and, in the paraxial regime, for a helically twisted guide, and embed the OAM doublet in a multimode mode-space model to show that the EP survives spectator modes. Eigenvalue coalescence, phase-rigidity collapse, linear EP tracking with residual detuning, and branch exchange under geometric encircling provide falsifiable signatures. An OAM-resolved input-output response maps these onto spectroscopy-level observables, including spectral maps and three-dimensional Riemann-surface visualizations. A device-level paraxial simulation of two distinct photonic platforms, one reciprocal and one asymmetric-coupling Wiersig-type platform, reproduces the predicted exceptional point and its linear geometric tracking.


---


## 与共同热储层耦合的简并玻色子模中的集体Mpemba型松弛

**Original Title:** Collective Mpemba-Type Relaxation in Degenerate Bosonic Modes Coupled to a Common Thermal Reservoir

**Authors:** I. M. de Araújo, H. Sanchez, L. F. Alves da Silva, L. F. Alves da Silva, Norton G. de Almeida, M. H. Y. Moussa

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22273v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22273v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-20


### 摘要

我们研究了与共同热库耦合的玻色子模简并家族中的集体Mpemba型松弛。从完全对称的M模式描述开始，并采用代表性的平均场约化，我们推导出弱耦合马尔科夫、强耦合Caldeira-Leggett和弱耦合非马尔科夫状态的有效主方程。在弱耦合马尔科夫极限下，驰豫分离为以速率γ衰变的非连贯热通道和以速率M γ衰变的集体连贯通道，产生由初始状态准备确定的显式Mpemba穿越时间。在强耦合Caldeira-Leggett状态中，瞬时交相动力学丰富了松弛模式，延迟了过衰减扇形的交叉并在欠衰减扇形中产生多次交叉。在非马尔科夫机制中，库记忆通过时间依赖性衰变率和兰姆位移重塑相同的通道竞争机制，产生延迟和聚集的交叉窗口。基于能量和Kullback-Leibler分歧的数值结果揭示了Mpemba和反Mpemba行为、准则依赖性以及集体相关性、积分动力学和水库记忆引起的多次瞬时重新排序。


### Abstract

We investigate collective Mpemba-type relaxation in a degenerate family of bosonic modes coupled to a common thermal reservoir. Starting from a fully symmetric M-mode description and employing a representative mean-field reduction, we derive effective master equations for weak-coupling Markovian, strong-coupling Caldeira-Leggett, and weak-coupling non-Markovian regimes. In the weak-coupling Markovian limit, relaxation separates into an incoherent thermal channel decaying at rate gamma and a collective coherent channel decaying at rate M gamma, yielding an explicit Mpemba crossing time determined by the initial-state preparation. In the strong-coupling Caldeira-Leggett regime, transient quadrature dynamics enriches the relaxation pattern, delaying crossings in the overdamped sector and generating multiple crossings in the underdamped sector. In the non-Markovian regime, reservoir memory reshapes the same channel-competition mechanism through time-dependent decay rates and a Lamb shift, producing delayed and clustered crossing windows. Numerical results based on the energy and the Kullback-Leibler divergence reveal Mpemba and anti-Mpemba behavior, criterion dependence, and multiple transient reorderings induced by collective coherence, quadrature dynamics, and reservoir memory.


---


## 用螺旋形中子阵面探测单粒子空间范围

**Original Title:** Probing Single-Particle Spatial Extent With Helical Neutron Wavefronts

**Authors:** D. Sarenac, O. Lailey, C. W. Clark, D. G. Cory, H. Ekinci, D. V. Garrad, M. G. Huber, L. Matthews, N. Shentevski, P. R. Vadnere, D. A. Pushin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22292v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22292v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

区分横向相干长度与单粒子波包范围具有根本性的挑战性，因为两者都通过传统实验中观察到的强度轮廓的空间拓宽来体现。在这里，我们介绍了一种基于螺旋式中子波阵面的方法，可以实现这种分离。螺旋形中子状态产生环形强度轮廓，其峰值半径取决于横向波包范围，而相干长度仅有助于轮廓增宽。在我们的实验几何结构中，我们测量到约1.1 mrad的束分歧度，对应于约180纳米的横向相干长度。相比之下，相同的测量结果在各个中子波包的空间范围上设定了>= 2 um的下限，比相干长度大一个数量级以上。这些结果提供了直接的实验证据，证明横向相干长度和单粒子波包范围是不同的物理量，解决了中子文献中长期存在的混乱根源。


### Abstract

Distinguishing transverse coherence length from single-particle wavepacket extent is fundamentally challenging, as both manifest through spatial broadening of observed intensity profiles in conventional experiments. Here we introduce a method based on helical neutron wavefronts that enables this separation. Helical neutron states produce annular intensity profiles whose peak radius depends on the transverse wavepacket extent, while coherence length only contributes to profile broadening. In our experimental geometry we measure a beam divergence of ~1.1 mrad, corresponding to a transverse coherence length of ~180 nm. In contrast, the same measurement places a lower bound of >= 2 um on the spatial extent of the individual neutron wavepackets, more than an order of magnitude larger than the coherence length. These results provide direct experimental evidence that transverse coherence length and single-particle wavepacket extent are distinct physical quantities, resolving a longstanding source of confusion in the neutron literature.


---


## 对称化背后的物理学

**Original Title:** The Physics Behind Symmetrization

**Authors:** R. E. Kastner

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22298v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22298v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

人们经常断言，由于“标签冗余”，同类型粒子的量子状态必须对称化，即假设直接积状态中标签的排列并不反映任何真正的物理区别，因此它们的排列构成了“交换简并”。这一假设受到电子等同类型粒子的散射情况的直接挑战，其中涉及两个物理上不同的散射通道，有效地对应于标签的排列。我在讨论这个反例时，重点关注文献中现存的省略了相关物理内容的描述。我进一步指出，对称化必须普遍实施的假设并没有得到粒子相互作用的实际计算的支持，也没有得到基于准备和结果的看似可行的粒子状态的支持。


### Abstract

It is often asserted that quantum states for same-type particles must be symmetrized due to ``label redundancy,'' i.e. the assumption that the permutations of labels in direct-product states do not reflect any real physical distinction and thus their permutations constitute an ``exchange degeneracy''. This assumption is directly challenged by the case of scattering of same-type particles such as electrons, which involves two physically distinct scattering channels effectively corresponding to permutation of the labels. I discuss this counterexample with critical attention to an extant portrayal in the literature that omits pertinent physical content. I further note ways in which the assumption that symmetrization must be universally imposed is not supported by actual calculations of particle interactions, nor by seemingly viable particle states based on preparations and outcomes.


---


## 让量子网络发挥作用：路由、校准和可编程量子中继器

**Original Title:** Making Quantum Networks Work: Routing, Calibration, and Programmable Quantum Repeaters

**Authors:** Vinay Kumar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22316v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22316v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

量子互联网使量子状态能够跨远程节点分布，支持安全通信、分布式计算和量子传感。与经典网络不同，它受到非克隆定理、概率纠缠生成、去相关和硬件漂移的限制，使得经典的抽象不充分。因此，可扩展量子网络需要新的架构、协议和优化方法来明确考虑这些限制。   本论文研究了现实约束下量子网络的架构、路由和操作，重点关注量子转发器网络上的双方纠缠分布。关键指标包括端到端保真度、吞吐量、可扩展性和公平性。在网络层，路由策略的开发超出了同质节点和完整网络知识的假设。异类转发器效率下的路由展示了对节点质量的部分了解如何提高保真度并减少路径阻塞。然后引入了一种灰箱路由方法，其中路径选择仅依赖于布局和端到端估计，无需详细的链路信息即可实现稳健性和公平性。   在链路层，通过分离激活和校准阶段的校准感知模型来解决校准和硬件漂移。对于线性转发器链，可以推导出最佳校准时间表来平衡操作时间和校准费用。这被扩展到具有共享链接的一般布局，其中提出了贪婪编排启发式。   最后，论文通过基于NV中心的可编程量子转发器节点的指令集架构将网络协议与硬件连接起来，实现一致的可编程性并将物理操作链接到更高层协议。


### Abstract

The quantum internet enables distribution of quantum states across distant nodes, supporting secure communication, distributed computing, and quantum sensing. Unlike classical networks, it is constrained by the no cloning theorem, probabilistic entanglement generation, decoherence, and hardware drift, making classical abstractions inadequate. Scalable quantum networking therefore requires new architectures, protocols, and optimisation methods that explicitly account for these limitations.
  This thesis studies the architecture, routing, and operation of quantum networks under realistic constraints, focusing on bipartite entanglement distribution over quantum repeater networks. Key metrics include end to end fidelity, throughput, scalability, and fairness. At the network layer, routing strategies are developed beyond assumptions of homogeneous nodes and full network knowledge. Routing under heterogeneous repeater efficiencies shows how partial knowledge of node quality improves fidelity and reduces path blocking. A grey box routing approach is then introduced, where path selection relies only on topology and end to end estimates, achieving robustness and fairness without detailed link information.
  At the link layer, calibration and hardware drift are addressed through a calibration aware model separating activation and calibration phases. For linear repeater chains, an optimal calibration schedule is derived to balance operation time and calibration overhead. This is extended to general topologies with shared links, where a greedy orchestration heuristic is proposed.
  Finally, the thesis connects network protocols with hardware via an instruction set architecture for programmable quantum repeater nodes based on NV centers, enabling coherent programmability and linking physical operations to higher layer protocols.


---


## 量子机器学习中没有无参考的概括

**Original Title:** No Reference-Free Generalization in Quantum Machine Learning

**Authors:** Jeongho Bang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22331v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22331v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

量子机器学习通常是由量子系统呈指数级大的状态空间驱动的，但这一承诺留下了一个未解决的基本概括问题：当训练数据没有提供首选基础、测量框架或其他定向结构时，学习者如何为不可见的量子方向赋予不同的含义？我们通过在没有外部量子参考系的情况下制定监督学习来解决这个可识别性问题，这样预测就不能依赖于对Hilbert空间坐标的任意选择。这一要求迫使学习的分类器保留训练数据未破坏的每个单位对称性。我们证明，每当训练状态未能跨越整个希尔伯特空间时，所有与其跨度垂直的纯状态都必须收到相同的预测--即使这些状态相互垂直并且一旦提供适当的测量结果就完全可区分。因此，该限制不是由状态歧视、优化或计算能力引起的，而是由缺失引用信息引起的。我们进一步在弱对称破缺下建立了一个稳健的版本，并表明在多量子位系统上学习通用非结构化概念需要指数级多的独立定向训练方向。数字插图可视化了由此产生的预测崩溃及其受控放松。我们的结果将特征地图、测量基、汉密尔顿体、局部性、对称性先验、架构和足够多样化的训练状态识别为概括的操作资源。其核心含义是，单凭Hilbert空间维度并不是一个可学习的特征空间：成功的QML必须指定赋予不可见量子方向语义意义的物理结构。


### Abstract

Quantum machine learning is often motivated by the exponentially large state space of quantum systems, but this promise leaves a basic generalization problem unresolved: how can a learner assign different meanings to unseen quantum directions when the training data provide no preferred basis, measurement frame, or other orienting structure? We address this identifiability problem by formulating supervised learning without an external quantum reference frame, so that predictions cannot depend on an arbitrary choice of Hilbert-space coordinates. This requirement forces the learned classifier to preserve every unitary symmetry left unbroken by the training data. We prove that whenever the training states fail to span the full Hilbert space, all pure states orthogonal to their span must receive the same prediction -- even when those states are mutually orthogonal and perfectly distinguishable once an appropriate measurement is supplied. The limitation is therefore not caused by state discrimination, optimization, or computational power, but by missing reference information. We further establish a robust version under weak symmetry breaking and show that learning generic unstructured concepts on multiqubit systems requires exponentially many independently oriented training directions. Numerical illustrations visualize the resulting prediction collapse and its controlled relaxation. Our results identify feature maps, measurement bases, Hamiltonians, locality, symmetry priors, architectures, and sufficiently diverse training states as operational resources for generalization. The central implication is that Hilbert-space dimension alone is not a learnable feature space: successful QML must specify the physical structure that gives unseen quantum directions semantic meaning.


---


## 来自铸造二维量子游动的圆周和凸区域积分的格分位数估计

**Original Title:** Lattice-quantile estimation of π and convex-region integrals from coined two-dimensional quantum walks

**Authors:** Jen-Yu Chang, En-Jui Kuo, Chih-Yu Chen, Tsung-Wei Huang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22334v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22334v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

蒙特卡洛积分从根本上受到Cramer-Rao界对期望值的任何样本均值估计量施加的M_^（-1/2）比率的限制，无论样本是如何绘制的。众所周知，创造的离散时间量子游动（DTQW）是以弹道方式传播的--它们的位置方差与经典随机游动的扩散T相比，缩放为T2--但这种更快的传播尚未被利用来进行数值积分。我们表明，将2D DTQW的弹道标度与高斯圆格数的Hardy-Huxley渐进式耦合会产生估计器，其主要误差是由行走深度T控制的确定性大数余差，而不是由样本计数M控制的统计波动。该结构用格数与辐射位置分位数平方的比率N（R-hat）/R-hat ' 2取代样本均值估计器的经验均值，这是一种绕过Cramer-Rao障碍的结构变化。然后，一批测量通过经典预先计算的乘数传播，以同时覆盖整个积分族。我们通过Kraetzel的格点渐进开发了凸光滑域的框架，并通过Cavalieri原理开发了具有凸或环形超水平集的光滑积分，并为偏差底提供了无参数的身份（在所有测试深度中验证为1.5x以内）。每个实验都以经典随机游走为基准，使用相同的估计器来隔离量子贡献;该框架在QAE意义上是无Oracle的（不需要对被积函数进行受控的么正编码），并且在结构上与量子幅度估计和Szegedy-walk方法不同。这些比率以固定精度比较测量计数，并且不包括量子电路执行成本。


### Abstract

Monte Carlo integration is fundamentally limited by the M^(-1/2) rate that the Cramer-Rao bound imposes on any sample-mean estimator of an expectation value, regardless of how the samples are drawn. Coined discrete-time quantum walks (DTQWs) are known to spread ballistically - their position variance scales as T^2 against the diffusive T of classical random walks - yet this faster spreading has not been exploited for numerical integration. We show that coupling the ballistic scaling of a 2D DTQW to the Hardy-Huxley asymptotic for Gauss circle lattice counts produces estimators whose dominant error is a deterministic number-theoretic residual controlled by walk depth T, not a statistical fluctuation controlled by sample count M. The construction replaces the empirical mean of a sample-mean estimator with the ratio N(R-hat)/R-hat^2 of a lattice count to the square of a radial position quantile, a structural change that sidesteps the Cramer-Rao barrier. A single batch of measurements then propagates through classically precomputed multipliers to cover an entire family of integrals simultaneously. We develop the framework for convex smooth domains via Kraetzel's lattice asymptotic and for smooth integrals with convex or annular super-level sets via Cavalieri's principle, and provide a parameter-free identity for the bias floor (validated to within 1.5x across all tested depths). Every experiment is benchmarked against the classical random walk with the identical estimator to isolate the quantum contribution; the framework is oracle-free in the QAE sense (no controlled unitary encoding the integrand is required) and structurally distinct from quantum amplitude estimation and Szegedy-walk approaches. These ratios compare measurement counts at fixed precision and do not include quantum circuit execution cost.


---


## 量子超级通道的概率存储和检索以进行“回顾性”干预

**Original Title:** Probabilistic Storage and Retrieval of Quantum Superchannels for "Retrospective'' Intervention

**Authors:** Wataru Yokojima, Jisho Miyazaki, Mio Murao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22343v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22343v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

将未知量子计算存储在量子状态中并在稍后期望的时间检索它是一项具有挑战性的任务，受到量子计算的无编程定理的阻碍。在之前关于量子通道概率存储和检索（pSAR）任务的研究中，推导出了从量子状态准确检索单个未知么正通道的最大概率，其中未知么正通道已通过多次调用对未知么正通道进行编码。在这项工作中，我们考虑了pSAR的更高级版本，即确定因果的单位超通道的概率存储和检索，它是由具有开放槽的单位通道序列进行物理建模的，其中任意通道可以插入单位通道之间进行干预。此任务需要激活超级通道上的“回顾性”干预功能，超出其正常干预功能。我们提出两个协议：部分隐形传输（对于少量存储查询是最佳的）和阶梯倒缝（随着查询数量的增加渐进地实现单位成功概率）。我们还推导出了一个针对正超通道的通用倒置协议。


### Abstract

Storing an unknown quantum computation in a quantum state and retrieving it at a desired later time is a challenging task, hindered by the no-programming theorem of quantum computations. In the previous studies on the task of probabilistic storage-and-retrieval (pSAR) of quantum channels, the maximum probability of exactly retrieving a single unknown unitary channel from a quantum state in which the unknown unitary has been encoded via multiple calls to the unknown unitary channel is derived. In this work, we consider a higher-order version of pSAR, the probabilistic storage-and-retrieval of definite-causal unitary superchannels, which are physically modeled by sequences of unitary channels with open slots where arbitrary channels can be inserted between the unitary channels for intervention. This task requires activating the ``retrospective'' intervention functionality on the superchannel, beyond its normal intervention functionality. We propose two protocols: partial teleportation, which is optimal for a small number of storage queries, and staircase backstitch, which achieves unit success probability asymptotically as the number of queries increases. We also derive a universal inversion protocol for unitary superchannels.


---


## Vibe校准：通过技能演示语言代理自主启动112量子位的超导量子处理器

**Original Title:** Vibe Calibration: Autonomous Bring-up of a 112-Qubit Superconducting Quantum Processor by a Skill-Orchestrating Language Agent

**Authors:** Huikai Xu, Jiaxiu Han, Shigang Ou, Cheng Ye, Zisong Shen, Jing Gao, Yijia Wang, Tianrui Che, Yu Song, Weiyang Liu, Lei Wang, Lin-Feng Zhang, Pan Zhang, Hai-Feng Yu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22376v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22376v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

超导量子计算是最成熟的量子计算固态平台之一，处理器超过一百个量子位。然而，进一步扩展到容错量子计算越来越受到校准复杂性的限制。传统脚本对异常信号很脆弱，而且专家判断受到认知带宽和序列操作时间的限制，无法跟上系统规模的步伐。在这里，我们报告Vibe Calibration，这是一个由大型语言模型代理精心编排的自主校准系统，它将专家隐性知识提炼成可重复使用的技能。每个技能都被组织为一个决策树，它打包了参数化的测量命令、量化接受标准和审计记录，从而实现自主执行和自我修复。我们通过三阶段人在循环蒸馏过程来捕获这些知识，并在经过验证的轨迹上微调大型语言模型。在具有频率可调转换子的112量子位处理器上，该系统在4.7小时内自主完成112个量子位中的108个量子位的校准，比手动校准完整112个量子位可实现4--5$\times $的加速。与对16个量子位子集进行的专家手动校准的交叉验证比较显示，对16个量子位中的14个达成了一致。更重要的是，该模型展示了跨设备的可转移校准工作流程。虽然低级控制脚本需要针对不同的硬件平台进行较小的接口调整，但核心决策逻辑和任务编排推广到新的处理器，展示了可重复使用的实验室接口而不是记忆脚本。这项工作首次展示了通过可重复使用和可审核技能对一百量子位的高温处理器进行完全自主校准，消除了可扩展量子硬件操作的关键障碍。


### Abstract

Superconducting quantum computing is one of the most mature solid-state platforms for quantum computation, with processors exceeding one hundred qubits. Yet further scaling toward fault-tolerant quantum computing is increasingly constrained by calibration complexity. Conventional scripts are brittle to anomalous signals, and expert judgment is bounded by cognitive bandwidth and serial operation time, failing to keep pace with system scale. Here we report Vibe Calibration, an autonomous calibration system orchestrated by large language model agents, which distills expert tacit knowledge into reusable Skills. Each Skill is organized as a decision tree that packages parameterized measurement commands, quantitative acceptance criteria, and audit records, enabling autonomous execution and self-healing. We capture this knowledge through a three-phase human-in-the-loop distillation process and fine-tune a large language model on validated trajectories. On a 112-qubit processor with frequency-tunable transmons, the system autonomously completes calibration of 108 out of 112 qubits in 4.7 hours, achieving a 4--5$\times$ speedup over manual calibration of the full 112 qubits. A cross-validated comparison with expert manual calibration on a 16-qubit subset shows agreement on 14 out of 16 qubits. More importantly, the model demonstrates transferable calibration workflows across devices. While low-level control scripts require minor interface adaptation for different hardware platforms, the core decision logic and task orchestration generalize to new processors, demonstrating a reusable laboratory interface rather than a memorized script.This work demonstrates, for the first time, fully autonomous calibration of a hundred-qubit superconducting processor through reusable and auditable Skills, removing a critical barrier to scalable quantum hardware operation.


---


## Quantum Otto发动机，采用非Hermitian XY模型，具有脱钩的空转水平

**Original Title:** Quantum Otto engine with decoupled idle levels in a non-Hermitian XY model

**Authors:** Maimaitiyiming Tusun, Fang Zhao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22405v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22405v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

我们研究了具有交错虚磁场的两量子位非厄米特XY模型中的量子奥托循环。该系统的能谱自然地分解为一对依赖于外场的工作级和一对完全独立于外场的闲置级，从而提供了de~Oliveira和Jonathan提出的闲置级量子热力机架构的第一个具体微观实现[Phys. Rev. E 104，044133（2021）]在物理旋转模型中。调整非埃尔米特参数eta_0会推动从具有负净功和热储存器净热吸收的消散状态持续过渡到真正的热力发动机模式，同时提高输出功和效率。随着eta_0在稳定PT不间断阶段内增加，发动机效率显着提高，达到卡诺极限的很大一部分。这种效应源于闲置层间隙的压缩，从而重新分配热平衡状态和冷平衡状态下的层占据重量，从而调节吸收的热量。网络运算式的分子独立于eta_0，但分母通过双曲cos函数间接取决于eta_0--这是闲置级控制机制的数学根源。我们对这些发现对参数变化的稳健性进行了详细分析，对非埃尔米特控制与埃尔米特极限进行了严格比较，以及捕获离子量子模拟器的具体实验提案。我们的结果表明，非厄米性是引导量子引擎操作模式和性能的不可或缺的工具。


### Abstract

We study a quantum Otto cycle in a two-qubit non-Hermitian XY model with a staggered imaginary magnetic field. The energy spectrum of this system naturally decouples into a pair of working levels that depend on the external field and a pair of idle levels that are completely independent of it, thereby providing the first concrete microscopic realization of the idle-level quantum heat engine architecture proposed by de~Oliveira and Jonathan [Phys. Rev. E 104, 044133 (2021)] in a physical spin model. Tuning the non-Hermitian parameter eta_0 drives a continuous transition from a dissipative regime with negative net work and net heat absorption from the hot reservoir into a genuine heat engine mode, while simultaneously enhancing both output work and efficiency. As eta_0 increases within the stable PT-unbroken phase, the engine efficiency rises significantly, reaching a substantial fraction of the Carnot limit. This effect originates from the compression of the idle-level gap, which redistributes the level occupation weights in the hot and cold equilibrium states and thereby modulates the absorbed heat. The numerator of the net work expression is independent of eta_0, but the denominator depends on eta_0 indirectly through hyperbolic cosine functions -- this is the mathematical root of the idle-level control mechanism. We provide a detailed analysis of the robustness of these findings against parameter variations, a critical comparison of the non-Hermitian control with the Hermitian limit, and a concrete experimental proposal for trapped-ion quantum simulators. Our results demonstrate that non-Hermiticity serves as an indispensable tool for steering both the operation mode and the performance of a quantum engine.


---


## 长期量子临界性的微扰重正化和普适性图

**Original Title:** Perturbative Renormalization and Universality Diagram for Long-Range Quantum Criticality

**Authors:** Zhiyi Li, Zhijie Fan, Kun Chen, Youjin Deng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22407v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22407v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

量子模拟器的实验进展凸显了远程（LR）相互作用在重塑量子临界性和稳定短程（SR）范式之外的奇异相方面的作用。我们研究相互作用衰变为$1/r '#+ Sigma '$的铁磁远程量子$O（n）'模型，并通过设置$d=3-e '和$Sigma =2-δ$在LR-SR边界周围发展微扰重正化群展开。在这种参数化中，完整的交互LR窗口$2d/3<Sigma <2$变成$0<δ<2 e/3$，因此受到扰动控制。双循环计算可以得到相关长度指数$v $以及频率和动量异常维$n_co $和$n$的显式表达，单位为$、$δ$和$n $。所得指数在$Sigma =2d/3$时简化为远程高斯标度，并在$Sigma\到2$极限时简化为SR量子Wilson-Fisher标度，从而将$Sigma_*=2$识别为受控$3-e $展开内的LR-SR边界。将RG结果与缩放边界和经典LR类比相结合，我们提出了铁磁性远程量子$O（n）$临界性的$（d，Sigma）$普适性图，并将其用作远程量子旋转链的相图的组织框架。


### Abstract

Experimental progress in quantum simulators highlights the role of long-range (LR) interactions in reshaping quantum criticality and stabilizing exotic phases beyond the short-range (SR) paradigm. We study ferromagnetic long-range quantum $O(n)$ models with interactions decaying as $1/r^{d+σ}$ and develop a perturbative renormalization-group expansion around the LR--SR boundary by setting $d=3-ε$ and $σ=2-δ$. In this parametrization, the full interacting LR window $2d/3<σ<2$ becomes $0<δ<2ε/3$, and is therefore perturbatively controlled. A two-loop calculation yields explicit expressions, in terms of $ε$, $δ$, and $n$, for the correlation-length exponent $ν$ and for the frequency and momentum anomalous dimensions $η_ω$ and $η_k$. The resulting exponents reduce to long-range Gaussian scaling at $σ=2d/3$ and to SR quantum Wilson-Fisher scaling in the $σ\to 2$ limit, thereby identifying $σ_*=2$ as the LR--SR boundary within the controlled $3-ε$ expansion. Combining the RG results with scaling boundaries and classical LR analogies, we propose a $(d,σ)$ universality diagram for ferromagnetic long-range quantum $O(n)$ criticality and use it as an organizing framework for the phase diagram of long-range quantum spin chains.

## 一种用于容差量子计算的三层架构

**Original Title:** A Three-Layer Architecture for Fault-Tolerant Quantum Computing

**Authors:** Zhirao Wang, Zhou You, Yiming Huang, Tianyi Li, Ying Li, Xiao Yuan, Yuan Yao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22418v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22418v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

故障容忍是构建大规模通用量子计算机不可或缺的先决条件。本文借鉴经典计算机体系结构的理念，提出了一个硬件不可知的三层高级体系结构框架，用于通用的容差量子计算。该模型在容错量子算法的实际执行工作流程的指导下，与特定的物理量子位硬件平台和量子错误纠正码脱钩，充当通用抽象标准而不是特定于平台的实现方案。特别关注中间的容差层，它充当应用程序级逻辑程序和硬件级执行之间的架构桥梁。我们系统地描述了它的五个内部组件，它们之间交换的接口和数据，以及执行，校正和适应路径，这些路径共同实现逻辑合成，容错资源管理，解码和运行时容错控制。最后给出了端到端的例子来说明该框架下容错量子算法的全栈操作流水线。鉴于对模块化、异构和跨层容错量子系统的日益重视，我们的架构为组织此类设计提供了统一的基础模型。


### Abstract

Fault tolerance is an indispensable prerequisite for constructing large-scale universal quantum computers. Drawing philosophies from classical computer architecture, this paper presents a hardware-agnostic three-layer high-level architectural framework for generic fault-tolerant quantum computation. Guided by the real execution workflows of fault-tolerant quantum algorithms, the proposed model is decoupled from specific physical qubit hardware platforms and quantum error correction codes, serving as a universal abstract standard rather than a platform-specific implementation scheme. Special attention is devoted to the intermediate Fault-Tolerance Layer, which serves as the architectural bridge between application-level logical programs and hardware-level execution. We systematically characterize its five internal components, the interfaces and data exchanged among them, and the execution, correction, and adaptation paths that together enable logical synthesis, fault-tolerant resources management, decoding, and runtime fault-tolerant control. An end-to-end example is further provided to illustrate the full-stack operating pipeline of fault-tolerant quantum algorithms under this framework. Given the increasing emphasis on modular, heterogeneous, and cross-layer fault-tolerant quantum systems, our architecture provides a unified foundational model for organizing such designs.

## 光限制的量子度量束缚态

**Original Title:** Quantum Metric Bound State of Light Confinement

**Authors:** Jinchao Zhao, Rongning Liu, Xue-Yang Song, K. T. Law

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22479v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22479v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

缺陷诱导束缚态的空间限制通常由分散带中的有效质量决定。最近，由精确相消干涉产生的紧凑定域状态（SCS）已被用来实现平带中的限制。然而，SCS依赖于原始的网格对称性和微调的缺陷轮廓。通用局部杂质的引入不可避免地打破了这些严格的相匹配条件，导致广泛的束缚状态，其基本长度尺度仍然是一个悬而未决的问题。在这里，我们建立了第三种限制状态：量子度量束缚状态。我们提供了严格的数学证明，证明在没有动能和CLS保护的情况下，这些状态的指数衰变长度受到未扰动平带的量子度量的下限。我们通过构建一系列高度可调的平带发生器来证明这种几何限制的紧密性，并验证了其在各种现实架构中的普遍性。最终，这种分类建立了独立可测量的量子度量，作为合成波平台中工程约束模式的预测设计原则。


### Abstract

The spatial confinement of defect-induced bound states is conventionally governed by the effective mass in dispersive bands. More recently, Compact Localized States (CLSs) arising from exact destructive interference have been utilized to achieve confinement in flat bands. However, CLSs rely on pristine lattice symmetries and fine-tuned defect profiles. The introduction of a generic local impurity inevitably breaks these strict phase-matching conditions, resulting in extensive bound states whose fundamental length scale has remained an open question. Here, we establish a third regime of confinement: the quantum metric bound state. We provide a rigorous mathematical proof demonstrating that in the absence of kinetic energy and CLS protection, the exponential decay length of these states is lower-bounded by the quantum metric of the unperturbed flat band. We demonstrate the tightness of this geometric limit by constructing a family of highly tunable flat-band generators, and we verify its universality across diverse realistic architectures. Ultimately, this classification establishes the independently measurable quantum metric as a predictive design principle for engineering confined modes in synthetic wave platforms.
