## 子系统去相关下扩展集群状态中混合对称保护的拓色状态层次

**Original Title:** Hierarchy of mixed symmetry protected topological states in extended cluster states under subsystem decoherence

**Authors:** Yoshihito Kuno, Takahiro Orito

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22507v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22507v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

我们研究了子系统去相干对扩展团簇状态的影响，扩展团簇状态是对称保护的topology（SPP）相。该模型包括许多子系统$Z_2$对称性。我们报告说，子系统退散会引起局部电荷波动，从而导致未受影响的子系统中出现混合SPL状态。如果我们从扩展集群状态开始，则会出现分层混合状态STP阶段以响应子系统分步去焦。这些混合状态SPL相保持强对称性，其对称性保护了初始集群SPL的对称性。此外，这些STP可以用Rényi-2串顺序来描述。然后，随着子系统逐渐去叠加，混合状态SPL相的层次结构在最后剩余子系统上终止为$Z_2$强到弱自发对称破缺（SWTSB）状态，其中出现远程纠缠状态，即玻璃状格林伯格-霍恩-蔡林格（GZZ）状态。我们的工作表明，去相干不仅是一个破坏性的过程，而且可以诱发和组织一系列非平凡的混合状态。这揭示了从混合态SPT有序到具有玻璃GHZ型长程纠缠的SWSSB的系统路径。


### Abstract

We study the effect of subsystem decoherence to an extended cluster state which is a symmetry protected topological (SPT) phase. The model includes many subsystem $Z_2$ symmetries. We report that subsystem decoherence induces local charge fluctuations, leading to a mixed SPT state in the unaffected subsystems. If we start from the extended cluster state, hierarchical mixed-state SPT phases emerge in response to step-by-step subsystem decoherences. These mixed-state SPT phases keep strong symmetries the symmetry of which is protecting symmetries for the initial cluster SPT. Moreover, these SPTs can be characterized by Rényi-2 string orders. Then, as the subsystems are progressively decohered, the hierarchy of mixed-state SPT phases terminates in a $Z_2$ strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SWSSB) state on the final remaining subsystem, where a long-range entangled state appears, namely a glassy Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ) state. Our work demonstrates that decoherence is not merely a destructive process, but can induce and organize series of nontrivial mixed-states. This reveals a systematic route from mixed-state SPT order to SWSSB with the glassy GHZ-type long-range entanglement.


---


## 开放量子系统中的几何响应：相关性、弯曲性和敏感性

**Original Title:** Geometric Response in Open Quantum Systems: Coherence, Curvature, and Susceptibility

**Authors:** Eric R. Bittner, Carlos Silva-Acuña

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22517v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22517v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

我们通过将稳态响应张量分解为对称和反对称扇形，为开放量子系统开发了响应几何框架。对称扇形定义了控制局部敏感性的类米制响应张量，而反对称扇形定义了与非互惠响应和几何功相关的弯曲二型。我们表明，功曲正是响应张量的反对称分量，建立了涨落-响应关系，将平衡热力学的几何结构扩展到非平衡稳态，并揭示了具有度规和辛扇形的响应几何。在平衡状态下，反对称扇形因互反作用消失，恢复了热力学响应熟悉的度量几何形状。开放量子系统承认一种更广泛的结构，其中互惠和非互惠响应共存于同一控制管汇上。我们用纯去相下的驱动消散量子位来说明这一点，其中有限弯曲来自汉密尔顿本征基和环境选择的指针基之间的失调，而不需要强驱动或工程库。与布雷斯度量的比较表明，响应几何和信息几何描述了稳态管的不同性质：前者控制敏感性和几何功，后者量化状态互换性。因此，几何功成为开放量子系统中非互惠响应的可测量特征。


### Abstract

We develop a response-geometric framework for open quantum systems by decomposing the stationary-state response tensor into symmetric and antisymmetric sectors. The symmetric sector defines a metric-like response tensor governing local susceptibility, while the antisymmetric sector defines a curvature two-form associated with nonreciprocal response and geometric work. We show that the work curvature is precisely the antisymmetric component of the response tensor, establishing a fluctuation--response relation that extends the geometric structure of equilibrium thermodynamics to nonequilibrium steady states, and reveals a response geometry with both metric and symplectic sectors. In equilibrium, the antisymmetric sector vanishes by reciprocity, recovering the familiar metric geometry of thermodynamic response. Open quantum systems admit a broader structure in which reciprocal and nonreciprocal responses coexist on the same control manifold. We illustrate this with a driven dissipative qubit under pure dephasing, where finite curvature emerges from the misalignment between the Hamiltonian eigenbasis and the pointer basis selected by the environment, without requiring strong driving or engineered reservoirs. Comparison with the Bures metric shows that response geometry and information geometry characterize distinct properties of the stationary-state manifold: the former governs susceptibility and geometric work, the latter quantifies state distinguishability. Geometric work thus emerges as a measurable signature of nonreciprocal response in open quantum systems.


---


## 多维光谱的刘维几何：开放量子系统中的路径输运和观测全息

**Original Title:** Liouvillian Geometry of Multidimensional Spectra: Pathway Transport and Observational Holonomy in Open Quantum Systems

**Authors:** Eric R. Bittner, Carlos Silva-Acuña, Hao Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22530v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22530v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

刘维尔路径为解释多维光谱学提供了概念基础，但通常被视为在光学相互作用之间独立进化的固定对象。在开放量子系统中，这张照片是不完整的。在每个自由进化间隔内，环境相互作用不断地在路径之间重新分配幅度，产生传输，在非线性光谱响应中留下可测量的特征。我们开发了一个几何框架，其中路径传输由刘维联系、其相关的弯曲以及由此产生的观测完整性来控制。该框架适用于开放量子系统，其中环境选择与用于构建光谱响应的观测基不同的指针基。这种基础不相容性会导致刘维尔路径之间的传输，产生特征性的光谱失真和不平凡的刘维尔弯曲。使用刘维传播子的杜哈梅尔展开，我们推导出一个重建过程，该过程识别负责观察到的路径权重重新分配的传输运营商，在整个基本失准范围内准确。这种观点重新构建了光谱特征，不仅取决于存在哪些路径，还取决于幅度在路径之间传输的方式。光谱失真、峰移和原本禁止的路径贡献成为弯曲刘维尔空间多管的几何特征，而不是现象学拓宽修正，从而将路径几何识别为非线性光谱学中的补充组织层。


### Abstract

Liouville pathways provide the conceptual foundation for interpreting multidimensional spectroscopies, yet are typically treated as fixed objects that evolve independently between optical interactions. In open quantum systems, this picture is incomplete. Environmental interactions continuously redistribute amplitude among pathways during every free-evolution interval, generating transport that leaves measurable signatures in the nonlinear spectroscopic response. We develop a geometric framework in which pathway transport is governed by a Liouvillian connection, its associated curvature, and the resulting observational holonomy. The framework applies to open quantum systems in which the environment selects a pointer basis distinct from the observational basis used to construct the spectroscopic response. This basis incompatibility induces transport among Liouville pathways, generating characteristic spectral distortions and a nontrivial Liouvillian curvature. Using a Duhamel expansion of the Liouvillian propagator, we derive a reconstruction procedure that identifies the transport operators responsible for the observed redistribution of pathway weight, accurate throughout the full range of basis misalignment. This perspective reframes spectral features as determined not only by which pathways exist but by how amplitude is transported among them. Spectral distortions, peak shifts, and otherwise-forbidden pathway contributions become geometric signatures of a curved Liouville-space manifold rather than phenomenological broadening corrections, identifying pathway geometry as a complementary layer of organization in nonlinear spectroscopy.


---


## 任意局部维的量子海明界

**Original Title:** The Quantum Hamming Bound in Arbitrary Local Dimension

**Authors:** Yu-Xuan Zhang, Jing-Ling Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22538v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22538v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

量子海明界是精确量子错误纠正的有限长度球体填充计数：代码维度乘以可纠正的局部错误模式的数量必须适合环境希尔伯特空间。对于非退化码，这源于不相交的错误范围。简并是唯一的障碍，因为明显的物理错误可能会在代码子空间上重合，并将球体填充变成超额计数。有限长度的核心问题是，这种超额计算是否会使海明不等式无效。早期的线性规划、渐进和结构性结果为任意精确子空间码留下了逐点有限长问题。将$Q= q#2 $写入海明方案字母表，非二进制范围从$Q=9$开始;在这里我们证明了每个$q\ge3$的界限，而二进制端点由一个不同的$Q=4$充电几何结构决定。对于该范围内的每个非平凡精确子空间码，任何可能的违规都简化为由劳埃德响应规范化的两中心Hamming-ball交集不等式。对于$q\ge4$，平方线性规划在简化为字母表$Q\ge16$和临界长度$n= 4 t +1$后具有均匀的半间隙。Qutrits形成边界：半间隙消失了，但桥由二次过滤劳埃德平方、精确的系数证书简化和斯坦切正性论点处理。因此，简并可能合并错误部门，但不足以击败海明计数。这证明了有限长度量子海明界的非二元部分;与独立二元端点定理一起，给出了任意局部维度的结果。


### Abstract

The quantum Hamming bound is the finite-length sphere-packing count for exact quantum error correction: the code dimension times the number of correctable local error patterns must fit inside the ambient Hilbert space. For nondegenerate codes this follows from disjoint error spheres. Degeneracy is the only obstruction, because distinct physical errors can coincide on the code subspace and turn sphere packing into an overcount. The central finite-length question has been whether this overcount can ever invalidate the Hamming inequality. Earlier linear-programming, asymptotic, and structural results left a pointwise finite-length problem for arbitrary exact subspace codes. Writing $Q=q^2$ for the Hamming-scheme alphabet, the nonbinary range begins at $Q=9$; here we prove the bound for every $q\ge3$, while the binary endpoint is governed by a distinct $Q=4$ charging geometry. For every nontrivial exact subspace code in this range, any possible violation reduces to a two-center Hamming-ball intersection inequality normalized by the Lloyd response. For $q\ge4$, the Lloyd-square linear program has a uniform half-gap after reduction to alphabet $Q\ge16$ and critical length $n=4t+1$. Qutrits form the boundary: the half-gap disappears, but the bridge is handled by a quadratic-filtered Lloyd square, an exact coefficient-certificate reduction, and a Stein-tangent positivity argument. Thus degeneracy may merge error sectors, but not enough to beat the Hamming count. This proves the nonbinary part of the finite-length quantum Hamming bound; together with the independent binary endpoint theorem, it gives the result in arbitrary local dimension.


---


## 带有穿梭巴士的旋转表面代码上的分层逻辑处理器

**Original Title:** Hierarchical Logical Processor on the Rotated Surface Code with Shuttle Buses

**Authors:** Zi-Han Chen, Ming-Cheng Chen, Chao-Yang Lu, Jian-Wei Pan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22594v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22594v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

具有超平面连接性的量子平台为容忍量子计算（FTQC）提供了新的机会。虽然量子低密度Parity-check（qDLC）码提供了高编码效率，但它们的直接实现需要在每一轮伴随式提取中进行非本地耦合，从而导致额外的物理错误和实现复杂性。为了减少此类耦合的频率，我们提出了分层逻辑处理器（HLP），它将高速率量子CSS代码与旋转表面代码（RSC）级联。HLP可以实现超RSC编码效率，同时每$0级错误纠正$0（d_0）$轮仅需要一次远程连接性，其中$d_0$表示基码距离，相对于qDLC码的直接实现，大大降低了非本地耦合的频率。HLPs引入了称为班车的细长RSC补丁。使用横向混合单元C诺特门，单个班车可以同时连接到多个标准RSC补丁。该功能可以实现高效的1级综合症提取，抑制1级错误相关性，并支持高度并行的逻辑泡利测量。我们对几个具体的HLP结构进行电路级模拟，并对逻辑存储器和逻辑泡利测量性能进行基准测试。物理错误率为$10 ''' s时，基于[[256，194，4]]码的HLP实现了比标准RSC高3-4倍的量子位效率。与同一级代码上的负磁表面代码相比，该HLP将每个逻辑量子位的空间负担减少了100-200个物理量子位，并将逻辑错误纠正周期时间缩短了20-30倍。


### Abstract

Quantum platforms with beyond-planar connectivity provide new opportunities for fault-tolerant quantum computation (FTQC). While quantum low-density parity-check (qLDPC) codes offer high encoding efficiency, their direct implementation requires non-local couplings in every round of syndrome extraction, incurring additional physical error and implementation complexity. To reduce the frequency of such couplings, we propose the Hierarchical Logical Processor (HLP), which concatenates a high-rate quantum CSS code with the rotated surface code (RSC). HLPs can achieve beyond-RSC encoding efficiency while requiring long-range connectivity only once every $Θ(d_0)$ rounds of level-0 error correction, where $d_0$ denotes the base-code distance, substantially reducing the frequency of non-local couplings relative to direct implementations of qLDPC codes. HLPs introduce elongated RSC patches called shuttle buses. Using transversal hybrid-unit CNOT gates, a single shuttle bus can simultaneously couple to multiple standard RSC patches. This capability enables efficient level-1 syndrome extraction with suppressed level-1 error correlations and supports highly parallel logical Pauli measurements. We perform circuit-level simulations of several concrete HLP constructions and benchmark both logical memory and logical Pauli measurement performance. At a physical error rate of $10^{-3}$, an HLP based on the [[256,194,4]] code achieves 3-4 times higher qubit efficiency than the standard RSC. Compared with the yoked surface code on the same level-1 code, this HLP reduces the space overhead per logical qubit by 100-200 physical qubits and shortens the logical error-correction cycle time by a factor of 20-30.


---


## 逼近全息码中状态相关原区域的非线性几何化

**Original Title:** Nonlinear Geometrizability of State-Dependent Proto-Area in Approximate Holographic Codes

**Authors:** Ruiliang Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22598v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22598v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

通过大约恢复产生的依赖于州的原型区域数据不需要与单一的本地批量指标兼容。使用在代码通道上校准并沿着逻辑状态族保持固定的恢复地图，我们推导出精确的有限分辨率准则，以及在双曲盘附近，规则原型区域双喷射从时间反射对称AdS$_3$切片上的度量双喷射产生的必要和充分条件。有限网络给出了一个具有原始和二元证书、稳定重建和非几何的显式见证的多边形实现问题。在连续体中，几何切空间是二阶测地X射线变换的范围。度量强迫的Jacobi方程确定重正化边界长度图像的正常海森，并产生规范不变的二次障碍。在分裂规律性假设下，附近的几何数据形成局部图;双喷射标准本身对于规则数据是无条件的。汉密尔顿偏码既实现了一阶非几何，又实现了第一个障碍仅出现在二次阶的响应。相容度量扰动是模定界自同胚重建的。


### Abstract

State-dependent proto-area data produced by approximate recovery need not be compatible with a single local bulk metric. Using recovery maps calibrated on the code channel and held fixed along a logical-state family, we derive exact finite-resolution criteria and, near the hyperbolic disk, necessary and sufficient conditions for a regular proto-area two-jet to arise from a metric two-jet on a time-reflection-symmetric asymptotically AdS$_3$ slice. Finite networks give a polyhedral realization problem with primal and dual certificates, stable reconstruction, and explicit witnesses of nongeometry. In the continuum, the geometric tangent space is the range of the rank-two geodesic X-ray transform. A metric-forced Jacobi equation determines the normal Hessian of the renormalized boundary-length image and yields a gauge-invariant quadratic obstruction. Under a split-regularity hypothesis, nearby geometric data form a local graph; the two-jet criterion itself is unconditional for regular data. Hamiltonian-skewed codes realize both first-order nongeometry and a response whose first obstruction appears only at quadratic order. The compatible metric perturbation is reconstructed modulo boundary-fixing diffeomorphisms.

## 无胎次猫州的可交配性的推广

**Original Title:** Generalization of catability for parity-less cat states

**Authors:** Michal Matulík, Jan Provazník, Petr Marek, Šimon Bräuer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22641v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22641v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

我们将基于取消者的可猫性认证框架从平价定义的一致猫状态扩展到无平价的克尔猫状态。由于克尔猫不能仅通过宇称来区分，因此我们用取代宇称运算符来替换原始抵消器的宇称成分，该运算符捕获了它们的特征干扰结构。由此产生的广义分解能力仍然可以直接观察到，并且可以根据有限数量的子数测量来评估，而无需全状态断层扫描。数字基准测试表明，该方法忠实地认证了Kerr-cat特征，产生了理想Kerr cat状态的准确逼近，并且比基于一致性的认证对光学损失的弹性更强。我们还确定了一个基于复共的精确反线性抵消器，为克尔猫状态提供了理想的代数描述。我们的结果拓宽了可催化性的范围，并为克尔猫状态的描述提供了一种实验实用的方法。


### Abstract

We extend the nullifier-based certification framework of catability from parity-defined coherent cat states to parity-less Kerr cat states. Since Kerr cats cannot be distinguished by parity alone, we replace the parity component of the original nullifier with a displaced-parity operator that captures their characteristic interference structure. The resulting generalized catability remains directly observable and can be evaluated from a finite number of photon-number measurements without full state tomography. Numerical benchmarks show that the method faithfully certifies Kerr-cat features, produces accurate approximations of ideal Kerr cat states, and is more resilient to optical loss than fidelity-based certification. We also identify an exact anti-linear nullifier based on complex conjugation, providing an ideal algebraic description of Kerr cat states. Our results broaden the scope of catability and provide an experimentally practical approach to the characterization of Kerr cat states.

## 用可逆纳米粒子指针进行连续自发定位的类测量测试

**Original Title:** A Measurement-Like Test of Continuous Spontaneous Localization with a Reversible Nanoparticle Pointer

**Authors:** Peter Renkel

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22707v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22707v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

We propose a measurement-like interferometric test of Continuous Spontaneous Localization (CSL), in which a trapped nanoparticle acts as a reversible mesoscopic pointer rather than as the initially prepared microscopic superposition. A microscopic two-branch system applies opposite weak forces to the nanoparticle, temporarily amplifying which-branch information into branch-conditioned pointer displacements. After one weak-trap period the pointer positions and momenta recombine, so ordinary quantum mechanics predicts recovery of the microscopic coherence, whereas CSL predicts an irreversible visibility loss accumulated while the pointer mass distributions were separated.   For a $10^{-18},{\rm kg}$ nanoparticle driven by a $10^{-21},{\rm N}$ differential force at $T=0.4,{\rm K}$, including thermal breathing and an ordinary loss budget $Λ_{\rm loss}\lesssim 0.1$, we find $λ_{\min}\simeq 1.4\times 10^{-10},{\rm s}^{-1}$ at $r_c=100,{\rm nm}$ with $10^5$ shots. A more aggressive lower-frequency point reaches $λ_{\min}\simeq 8.7\times 10^{-12},{\rm s}^{-1}$.   These sensitivities would improve over digitized direct matter-wave CSL bounds by about $7\times 10^3$ and $10^5$, respectively, while remaining above the strongest non-interferometric bounds. The proposal is therefore aimed at a substantially stronger direct visibility-loss test of CSL, and at a reversible measurement-like realization of collapse sensitivity, rather than at the strongest overall exclusion curve.


### Abstract

We propose a measurement-like interferometric test of Continuous Spontaneous Localization (CSL), in which a trapped nanoparticle acts as a reversible mesoscopic pointer rather than as the initially prepared microscopic superposition. A microscopic two-branch system applies opposite weak forces to the nanoparticle, temporarily amplifying which-branch information into branch-conditioned pointer displacements. After one weak-trap period the pointer positions and momenta recombine, so ordinary quantum mechanics predicts recovery of the microscopic coherence, whereas CSL predicts an irreversible visibility loss accumulated while the pointer mass distributions were separated.
  For a $10^{-18},{\rm kg}$ nanoparticle driven by a $10^{-21},{\rm N}$ differential force at $T=0.4,{\rm K}$, including thermal breathing and an ordinary loss budget $Λ_{\rm loss}\lesssim 0.1$, we find $λ_{\min}\simeq 1.4\times 10^{-10},{\rm s}^{-1}$ at $r_c=100,{\rm nm}$ with $10^5$ shots. A more aggressive lower-frequency point reaches $λ_{\min}\simeq 8.7\times 10^{-12},{\rm s}^{-1}$.
  These sensitivities would improve over digitized direct matter-wave CSL bounds by about $7\times 10^3$ and $10^5$, respectively, while remaining above the strongest non-interferometric bounds. The proposal is therefore aimed at a substantially stronger direct visibility-loss test of CSL, and at a reversible measurement-like realization of collapse sensitivity, rather than at the strongest overall exclusion curve.


---


## 含时两级系统的Lewis-Ermakov方法

**Original Title:** Lewis-Ermakov approach for the time-dependent two-level system

**Authors:** M. Huerta-Sandoval, I. Ramos-Prieto, H. M. Moya-Cessa

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22709v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22709v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

我们通过$su（2）$和$su（1，1）$代数利用它们与时相关的谐振子的代数对应关系，为时相关的两级系统构建了显式的Lewis-Ermakov型动力学不变量，这两个代数共享共同的复化$sl（2，\mathbb {C}）$。这个不变量为任意与时相关的耦合$a（t）$和失调$b（t）$提供了一个封闭形式的进化操作符和一个精确传播子。我们在代表性场景下说明了该方法，包括兰道-齐纳转变、非埃尔米特消散过程和隔热快速通过，并且当辅助标度函数被视为真实时，我们获得了具有完全显式控制场的隔热性的反向工程捷径。


### Abstract

We construct an explicit Lewis-Ermakov-type dynamical invariant for time-dependent two-level systems by exploiting their algebraic correspondence with the time-dependent harmonic oscillator through the $su(2)$ and $su(1,1)$ algebras, which share the common complexification $sl(2,\mathbb{C})$. This invariant provides a closed-form evolution operator and an exact propagator for arbitrary time-dependent coupling $a(t)$ and detuning $b(t)$. We illustrate the method on representative scenarios, including Landau-Zener transitions, non-Hermitian dissipative processes, and adiabatic rapid passage, and we obtain inverse-engineered shortcuts to adiabaticity with fully explicit control fields when the auxiliary scaling function is taken to be real.

## 由图神经网络引导的位串纠缠量的可解释封闭形式

**Original Title:** An interpretable closed form for entanglement entropy from bitstrings, guided by a graph neural network

**Authors:** Anas Saleh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22713v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22713v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

经验位串分布是里德伯格原子阵列上最容易观察到的分布，但它约束的二部冯诺伊曼熵的获得成本要高得多。我们提出了一个基于位串可推导物理量的六项线性闭合形式，并描述了其准确性、可移植性、缩放行为和校准成本。特征集是在经过训练的图神经网络的指导下选择的：探测网络将其熵预测本地化到双分区边界上的两点相关器，并进行仅限于这些边界相关器的详尽地面真相搜索来隔离形式。它达到了0.024美元$~nats平均分布绝对误差：6.4美元$倍网络误差，但采用人类无需再培训即可阅读和应用的形式。如果调整一次并不改变应用，它在六个分发外池中的五个上的误差低于基本网络，并与第六个持平。对一百个原子进行独立的密度矩阵重正化群研究--是精确对角化范围的五倍--解决了尺寸外推问题：冻结在小尺寸上的系数在规模上失败，但失败是结构性的。按尺寸改装该表格的价格为25美元-50美元~ mmat（交叉验证）;其六个斜坡中的两个遵循清晰的反尺寸定律，一个是向下弯曲生长，另一个是无趋势的;合适的定律部署了无标签的表格，价格约为40美元-80美元~ mmat。结果修复了标签预算规则：在大尺寸时，几十个标签重新校准封闭形式，以匹配相同特征上的微调分布集成，而非线性ML模型仅在给定大标签数据集时才领先。


### Abstract

The empirical bitstring distribution is the most accessible observable on Rydberg-atom arrays, but the bipartite von~Neumann entropy it constrains is far costlier to obtain. We present a six-term linear closed form for the entropy, built on bitstring-derivable physics scalars, and characterize its accuracy, portability, scaling behaviour, and calibration cost. The feature set is selected with guidance from a trained graph neural network: probing the network localizes its entropy prediction to the two-point correlators on the bipartition boundary, and an exhaustive ground-truth search restricted to those boundary correlators isolates the form. It reaches $0.024$~nats mean absolute error in distribution: $6.4$ times the network's error, but in a form a human can read and apply without retraining. Fit once and applied unchanged, it has lower error than the base network on five of six out-of-distribution pools and ties the sixth. An independent density-matrix renormalization-group study to one hundred atoms -- five times the reach of exact diagonalization -- settles the size-extrapolation question: coefficients frozen at small size fail at scale, but the failure is structured. Refit per size the form holds to $25$--$50$~mnat (cross-validated); two of its six slopes follow clean inverse-size laws, one a downward curving growth, and the others are trendless; the fitted laws deploy the form label-free at roughly $40$--$80$~mnat. The result fixes a label-budget rule: at large sizes, a few dozen labels recalibrate the closed form to match a fine-tuned in-distribution ensemble on the same features, while nonlinear ML models pull ahead only given large labelled datasets.


---


## 明亮压缩光驱动的高次谐振产生中高斯纠缠和非高斯纠缠的出现

**Original Title:** Emergence of Gaussian entanglement and non-Gaussianity in high-harmonic generation driven by bright squeezed light

**Authors:** J. Rivera-Dean, M. Even-Tzur, M. F. Ciappina, C. Granados, O. Cohen, P. Stammer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22714v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22714v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-21


### 摘要

高次谐振产生（HHG）是一种高度非线性的光学过程，其中来自强驱动场的辐射被上转换为其高次谐振。在原子系统中，这种非线性通过发射的谐振的强度与驱动场强度的比例来体现。尽管HHG具有高度非线性的性质，但当驱动场在经典高斯状态下制备并且原子耗尽保持可忽略不计时，产生的谐振的量子统计性质保留了经典高斯量子统计。用亮压缩真空（BSV）光驱动HHG挑战了这一范式，因为其增强的场波动可以修改所产生的和声的统计属性。在这项工作中，我们研究了BV驱动的HHG产生非经典高斯状态的条件，并确定了这种高斯描述崩溃的状态。对于频率为$ω$的强相干场和$2ω$的微扰BSV场的多色驱动，偶数调和响应在BSV积分中大致呈线性，从而导致非经典的多模式高斯纠缠在调和场中。我们表明，这种状态可以被描述为偶调和模上的分布式集体压缩模，并将其协方差矩阵、纠缠结构和量子隐形传输保真度描述为操作基准。我们的结果强调了非经典驱动的HHG作为工程设计极紫外区高斯和非高斯态光的平台的潜力。


### Abstract

High harmonic generation (HHG) is a highly nonlinear optical process in which radiation from a strong driving field is up-converted into its high-order harmonics. In atomic systems, this nonlinearity manifests itself through the intensity scaling of the emitted harmonics with the driving field strength. Despite the highly nonlinear nature of HHG, when the driving field is prepared in a classical Gaussian state and atomic depletion remains negligible, the quantum statistical properties of the generated harmonics retains classical Gaussian quantum statistics. Driving HHG with bright squeezed vacuum (BSV) light challenges this paradigm, as its enhanced field fluctuations can modify the statistical properties of the generated harmonics. In this work, we investigate the conditions under which BSV-driven HHG gives rise to non-classical Gaussian states, and identify the regimes where this Gaussian description breaks down. For bichromatic driving by a strong coherent field at frequency $ω$ and a perturbative BSV field at $2ω$, the even-harmonic response is approximately linear in the BSV quadrature, leading to non-classical multimode Gaussian entanglement in the harmonic field. We show that this state can be described as a distributed collective squeezed mode over the even-harmonic manifold, and characterize its covariance matrix, entanglement structure, and quantum teleportation fidelity as an operational benchmark. Our results highlight the potential of non-classically driven HHG as a platform for engineering Gaussian and non-Gaussian states of light in the extreme ultraviolet regime.


---


## 通过永久偶极保护量子位免受珀塞尔衰变的影响

**Original Title:** Protecting Qubits from Purcell Decay via Permanent Dipoles

**Authors:** Alex Krasnok

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22732v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22732v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

读出量子位通常需要将其耦合到共振器，但同一共振器也可以为量子位提供额外的衰变路径。在这里，我们研究了一种使用内置永久电偶极来减少这种损失的方法。对于量子位的基态和激发态，偶极将腔场向不同的方向移动。这种转变使相关波函数重叠得更少，从而削弱了横向量子位--导致珀塞尔衰变的腔交换。在简化的位移回旋波模型中，这种交换在$n =\SQRT{2}$处消失。在全横向模型中，这个精确的零点被解除，但在更大的偶极引起的位移处仍然存在强抑制。使用修饰的开放系统衰变率，我们找到了一个工作点，其中腔介导的衰变大大减少，而纵向读出信号保持有限。对于这里研究的基准，在固定指针间隔下，标准化寿命从$k T_1=11.1$增加到$47.3$，估计的单次读出误差从$0.21$下降到$0.07$。这些结果表明，永久电偶极可以提供一种内部的、通道选择性形式的珀塞尔保护。


### Abstract

Reading out a qubit often requires coupling it to a resonator, but that same resonator can also give the qubit an extra path to decay. Here, we study a way to reduce this loss using a built-in permanent electric dipole. The dipole shifts the cavity field in different directions for the qubit ground and excited states. This shift makes the relevant wave functions overlap less, which weakens the transverse qubit--cavity exchange that causes Purcell decay. In a simplified displaced rotating-wave model, this exchange vanishes at $η=\sqrt{2}$. In the full transverse model, this exact zero is lifted, but strong suppression remains at a larger dipole-induced displacement. Using dressed open-system decay rates, we find an operating point where the cavity-mediated decay is strongly reduced while the longitudinal readout signal remains finite. For the benchmark studied here, at fixed pointer separation, the normalized lifetime increases from $κT_1=11.1$ to $47.3$, and the estimated single-shot readout error drops from $0.21$ to $0.07$. These results show that permanent electric dipoles can provide an internal, channel-selective form of Purcell protection.


---


## 具有Rashba旋转轨道相互作用的单电子双量子点作为热力机的工作物质

**Original Title:** A single-electron double quantum dot with Rashba spin-orbit interaction as a working substance for heat machines

**Authors:** Ivan Romualdo de Oliveira, Vinícius N. A. Lula-Rocha, Moises Rojas

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22733v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22733v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

我们研究了量子奥托机的热力学性能，其工作物质是在外部磁场和拉什巴旋转轨道相互作用下限制在双量子点中的单个电子。汉密尔顿量由塞曼分裂、点间隧道幅度和拉什巴耦合控制，拉什巴耦合在局部轨道状态之间引发了旋转翻转隧道。在准静态奥托循环中，我们分析了与储层交换的热量、提取的功和效率作为汉密尔顿参数和储层温度的函数。我们表明，Rashba相互作用是在热力发动机、冰箱、加热器和加速器状态之间切换的有效控制参数。对Hamilton参数和储层温度的全球数值分析确定了热力发动机状态下效率和功输出的最佳操作点。最高的效率发生在探索的最大温度梯度附近并接近卡诺界，而最大的功输出出现在参数空间的不同区域。结果揭示了最大效率和最大提取功之间的明显权衡，该权衡由塞曼分裂、隧道幅度和拉什巴耦合引起的光谱变形决定。


### Abstract

We investigate the thermodynamic performance of a quantum Otto machine whose working substance is a single electron confined in a double quantum dot under an external magnetic field and Rashba spin-orbit interaction. The Hamiltonian is controlled by the Zeeman splitting, the interdot tunneling amplitude, and the Rashba coupling, which induces spin-flip tunneling between localized orbital states. Within a quasistatic Otto cycle, we analyze the heat exchanged with the reservoirs, the extracted work, and the efficiency as functions of the Hamiltonian parameters and reservoir temperatures. We show that the Rashba interaction acts as an effective control parameter for switching among heat-engine, refrigerator, heater, and accelerator regimes. A global numerical analysis over the Hamiltonian parameters and reservoir temperatures identifies the optimal operating points for efficiency and work output in the heat-engine regime. The highest efficiencies occur near the maximum temperature gradient explored and approach the Carnot bound, whereas the largest work output appears in a different region of parameter space. The results reveal a clear trade-off between maximum efficiency and maximum extracted work, governed by the spectral deformation induced by the Zeeman splitting, tunneling amplitude, and Rashba coupling.

## 广义量子隐形传送的全光实现

**Original Title:** All-optical Implementation of Generalized Quantum Teleportation

**Authors:** Takaya Hoshi, Akito Kawasaki, Xiruo Yan, Atsushi Sakaguchi, Takumi Suzuki, Tatsuki Sonoyama, Hironari Nagayoshi, Kosuke Fukui, Kan Takase, Warit Asavanant

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22736v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22736v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

基于测量的连续变量光学量子计算本质上提供高速、大规模操作，但其实际性能仍然受到经典电子前送电路施加的处理延迟和吞吐量瓶颈的限制。为了克服这些限制，我们提出了一种容损的全光前送（AFF）架构，用于广义量子隐形传态，能够执行任意线性操作。现实设备参数下的定量噪音分析表明，该架构成功地抑制了硬件引起的本底噪音，确认了其与容差量子计算要求的兼容性。通过消除光电子转换，该方案实现了连续的高吞吐量操作，从而大幅缩短了电路运行时间。最终，这种方法提供了一个抗噪平台，该平台将操作多功能性与光量子信息处理的固有速度和带宽相协调。


### Abstract

Measurement-based continuous-variable optical quantum computing inherently offers high-speed, large-scale operations, yet its practical performance remains constrained by the processing latencies and throughput bottlenecks imposed by classical electronic feedforward circuits. To overcome these limitations, we propose a loss-tolerant, all-optical feedforward (AOFF) architecture for generalized quantum teleportation capable of executing arbitrary linear operations. Quantitative noise analysis under realistic device parameters demonstrates that the architecture successfully suppresses hardware-induced noise floor, confirming its compatibility with fault-tolerant quantum computing requirements. By eliminating optoelectronic conversions, this scheme enables continuous high-throughput operations that drastically reduce circuit runtime. Ultimately, this approach delivers a noise-resilient platform that reconciles operational versatility with the intrinsic speed and bandwidth of optical quantum information processing.

## 来自非相干量子位泵的维格纳负磁振子稳态

**Original Title:** Wigner-Negative Magnon Steady States from Incoherent Qubit Pumping

**Authors:** Yan Liu, Jiahua Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22753v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22753v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

我们表明，非相关泵激量子位可以实现级联的消散机制来稳定维格纳负磁振子稳态。该机制将量子位抽运与分散磁振子数选择性相结合，以将稳态粒子数引导到选定的磁振子Fock状态。在单量子位的情况下，单马格子种群可以接近统一，并伴有强烈的反聚束和明显的维格纳负性。将相同的原理扩展到多个量子位，会产生由更高磁子Fock分量主导的维格纳负稳态。我们进一步推导出一个分析出生-死亡模型，该模型捕捉了该机制并与数值结果一致。这些结果确立了非连贯量子位抽运作为在混合量子系统中产生非经典磁振子状态的可控消耗资源。


### Abstract

We show that incoherently pumped qubits can realize a cascaded dissipative mechanism for stabilizing Wigner-negative magnon steady states. The mechanism combines qubit pumping with dispersive magnon-number selectivity to direct the steady-state population toward selected magnon Fock states. In the single-qubit case, the single-magnon population can approach unity, accompanied by strong antibunching and pronounced Wigner negativity. Extending the same principle to multiple qubits yields Wigner-negative steady states dominated by higher magnon Fock components. We further derive an analytical birth--death model that captures the mechanism and agrees with numerical results. These results establish incoherent qubit pumping as a controllable dissipative resource for generating nonclassical magnon states in hybrid quantum systems.

## 通过规范传播实现张量网络状态的等距化

**Original Title:** Isometrization of Tensor Network States via Gauge Propagation

**Authors:** Zhiyu Jiang, Hiroshi Ueda

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22816v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22816v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

我们引入了一种规范传播方法，用于将通用张量网络状态大约转换为具有指定垂直中心的等距张量网络状态形式。在一维中，这种传播是精确的，因为QR或奇异值分解产生的非等距因子支持在单个虚拟键上。然而，在更高维度的网络中，局部步骤可以有多个输出方向，并且剩余因子通常不能分离为独立的单边贡献。我们通过用由等距因子乘以输出分支因子的张量积组成的结构项来逼近局部张量或收缩局部集群来解决这个局部障碍。等距因子保留在当前站点或集群，而输出腿因子则被沿着传播方向吸收到邻近的张量中。这种结构为规范传播提供了局部截断标准，并提供了通过增加保留项数量或扩大局部集群来细化的实用途径。随机张量和Kitaev旋转液体的环气张量表示的基准表明，这种改进减少了局部残留和累积传播误差。对于环气张量，两个结构化项将局部剩余减少到数值精度，并将局部物体从2合2出扩大到4合2出和6合2出集群，降低了局部截断误差和有限蜂窝规范传播中的累积误差。这些结果将传播兼容的局部分解确定为近似等距化的有用构建块以及变分isoTNS算法的潜在初始化器或预条件器。


### Abstract

We introduce a gauge-propagation approach for approximately converting generic tensor-network states into an isometric tensor-network state form with a prescribed orthogonality center. In one dimension, this propagation is exact because the non-isometric factor produced by a QR or singular-value decomposition is supported on a single virtual bond. In higher-dimensional networks, however, a local step can have several outgoing directions, and the residual factor is generally not separable into independent single-bond contributions. We address this local obstruction by approximating a local tensor, or a contracted local cluster, by structured terms consisting of an isometric factor multiplied by a tensor product of output-leg factors. The isometric factor is retained at the current site or cluster, while the output-leg factors are absorbed into neighboring tensors along the propagation directions. This construction provides a local truncation criterion for gauge propagation and a practical route to refinement by increasing the number of retained terms or enlarging the local cluster. Benchmarks on random tensors and on the loop-gas tensor representation of the Kitaev spin liquid show that this refinement reduces both local residuals and accumulated propagation errors. For the loop-gas tensor, two structured terms reduce the local residual to numerical precision, and enlarging the local object from 2-in-2-out to 4-in-2-out and 6-in-2-out clusters lowers both local truncation errors and accumulated errors in finite honeycomb gauge propagation. These results identify propagation-compatible local decomposition as a useful building block for approximate isometrization and as a potential initializer or preconditioner for variational isoTNS algorithms.


---


## 旋转对称猫码的线性光学Bell状态测量

**Original Title:** Linear optical Bell state measurement for rotation-symmetric cat codes

**Authors:** Issa Oe, Suguru Endo, Rui Asaoka

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22832v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22832v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

旋转对称猫码（RS-cat）是一种用于量子信息处理的玻色子码平台，通过其离散旋转对称性将有限能量实现性与针对量子损失的鲁棒性结合在一起。对于远距离量子通信和基于融合的量子计算（FBQC）的应用来说，高效的贝尔状态测量（BSM）是一个关键的基础。在这项工作中，我们考虑了仅使用半分束器（HBS）和光数分辨探测器（PRDs）的RS-cat码的BSM协议。通过利用RS-cat码的离散旋转对称性引起的特征性光数结构，我们的协议提取光数模和相信息以进行Bell状态区分。我们表明，在理想的无损失条件下，对于足够大的幅度$a $，提出的BSM协议对于任意对称阶数$N$变得确定性。我们进一步从数字上评估了量子损失下的成功概率，并确定了更高级RS-cat码提供优势的损失机制。最后，我们表明后选择可以提高成功概率。


### Abstract

Rotation-symmetric cat (RS-cat) codes are a bosonic-code platform for quantum information processing, combining finite-energy realizability with robustness against photon loss through their discrete rotational symmetry. For applications in long-distance quantum communication and fusion-based quantum computation (FBQC), efficient Bell state measurement (BSM) is a key primitive. In this work, we consider a BSM protocol for RS-cat codes using only a half beam splitter (HBS) and photon-number-resolving detectors (PNRDs). By exploiting the characteristic photon-number structure induced by the discrete rotational symmetry of RS-cat codes, our protocol extracts both photon-number modulo and phase information for Bell-state discrimination. We show that, under ideal loss-free conditions, the proposed BSM protocol becomes deterministic for arbitrary symmetry order $N$ for sufficiently large amplitudes $α$. We further numerically evaluate the success probability under photon loss and identify the loss regime in which higher-order RS-cat codes provide an advantage. Finally, we show that post-selection can enhance the success probability.


---


## 当带错误学习问题遇到相干Ising机时：一种无惩罚的并行硬件协同设计

**Original Title:** When the Learning With Errors Problem Meets the Coherent Ising Machine: A Penalty-Free Algorithm-Hardware Co-Design

**Authors:** Shuxian Jiang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22843v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22843v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

带错误学习（LWE）问题构成了现代后量子密码学（PQC）的数学基础。LWE的密码分析范围从经典格约简到机器学习和量子经典混合。我们提出了CIM-BDD，这是一种混合有界距离解码求解器，通过严格\{无罚}映射将LWE简化为二次无约束二元优化（QUBO）问题。秘密的代数消除将LWE嵌入到$q$-ary网格中，吸收模算术并将问题重新铸造为最近向量问题（CVP）。然后，平方误差规范被用作\{直接}作为QUBO能量，因此加密噪音是要最小化的目标，而不是惩罚约束。为了在当前的有噪中间规模量子（NISQ）设备上实现这种通用模型，我们设计了一种特殊的编码方法：连续松弛Babai最近平面（CR-BNP）投影驱动自适应混合基数编码器，该编码器大大减少了量子位计数和QUBO系数范围，因此单批硬件提交即可。我们进一步推导出一个统计上有界的提前停止阈值（$T_{\text{early}}$），它充当单边证书，并兼作Decision-LWE触发器。我们在TU Darmstadt LWE挑战赛上验证了该框架，在Connorent Ising Machine CPQC-550上为搜索和决策LWE提供了一个价值40美元的维实例的端到端演示。这项工作为量子经典混合密码分析建立了一种新的算法-硬件协同设计范式。


### Abstract

The Learning With Errors (LWE) problem constitutes the mathematical foundation of modern Post-Quantum Cryptography (PQC). Cryptanalysis of LWE ranges from classical lattice reduction to machine learning and quantum-classical hybrids. We propose CIM-BDD, a hybrid Bounded-Distance-Decoding solver that reduces LWE to a Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) problem through a strictly \emph{penalty-free} mapping. An algebraic elimination of the secret embeds LWE into a $q$-ary lattice, absorbing the modular arithmetic and recasting the problem as a Closest Vector Problem (CVP). The squared error norm is then used \emph{directly} as the QUBO energy, so the cryptographic noise is the objective to be minimized rather than a penalized constraint. To realize this general model on current Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum (NISQ) devices, we design a special encoding method: a Continuous Relaxed Babai's Nearest Plane (CR-BNP) projection drives an adaptive mixed-radix encoder that greatly reduces both the qubit count and the QUBO coefficient range, so that a single batched hardware submission suffices. We further derive a statistically bounded early-stopping threshold ($T_{\text{early}}$) that acts as a one-sided certificate and doubles as a Decision-LWE distinguisher. We validate the framework on the TU Darmstadt LWE Challenge, giving an end-to-end demonstration for both Search- and Decision-LWE of a $40$-dimensional instance on the Coherent Ising Machine CPQC-550. This work establishes a new algorithm-hardware co-design paradigm for quantum-classical hybrid cryptanalysis.


---


## 兔子代码：通过先进控制工程拓宽超导量子误差纠正能力

**Original Title:** Bunny Codes: Broadening Superconducting Quantum Error Correction Capability through Advanced Control Engineering

**Authors:** Runshi Zhou, Xingye Yuan, Linghang Kong, Fang Zhang, Kai Zhang, Zhaohui Yang, Jianxin Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22853v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22853v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

利用在硬件层面解锁丰富的原生门集的超导量子位控制方案的进展，我们系统地研究如何利用这个扩大的物理两量子位门池（特别是C诺特和CXSWAP）来简化某些具有非本地稳定器的qDLC码的症状提取。通过详尽的搜索，我们发现了一组具有各种稳定器权重和距离的q低脂码，这些码可以在原生于高温硬件的二维最近邻量子位连接上实现，同时实现与需要远程交互的直接Cnot实现相当的性能。我们将这些代码称为兔子代码。在我们检查的所有代码距离中，在周期性边界条件下具有权重为6的稳定器的最佳兔子代码的代码速率约为复曲面代码的3美元倍;当转换为开放边界条件时，它们与旋转表面代码相比保留了大约2美元倍的代码速率优势。在电路级模拟中，我们发现一些兔子码的逻辑错误率比具有相当速率的复曲面码低一个数量级。我们的结果表明，使用扩展门集而不是远程耦合器可以实现高性能量子误差纠正，从而显着降低硬件复杂性。


### Abstract

Drawing on advances in superconducting qubit control schemes that unlock enriched native gate sets at the hardware level, we systematically examine how harnessing this enlarged physical two-qubit gate pool -- specifically CNOT and CXSWAP -- streamlines syndrome extraction for certain qLDPC codes with nonlocal stabilizers. Through an exhaustive search, we discover a set of qLDPC codes with various stabilizer weights and distances that can be implemented on the two-dimensional nearest-neighbor qubit connectivity native to superconducting hardware while achieving performance equivalent to that of the direct CNOT implementation requiring long-range interactions. We refer to those codes as Bunny codes. Across all code distances we examine, the best Bunny codes with weight-6 stabilizers in periodic boundary conditions have a code rate approximately $3\times$ that of the toric code; when converted to open boundary conditions, they retain an approximately $2\times$ code rate advantage over the rotated surface code. In circuit-level simulation, we find that some Bunny codes exhibit logical error rates an order of magnitude lower than toric codes with comparable code rates. Our results demonstrate that high-performance quantum error correction can be achieved using an expanded gate set rather than long-range couplers, thereby significantly reducing hardware complexity.


---


## 分子光机系统的混乱产生与控制

**Original Title:** Chaos Generation and Control with Molecular Optomechanical System

**Authors:** Hui-Hui Xu, Jian-zhuang Wu, Lei-Bo Deng, E Wu, Yong-Hong Ma

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22920v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22920v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

混乱是安全通信和物理随机数生成的核心。然而，传统的腔光机实现通常依赖于弱单量子光机耦合和低频机械模式，因此访问确定性混乱动力学通常需要大的驱动功率和仔细抑制热噪音。在这里，我们从理论上研究了通过将等离子体纳米腔耦合到耳语画廊模式（WGM）微腔而形成的混合分子光学机械系统。等离子体纳米腔提供太赫兹规模的单量子光学机械耦合到分子振动，而WGM共振器提供了低损耗的光通道，可以减轻较短的等离子体寿命。通过整合的半经典运动方程和评估的最大李雅普诺夫指数，我们映射的非线性动力学制度的WGM失谐，等离子体-WGM耦合，等离子体振动光机耦合的参数空间。我们发现，增加等离子体振动耦合驱动系统从自持振荡到混沌通过倍周期级联。在中等耦合强度下，通过调节WGM失谐量和腔间耦合，可以打开或关闭孤立的混沌窗口。这些结果确定分子光学力学作为一个可控的室温平台，片上混沌光产生和随机信号的应用。


### Abstract

Chaos is central to secure communication and physical random-number generation. Conventional cavity-optomechanical implementations, however, usually rely on weak single-photon optomechanical coupling and low-frequency mechanical modes, so access to deterministic chaotic dynamics often requires large driving power and careful suppression of thermal noise. Here we theoretically study a hybrid molecular optomechanical system formed by coupling a plasmonic nanocavity to a whispering-gallery-mode (WGM) microcavity. The plasmonic nanocavity provides terahertz-scale single-photon optomechanical coupling to a molecular vibration, while the WGM resonator offers a low-loss photonic channel that mitigates the short plasmon lifetime. By integrating the semiclassical equations of motion and evaluating the largest Lyapunov exponent, we map the nonlinear dynamical regimes in the parameter spaces of WGM detuning, plasmon--WGM coupling, and plasmon--vibration optomechanical coupling. We show that increasing the plasmon--vibration coupling drives the system from self-sustained oscillations to chaos through a period-doubling cascade. At moderate coupling strengths, isolated chaos windows can be opened or closed by tuning the WGM detuning and the inter-cavity coupling. These results identify molecular optomechanics as a controllable room-temperature platform for on-chip chaotic light generation and random-signal applications.


---


## BB 84量子密钥分发中用于自适应发射器丢弃的对抗强化学习

**Original Title:** Adversarial Reinforcement Learning for Adaptive Eavesdropping in BB84 Quantum Key Distribution

**Authors:** Ramon Jose C. Bagunu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.22962v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.22962v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

BB 84量子密钥分发的安全性源于任何窃听者以统计上可检测的方式扰乱通道的物理保证。之前的工作通过假设Eve以固定的、分析优化的速率攻击来评估这一点。我们研究了当Eve被建模为学习代理时会发生什么。经典强化学习，特别是表格Q-Learning、SARSA和Double Q-Learning，用于自适应BB 84窃听。这将攻击者的决策制定为马尔科夫决策过程，其中代理观察量子比特错误率（QBER）反馈并逐量子比特决定是拦截还是通过。实验跨越三个通道噪音水平（$μ_{ch}\in\{1，%，3，%，5\%\}$），并在五个独立的随机种子上进行验证（每个条件45次训练运行，每个10，000集）。相对于最佳非自适应分析基线，Q-Learning在$μ_{ch}=1\%$处将检测率从99.4美元减少到0.28美元\%$，同时每集提取约10.5个正确位。这是355倍的减少，具有统计学意义（$p=0.020$，Mann-Whitney $U$检验）。我们还报告了游戏结束爆发的自发出现，其中代理人独立学习在最后一个区块提高攻击率。该漏洞在随机检查点间隔内消失，而隐形性能在统计上仍然难以区分。这些结果促使在量子加密安全评估中纳入自适应对手基线。


### Abstract

BB84 quantum key distribution derives its security from a physical guarantee that any eavesdropper disturbs the channel in a statistically detectable way. Prior work evaluates this by assuming Eve attacks at a fixed, analytically optimized rate. We examine what happens when Eve is modeled instead as a learning agent. Classical reinforcement learning is used, specifically tabular Q-Learning, SARSA, and Double Q-Learning, to adaptive BB84 eavesdropping. This formulates the attacker's decision as a Markov Decision Process where the agent observes Quantum Bit Error Rate (QBER) feedback and decides, qubit by qubit, whether to intercept or pass. Experiments span three channel noise levels ($μ_{ch}\in\{1\%,3\%,5\%\}$) and are validated across five independent random seeds (45 training runs per condition, 10,000 episodes each). Against the best non-adaptive analytical baseline, Q-Learning reduces detection from $99.4\%$ to $0.28\%\pm0.27\%$ at $μ_{ch}=1\%$ while extracting approximately 10.5 correct bits per episode. This is a 355-fold reduction that is statistically significant ($p=0.020$, Mann-Whitney $U$ test). We also report the spontaneous emergence of an end-game burst, where agents independently learn to surge their attack rate at the final block. This exploit vanishes under randomized checkpoint intervals while stealth performance remains statistically indistinguishable. These results motivate the inclusion of adaptive adversary baselines in quantum cryptographic security evaluations.


---


## 与莱德伯原子进行卫星任务规划

**Original Title:** Satellite Mission Planning with Rydberg Atoms

**Authors:** Michel Nowak, Benjamin Marchand, Yassine Naghmouchi, Serge Rainjonneau, Wesley Coelho, Louis Vignoli, Louis-Paul Henry

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23045v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.23045v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

依赖冷原子的量子计算机正在被建造中，并承诺将信息编码到物理系统中的方式具有高度灵活性。特别是，模拟模式正在激发优化领域的兴趣，因为可以解决经典棘手的配置数量。在这项工作中，我们研究了一个需要每天安排涉及大量参与者的关键任务的问题。即，确定由几个暴露于高密度待扫描目标的单元组成的地球观测卫星舰队的规划。我们探索将公式化问题转化为冷原子友好设置的数字方案。我们首先对卫星任务规划问题进行了天真的表述，没有考虑卫星的敏捷性。然后我们根据文献扩展该问题以考虑它。通过将规划问题表述为最大独立集问题，我们能够使用基于里德伯原子的QPU来解决该问题。我们探索了在QPU上解决MIS问题的两种方法，一种依赖于图，另一种依赖于二次无约束二进制优化框架（QUBO）。我们表明QUBO方法是最相关的，并通过数值实验更深入地探索它。我们总结了使用QPU来解决运营背景下的卫星任务规划问题的潜在用途。


### Abstract

Quantum computers relying on cold atoms are being built and promise a high flexibility in the way information in encoded into the physical system. In particular, the analog mode is spiking interest in the field of optimization as a classically intractable number of configurations can be tackled. In this work, we investigate a problem that requires every-day scheduling of critical tasks involving a large number of actors. Namely, fixing the planning for a Earth Observation satellite fleet composed of several of units exposed to a high density of targets to be scanned. We explore numerical schemes that convert the formulated problem into a cold-atoms friendly setup. We begin by a naive formulation of the Satellite Mission Planning problem without taking account for the agility of the satellites. We then extend the problem to take it into account based on the literature. By formulating the planning problem as a Maximum Independent Set problem, we are able to solve the problem with a QPU based on Rydberg atoms. We explore two ways of solving the MIS problem on the QPU, one relying on the graphs and on the Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization Framework (QUBO). We show that the QUBO methodology is the most relevant and explore it more deeply with numerical experiments. We conclude on the potential utility of using a QPU to solve the Satellite Mission Planning problem in an operational context.


---


## 一类非最大量子访问结构上的高效完美秘密共享方案

**Original Title:** An Efficient and Perfect Secret Sharing Scheme on a Class of Non-Maximal Quantum Access Structure

**Authors:** Lei Li, Zhi Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23082v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.23082v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

量子秘密共享是量子通信领域的核心安全技术之一。针对当前非最大量子访问结构（QAS）下的量子秘密共享方案存在的量子资源消耗高、安全性与效率难以平衡的问题，重点研究了非最大量子访问结构（QAS）的判断标准以及一种非最大量子访问结构（QAS）上高效、完美的量子秘密共享方案的构建方法，即具有三个超半径的超级星。首先，我们对该非极大QAS中的禁止集和中间集进行了刻画，并对可通过纯状态编码实现的非极大QAS提供了刻画。其次，定义了具有三个超半径的超星的代表元素QAS，它作为该超星QAS的子结构，属于非极大QAS。此外，我们在这个超级明星QAS的基础上，并以相应的经典秘密共享方案为辅助，提出了一个通用、高效、完美的量子秘密共享方案。该方案通过将轻量级量子资源部署到代表性单元访问结构中，降低了量子状态准备和分发的难度，提高了其安全性和资源利用效率。


### Abstract

Quantum secret sharing is one of the core security technologies in the field of quantum communication. Aiming at the problems of high quantum resource consumption and the difficulty in balancing security and efficiency existing in current quantum secret sharing schemes under non-maximal quantum access structure(QAS), this paper focuses on the judgment criteria of non-maximal QAS and the construction methods of efficient and perfect quantum secret sharing schemes on a kind of non-maximal QAS, i.e. hyperstar with three hyperedges. Firstly, we characterizes the forbidden sets and intermediate sets within this non-maximal QAS, and provides a characterization for non-maximal QAS realizable by pure-state encoding. Secondly, the representative element QAS of hyperstar with three hyperedges is defined, which serves as a substructure of this hyperstar QAS, and belongs to non-maximal QAS. Furthermore, we propose a universal, efficient, and perfect quantum secret sharing scheme based on this hyperstar QAS using corresponding classical secret sharing scheme as an auxiliary. By deploying lightweight quantum resources to representative element access structures, the proposed scheme reduces the difficulty in quantum state preparation and distribution, and enhances its security and resource utilization efficiency.

## 通过维格纳相空间理解光的压缩状态

**Original Title:** Understanding Squeezed States of Light Through Wigner's Phase-Space

**Authors:** Sibel Baskal, Marilyn E. Noz

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23102v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.23102v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

本文首先介绍了从经典物理学到量子力学的过渡，相空间概念极大地帮助了量子力学。讨论了经典变换在量子力学中的作用。然后定义维格纳相空间分布函数，该函数源自密度矩阵的公式，随后是相空间中的谐振子。在相空间图片中讨论了光的相干、单模和双模压缩态以及压缩真空。人们还注意到这样一个事实：压缩状态自然地产生两个模式之间的纠缠。还结合维格纳相空间阐述了耦合谐振子。值得注意的是，量子力学的相空间图景已成为快速扩张的量子光学领域的重要科学语言。在这里，我们主要关注维格纳函数的最简单形式，它在量子力学的许多分支中都有应用。我们利用了几个对称群，例如洛伦兹群、二维和二维辛群以及欧几里得群。通过庞加莱球的重新公式来检查光场的退散问题，作为密度矩阵的进一步说明。


### Abstract

This paper starts with the transition from classical physics to quantum mechanics which was greatly aided by the concept of phase space. The role of canonical transformations in quantum mechanics is addressed. The Wigner phase-space distribution function is then defined which arises from the formulation of the density matrix, followed by the harmonic oscillator in phase space. Coherent and one- and two-mode squeezed states of light as well as the squeezed vacuum are discussed in the phase-space picture. Attention is also drawn to the fact that squeezed states naturally generate entanglement between the two-modes. Coupled harmonic oscillators are also elucidated in connection with the Wigner phase space. It will be noted that the phase-space picture of quantum mechanics has become an important scientific language for the rapidly expanding field of quantum optics. Here, we mainly focus on the simplest form of the Wigner function, which finds application in many branches of quantum mechanics. We make use of several symmetry groups such as Lorentz groups, the symplectic group in two and four dimensions, and the Euclidean group. The decoherence problem of an optical field is examined through a reformulation of the Poincaré sphere as a further illustration of the density matrix.

## S=1双线性双二次链Haldane相的角时演变和边旋转动力学

**Original Title:** Angular-time evolution and edge-spin dynamics in the Haldane phase of the S=1 bilinear-biquadratic chain

**Authors:** Takuma Kaise, Kouichi Okunishi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.23117v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.23117v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-22


### 摘要

我们研究了S=1双线性双二次链在上边缘旋转的开放边界条件下的二分区态的角时间演变--由纠缠Hamilton量产生的参数时间演变。使用接地状态波函数的矩阵积状态表示，我们计算了Haldane相中的角-时间旋转相关函数$\langle S_n^{a}（T）S_{n '\rangle$，并提取其主要振荡模式，该模式归因于与$\mathbb {Z}_2 \times \mathbb {Z}_2$对称性相关的近两倍简并纠缠谱。我们还计算了系统部分施加均匀磁场下的有效边旋转动力学，并通过精确比较其幅度的子系统大小依赖性来数值验证其与主要角时间模式的对应性。


### Abstract

We investigate the angular-time evolution -- a parameter-time evolution generated by the entanglement Hamiltonian -- for the bipartitioned ground state of the S=1 bilinear-biquadratic chain under the open boundary condition with the up edge spin. Using a matrix-product-state representation of the ground-state wavefunction, we calculate the angular-time spin correlation functions $\langle S_n^{α}(τ)S_{n'}^{α}(0)\rangle$ in the Haldane phase, and extract its dominant oscillation mode attributed to the nearly two-fold-degenerate entanglement spectrum associated with the $\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. We also compute the effective edge-spin dynamics under a uniform magnetic field applied to the system part and numerically verify its correspondence to the dominant angular-time mode by precisely comparing the subsystem-size dependence of their amplitudes.
